# PROGRESS-HISTORY.md — KhundiConnect full build history (archive)

> This is the append-only long-form record split out of PROGRESS.md. Newest archived entries first. The live SHORT tracker is PROGRESS.md. Do not delete entries here — this is the state-recovery record.

---

- **Build-step 85 — Brand / logo deployment** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode). First step after v3.1 (54–84).** branch `feat/85-brand-logo-deploy-v31` (off the staging head after 84); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (replaces the single placeholder `icon.svg` with the real KhundiConnect brand everywhere — favicon/PWA/maskable/iOS/login/header/push). spec `specs/85-brand-logo-deploy-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/85-CODEREF.md`. **NO schema / RLS / auth / permission / module change — pure web client + public static assets.** Isolation gate ➖ (the assets are public-safe branding — a green-tile/white-K icon set + wordmark lockups; no tenant data path; the manifest/SW only ever carry branding, never member/auth data). Gates: typecheck (shared+api+web) ✅ / web lint (no warnings) ✅ / web build (44 routes, all icons emitted to static output) ✅ / i18n parity + web-coverage ✅ / `pwa-manifest.spec.ts` (6) ✅. Zero physical-direction Tailwind; RTL unaffected (login lockup is theme-toggled, not direction-toggled).

  **Problem (spec §1).** Every icon reference pointed at one generic `apps/web/public/icon.svg`, and the two brand surfaces rendered a letter-in-a-square (`APP_NAME.charAt(0)` on login; `name.charAt(0)` in the header) — unbranded. The operator pre-placed the approved brand set in `apps/web/public/`; this step WIRES those existing files (the agent generates no images). The KhundiConnect brand is the **DEFAULT** — the existing per-Khundi white-label flow (`logoUrl`, build-step 36/44) MUST still win when a Khundi uploaded its own logo.

  **Assets verified present (spec §2 / CODEREF):** `logo-full.svg`, `logo-full-inverse.svg`, `logo-mark.svg`, `logo-mark-white.svg`, `icon-default-192/512.png`, `icon-default-maskable-192/512.png`, `favicon.svg`, `favicon.ico`, `apple-touch-icon.png` — all confirmed before editing (no `[HUMAN_REQUIRED]` for missing assets).

  **Static-vs-dynamic manifest decision (spec §3.2 / CODEREF).** Build-step 83 already converted the manifest to a DYNAMIC per-subdomain route (`apps/web/app/manifest.webmanifest/route.ts`) that resolves the tenant via the public `/api/tenants/current` and emits via the pure `@kc/shared` `buildTenantManifest`, falling back to `DEFAULT_PWA_MANIFEST`. So I set the **DEFAULT/fallback `icons[]` in `@kc/shared` `DEFAULT_PWA_MANIFEST`** (NOT a static file — the static `public/manifest.webmanifest` was already deleted in 83) to the four PNGs: `icon-default-192/512.png` (`purpose:"any"`) + `icon-default-maskable-192/512.png` (`purpose:"maskable"`). A white-labeled Khundi with a `logoUrl` still overrides these via `buildTenantManifest` (unchanged) — KhundiConnect PNGs are the fallback only. `theme_color #157A3C` / `background_color #ffffff` kept. Rebuilt `@kc/shared` so the dist + web build + `pwa-manifest.spec.ts` pick up the new defaults.

  **Files wired:**
  - `apps/web/app/layout.tsx` — `icons` replaced `{ icon:'/icon.svg', apple:'/icon.svg' }` with `icon: [favicon.svg (svg+xml), favicon.ico (any)]`, `apple: [apple-touch-icon.png 180×180]`. `manifest`/`applicationName`/`appleWebApp`/`title` (APP_NAME)/`viewport.themeColor` kept.
  - `packages/shared/src/index.ts` — `DEFAULT_PWA_MANIFEST.icons` → the four `icon-default-*` PNGs (separate `any` + `maskable` so Android fills the adaptive-icon crop with no clipped corners). `buildTenantManifest` white-label branch untouched.
  - `apps/web/public/sw.js` — `CACHE 'kc-shell-v3'`→`'kc-shell-v4'` (REQUIRED: 83 had already set v3, so a fresh bump is needed to evict the cached `/icon.svg` and re-precache the real assets); `SHELL` `/icon.svg`→`/favicon.svg` + added `/icon-default-192.png`; push `icon`/`badge` `/icon.svg`→`/icon-default-192.png` (icon) + `/favicon.svg` (badge). `/api` no-cache exclusion + SWR/precache logic + `SKIP_WAITING` handler untouched (build-step 32/83). Header comment updated to note the 85 change.
  - `apps/web/app/login/page.tsx` — `brandHead` letter-square + visible `<h1>{APP_NAME}</h1>` replaced with TWO theme-toggled lockups (`logo-full.svg` `dark:hidden` + `logo-full-inverse.svg` `hidden dark:block` — Tailwind `dark:` class strategy, so the wordmark stays legible in both light and dark; login `Shell` bg is the page background + faint primary radial, not a solid green panel, and carries a `ThemeToggle`) both `alt="" aria-hidden`, with an `sr-only <h1>{APP_NAME}</h1>` supplying the accessible name. "Sign in with your OMJ Card Number" subtext kept.
  - `apps/web/app/ui/shell.tsx` — `BrandMark` letter-square replaced with theme-toggled marks (`logo-mark.svg` `dark:hidden` + `logo-mark-white.svg` `hidden dark:block`, `size-9`, `alt="" aria-hidden`). The tenant-name precedence (build-step 44 #1 — `useTenantName` resolves the Khundi's display name via `/api/tenants/current`, NOT the white-label brand) is unchanged — only the MARK swapped, never the name logic.
  - **Deleted** `apps/web/public/icon.svg` after `grep -rn "/icon.svg" apps/web` returned ZERO real references (remaining matches were `favicon.svg` substring hits + the SW comment that the placeholder is gone).

  **i18n.** No new `t()` keys — login alt is decorative (`aria-hidden`, accessible name via `sr-only` h1 using `APP_NAME`), header mark is decorative; `layout` `title` already `APP_NAME`. i18n parity + web-coverage stay green with zero deltas.

  **Acceptance (spec §4) met:** real favicon (svg + ico) + iOS apple-touch-icon; PWA install shows the green-tile/white-K with proper maskable PNGs; login shows the real lockup (Khundi `logoUrl` still wins on its subdomain); header shows the real mark with tenant-name precedence preserved; push uses the real icon; SW cache bumped (v4) so returning users evict the placeholder, `/api` still never cached; `icon.svg` removed and grep-clean.

  **Do-NOT-break upheld:** per-Khundi white-label `logoUrl` precedence (`buildTenantManifest` unchanged); header tenant-name precedence (build-step 44); SW `/api` no-cache (build-step 32); build-step-83 dynamic manifest (edited its DEFAULT branch, not reverted to a static file); `theme_color #157A3C`/`background_color` kept.

- **Build-step 84 — Reporting module** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode). CLOSES v3.1 (54–84).** branch `feat/84-reporting-module-v31` (off the staging head after 83); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (a registry-driven report LIBRARY + PDF/Excel on the build-step-13/31 reporting layer; Wave 6 / item 2 — final build-step). spec `specs/84-reporting-module-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/83-84-CODEREF.md`. tests **1638/1638** (199 suites; **+14** net, **+2 suites** — NEW `reports/report-render.spec.ts` (6: registry shape + altitude split; sensitive-permission/shareable assertions; HTML deck RTL/escaping/logical-CSS-only + `safeColor` rejection; `.xlsx` valid-ZIP + OOXML parts; RTL `rightToLeft` + numeric-cell + XML-escape; deterministic bytes) + `reports/report-library.access.spec.ts` (8: registry list/altitude isolation; sensitive report DENIED without source permission + domain service untouched; ALLOWED with permission + delegates; family-tree requires memberId; unknown/altitude-mismatch NotFound; export to real `.xlsx` + HTML deck)). **NO SCHEMA CHANGE** — reports READ existing data; `npx prisma validate` ✅ unchanged. typecheck (shared+api+web) / web lint (clean) / api+web build all green.

  **Problem (spec §1, C-reporting; ARCHITECTURE §13).** A 3-altitude dashboard + CSV layer existed (build-step 13/31) but there was no dedicated report LIBRARY (named, filtered reports) and exports were CSV-only. The decision: a registry-driven Reporting module with hybrid server-side **PDF + Excel**.

  **Design.**
    - **Report registry (pure `@kc/shared`, pattern = build-step-22 `LIST_COLUMN_REGISTRY`).** NEW `REPORT_REGISTRY` / `ReportDefinition` / `REPORT_DEFINITIONS` / `reportsForAltitude`. Each def = `{key, labelKey, descriptionKey, altitude, requiresPermission?, filterKey?, requiresMemberId?, shareable}`. Reports: **member-directory** (members.view, member-audience filter), **financial-statements** (accounting.view), **lawazim-defaulters** (lawazim.view), **welfare-summary** (welfare.view, aggregate→shareable), **census-report** (census.view, aggregate→shareable), **family-tree** (family.view, requiresMemberId), **khundi-dashboard** (reports.view) — Khundi altitude; **jamat-aggregate** — OMJ altitude. New reports are added here without touching the engine (acceptance #4).
    - **Portable document + two PURE renderers.** NEW `ReportDocument` (`{key,title,subtitle?,generatedAt,locale,stats?,sections[],branding?,note?}`; sections carry localized columns + rows). `renderReportHtml(doc)` = the **PDF face** — a self-contained, print-ready HTML deck (the build-step-68 browser-print approach: Urdu shaping + RTL correct; logical CSS only; branding via `safeColor`; colours kept on print). `renderReportXlsx(doc)` = the **Excel face** — a real `.xlsx` from a **hand-rolled, ZERO-DEPENDENCY OOXML writer**: a tiny STORED-entry ZIP + IEEE CRC-32 + SpreadsheetML emitter (one Summary sheet + one sheet per section; RTL via `<sheetView rightToLeft="1">`; numeric cells stay numeric so a recipient can sum them; bijective base-26 column letters; unique ≤31-char sheet names; deterministic fixed-date bytes).
    - **DEPENDENCY CHOICE (documented, acceptance #5): ZERO-DEP, no exceljs/SheetJS.** Same rationale as the build-step-68 PDF — ARM-safe (no native/binary npm install), deterministic, unit-testable in `@kc/shared` alongside the HTML renderer, and the gates stay clean. The OOXML output was VALIDATED as a real archive with `unzip -t` (all 6 parts OK) during development. (exceljs *is* pure-JS and installable on ARM — it was considered — but the zero-dep path is the stronger fit with the codebase's documented build-step-68 precedent.)
    - **API `ReportLibraryService` (NEW) — orchestrate + render, never recompute.** Injects the existing domain services (`MembersService`/`LawazimService`/`FundsService`/`WelfareService`/`CensusService`/`FamilyService` + the build-step-13 `ReportsService` dashboard) and reuses their public methods (`members.list`, `lawazim.getRegister`/`listYears`, `funds.listFunds`+`summarizeFunds`, `welfare.getFundReport`, `census.report`/`listInstances`, `family.getFamily`) — every figure comes from the module that owns it, so a report can never disagree with its source screen (acceptance #2). Each method runs through those services' own `runWithTenant`, so every report is RLS-isolated to the requesting Khundi (jamat-aggregate runs on the audited cross-Khundi path) (acceptance #3).
    - **Per-report permission gate.** `assertAllowed` checks `def.requiresPermission` via `PermissionService.hasPermission(userId, perm, OWN_TENANT, tenantId)` BEFORE the report runs and before any domain service is touched — a sensitive report is gated by the SAME permission as its source (welfare→`welfare.view`, finance→`accounting.view`, …). The controller still enforces `reports.view`. Only `shareable` (aggregate) reports are flagged for build-step-77 public linking.
    - **Localization.** Every title/section/column/stat/note is resolved server-side via `translate(locale, key)` and enum cells via `formatLabel(value,{domain,locale})` (gender/member_status/welfare_fund_source/age_group/education_level/income_band/need_ask/relation) — so the JSON preview AND the server-rendered PDF/Excel are all locale-correct with no raw enums; `?locale=en|ur` drives RTL.

  **API + Web.**
    - Endpoints on the existing controllers (no new controller): Khundi `GET /reports/library`, `/reports/library/:key`, `/reports/library/:key/export?format=pdf|excel` (`@RequireModule(REPORTS)` + `reports.view`@OWN_TENANT + the per-report gate); OMJ mirror on `JamatReportsController` (`crossKhundi.view`@ALL_TENANTS). Export streams via `@Res()` — Excel as an `attachment` `.xlsx` (`…spreadsheetml.sheet`), the PDF deck as inline `text/html` to print. The legacy dashboard/jamat/platform/graves CSV exports are UNCHANGED (do-not-break).
    - Web `/reports` deepened: the dashboard stays; NEW `ReportLibrary` component (`apps/web/app/reports/report-library.tsx`) lists the registry as cards → opens a filtered run (gender/status/voting for member-directory; a member-id field for family-tree) → shows a read-only `ReportDocument` preview (stats + per-section tables) → PDF/Excel buttons. NEW `openFileInNewTab(path)` helper in `lib/api.ts` (bearer-auth fetch → blob → `window.open`) so the print deck opens authenticated; Excel reuses `downloadFile`.

  **Gates (acceptance #5).** typecheck shared+api+web; web lint clean; api+web build; `npx prisma validate` (no schema change); full api jest **1638/1638** (199 suites). i18n: **99 new `t()` keys** (`report.*` titles/sections/columns/stats/notes + `reports.library*` web copy + `common.yes/no`) authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` + delta `i18n-deltas/reports.json`; `i18n.spec.ts` (parity) + `i18n-web-coverage.spec.ts` (every web `t()` resolves) green. Zero physical-direction Tailwind in new markup (logical `text-start`/`text-end` only); RTL correct in the HTML deck (`dir="rtl"`, logical CSS) and the `.xlsx` (`rightToLeft`); no raw enums (all via `formatLabel`).

  **Do-NOT-break upheld.** Build-step-13/31 dashboards + CSV exports kept verbatim (library added on top). Domain derivations reused, never forked (member/lawazim/accounting/funds/welfare/census/family-tree). Tenant isolation absolute (every report `runWithTenant` via the source service, or OMJ-altitude). Welfare report is AGGREGATE-by-fund only (no individual case detail) + gated by `welfare.view`; financial-individual data gated by `accounting.view`. PDF reuses the build-step-68 HTML-print renderer/fallback.

  **v3.1 COMPLETE (build-steps 54–84).** After this the controller advances to the missing spec **85** and stops with `[HUMAN_REQUIRED]` — the expected end-of-program signal. Next program: v4 cross-org CNIC welfare ledger (ARCHITECTURE §27.1), build-steps 85+.

- **Build-step 83 — Full PWA** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/83-pwa-full-v31` (off the staging head after 82); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (deepens the build-step-14/32/52 PWA base; Wave 6 / item 1). spec `specs/83-pwa-full-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/83-84-CODEREF.md`. tests **1624/1624** (197 suites; **+8** net, **+1 suite** — NEW `tenancy/pwa-manifest.spec.ts` (6: default fallback, display-name vs brand precedence, branded name/colors/logo, invalid-color fallback, icon-MIME inference, **branding-only/no-member-data**) + 2 in `auth/token.service.spec.ts` (90-day TTL constants + ~90-day session expiry)). **NO SCHEMA CHANGE** — `npx prisma validate` ✅ unchanged. typecheck (shared+api+web) / web lint / api+web build all green.

  **Problem (spec §1, C-pwa/N-pwa).** A working PWA base existed (precache shell + SWR, never caches `/api`, web push) but had gaps: no install banner, a single STATIC manifest for every Khundi, silent SW updates, no offline indicator, a too-short (30-day) session, and no realtime-ready seam. This step closes all six without opening any cross-tenant seam.

  **Changes.**
    - **90-day session (spec §2.5, flagged).** `apps/api/src/auth/token.service.ts`: `REFRESH_TTL_SECONDS` 30d → **90d** (one constant). Access token stays 15 min; silent refresh against the httpOnly `kc_refresh` cookie is unchanged. All security preserved — httpOnly + secure-in-live + parent-domain scoping (`refreshCookieDomain`), token still rotated + SHA-256-hashed at rest, reuse-detection + logout revocation untouched. Tests assert the TTL constants and that a started session's `refreshExpiresAt`/row `expiresAt` sit ~90 days out.
    - **Per-subdomain white-label manifest (spec §2.2).** NEW pure `@kc/shared` `buildTenantManifest({displayName, branding})` + `PwaManifest`/`PwaManifestIcon` types + `DEFAULT_PWA_MANIFEST` (mirrors the old static file). Field-by-field fallback to the default: `name/short_name` = white-label `brandName` else `displayName` else KhundiConnect; `theme_color` = branding `colors.primary` (validated hex) else default; `background_color` = `colors.secondary` else default; icon = branding `logoUrl` (already a STABLE public URL — build-step 36/46 — never a raw key) else `/icon.svg`. **BRANDING-ONLY by construction** — `PwaManifest` has no member field; a unit test asserts the exact key-set + no member-data substrings. NEW Next route handler `apps/web/app/manifest.webmanifest/route.ts` (`dynamic='force-dynamic'`, `application/manifest+json`, short cache) resolves the tenant for the host via the existing public, branding-only `/api/tenants/current` (forwards the Host header, sends NO cookies) → `buildTenantManifest`; any failure falls back to the default. **DELETED the static `apps/web/public/manifest.webmanifest`** so the route owns `/manifest.webmanifest` (the route's default branch IS the static fallback); the `<link rel="manifest">` already points there.
    - **Smart updates (spec §2.3).** `public/sw.js`: `CACHE` `kc-shell-v2` → **`kc-shell-v3`**; SHELL precache extended to key routes (`/me /login /members /polls /notifications` — route shells only, member data always live via `/api`); each entry `add().catch()` so install never fails wholesale; NEW `message` handler runs `skipWaiting()` ONLY on a `SKIP_WAITING` message. `sw-register.tsx` rewritten: on `updatefound`/`waiting`-with-controller it shows an "Update available — Reload" **toast** (build-step 57); tapping Reload posts `SKIP_WAITING`, and a `controllerchange` listener reloads once. NEVER force-reloads silently. Toast system gained an optional `action:{label,onClick}` (renders an inline button, self-dismisses).
    - **Offline UX (spec §2.4).** NEW `ui/offline-indicator.tsx` — a top, localized, direction-aware banner driven by `navigator.onLine` + online/offline events. SW still never caches `/api`; the build-step-32 census offline-queue replay is untouched.
    - **Install banner (spec §2.1).** NEW `ui/install-prompt.tsx` — captures `beforeinstallprompt`, shows a dismissible bottom banner on AUTHENTICATED pages only (gated on `useAuth().status`), dismissal remembered in **sessionStorage** (not localStorage of member data); shows the Khundi brand (public `/api/tenants/current` `brand`) else KhundiConnect. `appinstalled` clears it.
    - **Realtime-ready, NO socket (spec §2.6).** NEW `lib/refresh-source.ts` `useRefreshSource(loader,{enabled,intervalMs,deps})` + `REFRESH_EVENT` — a single seam owning load lifecycle, optional polling, and a shared window-event a future Socket.io feed would dispatch. Wired the **poll detail** live turnout to it (auto-poll every 15s while open + a manual "Refresh" button); Socket.io stays DEFERRED.
    - **`layout.tsx`:** mounts `<OfflineIndicator/>` + `<InstallPrompt/>` inside the providers; moved `<ServiceWorkerRegister/>` inside Toast+I18n so the update prompt is localized.

  **Gates (acceptance #7).** typecheck shared+api+web, web lint (clean), api+web build (manifest route builds as `ƒ /manifest.webmanifest`, no public-file conflict), `npx prisma validate` (no schema change), full api jest **1624/1624** (197 suites). i18n: **9 new `t()` keys** (`common.refresh` + `pwa.installTitle/installBody/install/notNow/updateTitle/updateBody/reload/offline`) authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` + delta `i18n-deltas/pwa-full.json`; `i18n.spec.ts` (parity) + `i18n-web-coverage.spec.ts` (every web `t()` resolves) green. Zero physical-direction Tailwind in new markup; no raw enums. **Isolation:** the dynamic manifest is BRANDING-ONLY (asserted — no member-data key/substring; route sends no cookies, reads only the public branding profile) and the SW NEVER caches `/api` (rule preserved + commented).

  **Do-NOT-break upheld.** `/api` no-cache rule kept; census offline-queue replay untouched; web push (build-step 52) untouched; refresh-cookie security (httpOnly/secure/parent-scope/revocation) preserved; best-effort SW register (plain-SPA fallback) kept; static manifest fallback = the route's default branch. **Socket.io / first-class realtime remains DEFERRED to v4.**

- **Build-step 82 — Scoped Committee Roles** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/82-committee-roles-v31` (off the staging head after 81); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (committee conventions + role-term support on the existing role engine; closes Wave 5 / item 7). spec `specs/82-committee-roles-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/76-82-CODEREF.md`. tests **1616/1616** (196 suites; **+4** net — all in `role-editor.service.spec.ts`: term set/expose-as-`expiresAt`/clear-on-update, unparseable-term-rejected, no-term→`expiresAt=null`, and a templates-are-tenant-assignable + adopt-as-role assertion). **NO SCHEMA CHANGE** — committees are modelled as scoped custom roles on the existing `Role`/`RolePermission`/`UserRole` engine; the term reuses the existing `Role.timeLimitedUntil` column. `npx prisma validate` ✅ unchanged. typecheck (shared+api+web) / web lint / api+web build all green.

  **Problem (spec §1, C-committee).** A Khundi has committees (Census / Prize / Welfare Committee, a chairman per committee). v3.1 deliberately does NOT build a first-class Committees entity (rosters, terms, a structured chairman office) — **that is DEFERRED to v4** (noted here per Do-NOT-break). Instead a committee is a **scoped custom role** on the rich role engine (arbitrary roles, altitudes, scopes, mode-ceiling, time-limited, IP-restricted already exist).

  **Design — pure convention + seed + UX, no new table.**
    - **Committee role templates (`@kc/shared`).** New `CommitteeRoleTemplate` interface + `COMMITTEE_ROLE_TEMPLATES` constant: four editable starting points — `census_committee` (census.view/enter/approve/finalize), `prize_committee` (prize.view/approve/assign), `welfare_committee` (welfare.view/create/approve/disburse), `committee_chairman` (mom.view/edit, reports.view, polls.view/manage — so a chairman can run elections + keep minutes + read reports). Each template's every permission key is drawn from `TENANT_ASSIGNABLE_PERMISSIONS`, so adopting a template can NEVER grant more than a Khundi could grant by hand (a spec asserts this + asserts none is in `NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS`). A template is a CONVENTION, never a new entity or a hidden privilege.
    - **Committee TERM = `Role.timeLimitedUntil`.** The role editor now reads/writes an optional term-end date. `CreateRoleDto`/`UpdateRoleDto` gain `timeLimitedUntil?: string | null` (`@IsDateString`, `null` allowed via `@ValidateIf` to clear). `PermissionService.parseTerm()` is the one shared rule: `undefined`=untouched, `null`/''=clear, ISO string=set (BadRequest on unparseable). `createRole`/`updateRole` persist it; `toSummary` exposes it as `RoleSummary.expiresAt` (ISO, `null`=permanent). The existing `getEffectiveAccess` ALREADY drops expired roles, so a past term-end means the role stops granting access — no new enforcement code, just exposure of the field through the editor.
    - **Chairman elections → build-step-81 polling.** No bespoke election flow: a chairman is a member holding the committee role (optionally plus the Chairman template, which carries `polls.manage`); chairman elections run as a build-step-81 poll whose candidate/voter eligibility is the committee's own audience. Documented in the shared interface doc-comment.

  **Web (role editor, build-step 43 surface — `apps/web/app/settings/sections/roles-section.tsx`).** The create-role modal gains a "Start from a committee template" block (new roles only) — one button per template that pre-fills the (localised) name + ticks its permission set, fully editable after. A "Term end (optional)" `<input type="date">` binds to `timeLimitedUntil` (ISO⇄date-input helpers; empty = no term). The role list card shows a term badge — `warning` "Term ends {date}" while active, `danger` "Term ended {date}" once past. Permissions still render as human labels (never raw keys); admin/config never hidden by mode (build-step 60 untouched).

  **Gates (acceptance #4).** typecheck shared+api+web, web lint (clean), api+web build, `npx prisma validate`, full api jest **1616/1616** (196 suites). i18n: **10 new `t()` keys** authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` (EN+UR) + delta `i18n-deltas/committee-roles.json`; `i18n.spec.ts` (en⇔ur parity) + `i18n-web-coverage.spec.ts` (every web `t()` resolves) green. Zero physical-direction Tailwind in the new markup; no raw enums on screen. Isolation is LIGHT per CODEREF (existing role engine — already covered by the build-step-43 tenant-isolation specs in `role-editor.service.spec.ts`, which still pass after the term field was threaded through the in-memory store).

  **Do-NOT-break upheld.** Permission engine scopes/altitudes/protected-roles untouched (templates only reference tenant-assignable keys, enforced by test; `NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS` unchanged); build-step-60 mode-not-gating-admin untouched; build-step-81 polling untouched (reused for elections). **First-class Committees entity remains DEFERRED to v4.**

  **File list.** shared: `packages/shared/src/index.ts` (`CommitteeRoleTemplate`+`COMMITTEE_ROLE_TEMPLATES`; `RoleSummary.expiresAt`), `packages/shared/src/messages-extra.ts` (+10 EN +10 UR), `packages/shared/i18n-deltas/committee-roles.json` (new). api: `permissions/role.dto.ts` (term on both DTOs), `permissions/permission.service.ts` (`parseTerm`, term in create/update, `timeLimitedUntil` selected + mapped to `expiresAt`), `permissions/access.controller.ts` (pass `timeLimitedUntil`), `permissions/role-editor.service.spec.ts` (store supports term; +4 tests). web: `apps/web/app/settings/sections/roles-section.tsx` (template picker, term input, term badge, helpers).

- **Build-step 80 — CSV Bulk Member Import** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/80-csv-import-v31` (off the staging head after 79); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE.** spec `specs/80-csv-import-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/76-82-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 5 / item 5.** tests **1582/1582** (193 suites; **+26** net — pure CSV helpers ×12: `parseCsv`/`serializeCsv` RFC-4180, sample template, header map, `parseImportBoolean`, error-report builder; import service ×9: preview validation/duplicate/intra-batch/suspended-guard/§17, commit create+encrypt/skip/update/flag-not-drop; import isolation ×5 on the real migration chain). **NO SCHEMA CHANGE** — the import reuses `members`; imported rows keep `provenance='manual'` (the `MemberProvenance` enum has only `omj_fetch`/`manual`, and adding a value was unnecessary for the spec). `npx prisma validate` ✅ unchanged.

  **Problem (spec §1, C-import).** Members were added one-by-one; a Khundi onboarding from a paper register / Excel needs BULK import with a labeled sample, server-side validation, and a clear flagged-errors report — no silent partial imports.

  **Design.** Two POST endpoints under `/members/import` (POST so the CSV body never lands in a URL/proxy log), both gated `members.create` @ OWN_TENANT (bulk creation IS a create action — **no new permission key**), under the same triple-gate as the rest of the members module (`JwtAuthGuard` → `ModuleEnablementGuard(MEMBERS)` → `PermissionGuard`):
    - `POST /members/import/preview` — DRY RUN: parse + validate every row, return per-row `new`/`duplicate`/`error` with reasons + a summary; **writes nothing**.
    - `POST /members/import/commit` — writes the valid rows in ONE `runWithTenant` transaction (atomic + RLS-scoped), audited, and returns explicit `imported`/`updated`/`skipped`/`failed` counts + per-row actions. **No silent partial import** — error rows are reported, never silently dropped; the result spells out exactly what happened.

  **Validation reuse (Do-NOT-break #1).** Each row is mapped (human header → field key, tolerant of case/spacing, also accepts the bare key) into a record and validated by constructing a real `CreateMemberDto` + running class-validator `validate()` — the SAME validators as `POST /members` (the build-step-58 shared CNIC/phone E.164 rules included). There is NO second validation path. The `@Normalize*` transforms (phone → E.164, OMJ card → canonical) run via `plainToInstance`, and the normalized forms are what get stored. `isOkhaiByBirth` is pre-coerced (`parseImportBoolean`: yes/no/true/false/1/0/haan/nahi) with a friendly message instead of the generic `@IsBoolean`. `status=suspended` is rejected (suspension is an OMJ-altitude power, §2.3 — never a bulk-import backdoor). Derived fields (voting-eligible / married-in / child) are simply absent from the column map, so they can never be imported (build-step 61).

  **Governed taxonomy (build-step 66).** `education`/`occupation`/`income_band` columns are resolved against the per-tenant option universe (`TaxonomyService.listDomain`, loaded once per import) — a value matching a known label/value (case/space-insensitive) is normalized to the canonical option label; an unknown value is flagged as a row error (enforced, not silently accepted). MembersModule now imports TaxonomyModule for this.

  **CNIC (build-step 48, §17).** A supplied CNIC is validated (shared `isValidCnic` via the DTO), then encrypted (`cnicEncrypted`) + tokenized (`cnicToken`) at write time. The plaintext CNIC is held only transiently on the internal prepared-row and is NEVER returned in the preview/commit result or written to a log (tested: `JSON.stringify(result)` contains neither the formatted nor the bare CNIC).

  **Dedupe (idempotency, §3.5 no silent overwrite).** Existing members are loaded once (id + cnicToken + omjCardNumber, this Khundi only) into lookup maps. A row matching by CNIC token (wins) or OMJ card is marked `duplicate`; the commit applies the explicit `onDuplicate` choice — `skip` (default, non-destructive) leaves the existing record untouched; `update` applies the row's fields. **Never a silent overwrite.** Intra-batch duplicates (the same CNIC/card twice in ONE file) flag the 2nd occurrence as an error. The within-Khundi `(tenant_id, cnic_token)` / `(tenant_id, omj_card_number)` partial-unique constraints DB-back the dedupe.

  **Tenant isolation (acceptance #4).** No new table → isolation is the members-table RLS exercised on the import's two real paths. The new `member-import.isolation.spec.ts` loads the FULL real migration chain on PGlite as a non-superuser app role and proves: (1) the dedupe lookup under Khundi A sees ONLY A's card/token rows — never B's identical card/token (cross-tenant equal tokens allowed; isolation absolute); (2) an import row can NEVER be written to another tenant (INSERT WITH CHECK → "row-level security"); (3) within one Khundi a true duplicate card is refused (DB-backed dedupe); (4) deny-by-default holds; the audited platform path is the only cross-Khundi reader.

  **Shared (pure).** Added to `@kc/shared`: RFC-4180 `parseCsv` (quoted fields, embedded commas/newlines, `""` escapes, BOM strip, CRLF normalize, trailing-blank drop) + `serializeCsv` (reuses the existing `csvCell` escaper); `MEMBER_IMPORT_COLUMNS` (the labeled column map — dotted paths like `contact.cell`/`address.line`) + `buildMemberImportSampleCsv`; `mapMemberImportHeaders`; `normalizeImportHeader`; `parseImportBoolean`; `buildImportErrorReportCsv` (original columns + an `Errors` column, error rows only); result types (`MemberImportPreviewResult`/`CommitResult`/`RowResult`/`Column`).

  **Infra.** `main.ts` switched to `NestExpressApplication` + `app.useBodyParser('json', { limit: '8mb' })` so the CSV-in-body upload is accepted (default was 100 kB). The importer additionally caps the CSV at ~6 MB (DTO `@MaxLength`) and 5000 rows (explicit 400). Server secrets are untouched.

  **Web.** Members page gained an **Import** tab (only when `members.create`) — `members-import.tsx`: download sample CSV (client-side from the shared helper), upload a file (read via `File.text()`), preview the per-row table (name + new/on-record/flagged badge + reasons), choose skip/update for duplicates, confirm "Import N valid rows", and download the flagged-rows report (built client-side from `buildImportErrorReportCsv`). Result summary shown via a `Notice`. Uses only semantic color tokens + logical CSS; RTL-safe; no raw enums on screen.

  **Gates.** shared build ✅; api typecheck ✅; web typecheck ✅; web lint ✅; api build (`nest build`) ✅; web build (`next build`) ✅; `prisma validate` ✅; full api jest **1582/1582** (193 suites) ✅ incl. i18n en⇔ur parity + web-coverage. **i18n:** 35 new `t()` keys in BOTH locales (members.tabImport + `mimport.*`) in `messages-extra.ts` (EN+UR) + delta `i18n-deltas/member-import.json`; shared rebuilt before api/web typecheck.

- **Build-step 79 — Access & Credentials (onboarding wizard)** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/79-access-credentials-v31` (off the staging head after 78); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (auth-sensitive — touches credentials; isolation light per CODEREF, §17 secret discipline REQUIRED + delivered). spec `specs/79-access-credentials-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/76-82-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 5 / item 4.** tests **1556/1556** (190 suites; **+24** net — crypto `generatePassword` ×4; `AuthService.changePassword`+`loginMethods`+§17 ×9; migration regression ×3; `provisionCredentials`+`OnboardingService`+shared handoff helpers ×8). **SCHEMA (additive, GLOBAL `users` — no RLS touched).**

  **Problem (spec §1, C-access).** The permission engine is rich but onboarding was clunky and OTP was treated as the default credential — yet many Khundis have no SMS provider, so OTP-only locks people out; and My-Access showed raw permission keys, not human capabilities. Decision (spec): **password is the PRIMARY credential** (auto-generated, shown once, delivered by a `wa.me` handoff that needs no provider); OTP becomes OPTIONAL, offered only where a provider exists; My-Access reads as human capabilities grouped by module.

  **Schema (migration `20260722000000_must_change_password`).** ONE ADDITIVE column `users.must_change_password BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false`. `users` is GLOBAL identity (no tenant_id / no RLS), so NO tenant table's isolation policy is touched; the DEFAULT false backfills every existing row to "no change required", preserving current login behaviour. Prisma field `User.mustChangePassword`. `npx prisma validate` ✅. Migration regression spec applies the real step-2 → step-3 → step-79 SQL on PGlite and asserts the column is NOT NULL / default false, `users` stays RLS-off while `tenants` stays RLS-on, and an insert omitting the column backfills to false.

  **Crypto + shared helpers.** NEW `generatePassword(length=12)` in `auth/crypto.util` — built on `crypto.randomInt` (uniform, no modulo bias), an UNAMBIGUOUS alphabet (no `0/O/1/l/I/5/S/2/Z/8/B`, no symbols so it survives `wa.me` URL-encoding + dictation), GUARANTEED ≥1 upper/lower/digit (placed at random positions via a `randomInt` Fisher–Yates shuffle), ≥10-char floor. NEW pure `@kc/shared` helpers: `buildWhatsappHandoffUrl(phone, text)` (digits-only phone, URL-encoded text, null for an unusable phone → caller falls back to manual copy) and `buildCredentialMessage({locale, khundiName, cardNumber, password})` (localized `onboarding.credentialMessage` template resolved via `resolveMessageTokens`, both locales added) + `OnboardingResultView`/`CredentialMessageInput` types.

  **Auth (`auth.service`/`auth.controller`/`auth.dto`).** `AuthUserProfile` + `toProfile` now carry `mustChangePassword` (populated everywhere via the guard's `profileById`). NEW `changePassword(userId, current, new)` — verifies the current password (when one is set), enforces ≥8 chars + differs-from-current, writes a fresh scrypt hash and clears the flag; never logs/returns plaintext (§17). NEW `loginMethods(tenantId|null)` → `{password:true, otp}` where otp = the tenant has an enabled SMS/WhatsApp channel config (with credentials / Generic REST) or the legacy bring-your-own config; null tenant → otp false. NEW routes: unauth `GET /auth/methods` (tenant resolved from host via injected `TenantContextService` — reveals only a tenant-level capability, anti-enumeration intact) and authed `POST /auth/change-password` (`ChangePasswordDto`).

  **Provisioning + onboarding.** NEW `PermissionService.provisionCredentials(tenantId, {omjCardNumber, roleIds}, actor)` — the single user-provisioning seam: validate the member by card (tenant-isolated), validate every roleId is one of this Khundi's TENANT-altitude roles, `user.upsert` (create-or-load) with the new hash + `mustChangePassword:true`, idempotently assign roles, return the plaintext ONCE (`ProvisionedCredentials`, also `locale`/`phone` for the handoff). Re-running regenerates the password (doubles as a reset). Audit logs user id + role count only — never the password. NEW **leaf** `OnboardingModule` (`apps/api/src/onboarding/`) imports PermissionsModule + NotificationsModule + AuthModule — there is NO cycle because nothing imports it (NotificationsModule already imports PermissionsModule, which is why the onboarding orchestration could NOT live in PermissionsModule). `OnboardingService.onboard` composes `provisionCredentials` → `buildCredentialMessage` (Khundi displayName + member locale) → `buildWhatsappHandoffUrl` + best-effort SMS, returns `OnboardingResultView` (temporaryPassword + waHandoffUrl ONCE, phoneOnFile, smsDelivered/smsSimulated, roles). `OnboardingController` `POST /onboarding` gated `roles.manage` @ OWN_TENANT (CORE — no module gate). NEW `NotificationsService.deliverCredentialSms(tenantId, phone, body)` — dispatches SMS directly via the existing `MessagingDispatcher` (like `testSend`) with **NO `Notification` row**, so the body (which carries the temp password) is never persisted; audits the FACT only (no body); best-effort (returns `delivered:false`, not throwing, when no SMS provider) so the wa.me handoff always completes.

  **§17 secret discipline (tested).** The plaintext flows in memory only — generated → hashed → returned ONCE in the onboarding/change responses; what is STORED is always a `scrypt$…` hash (asserted not to contain the plaintext, and `verifyPassword(plaintext, storedHash)` proves it round-trips); a spy over `Logger.prototype.log/warn` asserts neither the temp nor the new password ever appears in a log line; the SMS path never writes a row.

  **Web.** **My-Access** (`/access`): grants now GROUPED by module (`PERMISSION_BY_KEY[key].module`) and rendered as human capability text (`perm.*`) with plain scope labels — the raw key is gone. Extracted `apps/web/app/lib/perm-labels.tsx` (`humanizeModule` + `usePermLabel` + `useModuleLabel`) as the single source of truth and refactored the build-step-43 role editor onto it (removing its local copies). **Login** (`/login`): replaced the build-time-only `isOtpLoginAvailable()` with a runtime `GET /auth/methods` query (per-Khundi OTP gating; env flag stays as the fallback); on success, a member with `mustChangePassword` is routed to the forced change-password screen on the current host before the normal tenant routing resumes. NEW `/change-password` page (forced first-login + routine). NEW onboarding **wizard modal** (`settings/sections/onboard-wizard.tsx`) launched from Settings → Roles & Permissions ("Onboard a member"): pick member (MemberPicker) → tick roles → optional "send by SMS" → generate → a one-time credential panel (card + temp password with copy buttons, a "Send on WhatsApp" deep link or a "no phone, copy securely" notice, SMS-status + assigned-roles + first-login note, all under a "shown once" warning).

  **Acceptance (spec §4).** (1) creating a user auto-generates a password shown once + a wa.me handoff (no provider) + SMS where configured; plaintext never stored/returned twice; first login forces a change ✅; (2) OTP offered only where a provider exists, else hidden; anti-enumeration intact ✅; (3) My-Access reads as human capabilities grouped by module with plain scopes (no raw keys) ✅; (4) the wizard creates user + assigns roles + delivers credentials in one flow; audited ✅; (5) migration regression + permission gates + §17 secret test ✅.

  **Gates.** typecheck (shared+api+web) ✅ · lint (web, 0 warnings — caught + fixed a `module` variable-name rule in the My-Access grouping) ✅ · api build (`nest build`) + web build (`next build`, `/change-password` emitted) ✅ · `prisma validate` ✅ · `npm test -w apps/api` **1556/1556 / 190 suites** ✅ · i18n parity + web-coverage ✅ · §17 secret discipline tested ✅ · zero physical-direction CSS in new files ✅ · 40 new `t()` keys both locales (delta `access-onboarding.json` + `messages-extra.ts`).

  **Notes / decisions.** SMS credential delivery deliberately does NOT go through the notifications `send` pipeline (which persists `body`/`recipients` — would store the plaintext, a §17 violation); it dispatches directly with no row. The onboarding orchestration lives in its own leaf module specifically to depend on BOTH Permissions + Notifications without a dependency cycle. OTP delivery itself remains the build-step-11 stub (`OtpNotifierService`) — build-step 79 only gates the OFFER on a configured provider; wiring OTP to a tenant's provider stays future work. Committee-style scoped roles (build-step 82 substrate) already work through the existing role engine — the onboarding wizard simply makes assigning them comfortable. `mustChangePassword` is a flag only, never a secret.

- **Build-step 78 — Custom audience builder (saved audiences)** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/78-audience-builder-v31` (off the staging head after 77); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE.** spec `specs/78-audience-builder-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/76-82-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 5 / item 3.** tests **1532/1532** (187 suites; **+25** net — 3 NEW audience specs: shared pure-engine ×7, service ×7, isolation+migration ×8; + reworked notif-engine forward-compat test + 2 OMJ-broadcast saved-audience tests). **SCHEMA + ISOLATION (REQUIRED + delivered).**

  **Problem (spec §1, C-audience/N-audience).** Sending resolves an audience inline; there was no way to SAVE + REUSE a named segment ("voting members in Block A", "lapsed members 2026"). Decision: a custom audience builder over the SAME build-step-56 filter engine (one filter language; no second DSL), usable at Khundi AND OMJ altitude, resolved LIVE against the current roster (never a frozen list).

  **Schema (migration `20260721000000_saved_audience`).** ONE ADDITIVE table `saved_audiences` (TENANT DATA, RLS ENABLE+FORCE with the standard `app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()` policy + tenant FK cascade) — `tenant_id` **NULLABLE**: a null row is an OMJ-LEVEL cross-Khundi audience at OMJ altitude (build-step 49 pattern); a NULL tenant_id matches no `app_current_tenant_id()`, so a Khundi context can neither READ nor INSERT one (proven). Columns: `name, description?, definition JSONB (a build-step-56 FilterState — the FILTER only, never a member-id list), created_by, timestamps`. No enum added. Prisma model `SavedAudience` (+ Tenant back-relation `savedAudiences`). `npx prisma validate` ✅.

  **Shared engine (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** NEW `MEMBER_AUDIENCE_FILTER_CONFIG` = EXACTLY the build-step-56 member-roster filters (`gender`/`status`/`votingEligible`) — one filter language. NEW pure `resolveAudienceDefinition<T extends AudienceMemberFacts>(members, definition)` runs the shared `applyFilters` engine, then applies the **active-only default** (`isActiveForSelection`, build-step 61) UNLESS the definition explicitly sets a `status` filter (so a "lapsed members" re-engagement audience can include inactive). `votingEligible` resolves against the DERIVED build-step-61 fact, never a stored flag. NEW `audienceMemberFilterValue` (the `applyFilters` accessor), `audienceDefinitionSetsStatus`, `SavedAudienceView`. Extended `NotificationAudienceSelector` with `filters?: FilterState` (the inline definition the OMJ broadcast fans down). **Hardened** `filtersToQuery` to guard `typeof value === 'object'` before `'in' value` so an untrusted definition with a malformed (e.g. numeric) value is ignored, not a crash.

  **API.** NEW `apps/api/src/audiences/` module: `AudiencesService` OWNS the single roster-resolution path `resolveMemberIdsInTx(tx, definition)` (loads the roster bound to the RLS tx, derives `isVotingEligible`, runs `resolveAudienceDefinition`), plus CRUD at both altitudes (`listForTenant`/`createForTenant`/… via `runWithTenant`; `listOmj`/`createOmj`/`getOmjDefinition` via `runAsPlatform`, scoped `tenantId: null`), a live `preview`/`previewDefinition`, and a `sanitizeDefinition` that round-trips through the (de)serializers so only known typed filter fields are ever stored. `AudiencesController` (`/audiences`, gated by EXISTING `notifications.send` read / `notifications.config` author — NO new key/module, §9) + `AudiencesPlatformController` (`/platform/audiences`, gated by the EXISTING `announcements.broadcast` @ ALL_TENANTS). Wired into the build-step-76 engine: `collectCustomMemberIds` now resolves `sel.audienceId` (same-tenant saved audience, read in-tx → RLS-bound) AND `sel.filters` (inline) via `AudiencesService.resolveMemberIdsInTx`, unioned + deduped with `memberIds`/`roleIds`. The build-step-77 OMJ broadcast gains a `saved` audience type: `broadcast` reads the OMJ-level definition ONCE at OMJ altitude (`getOmjDefinition`) then `resolvePerTenantAudience` returns `{type:'custom', filters: definition}` so it resolves INSIDE each Khundi's own context (isolation absolute, broadcast-down; a Khundi with no match / no channel is a SKIP, never an abort). NotificationsModule + AnnouncementsModule import AudiencesModule (one-directional; no cycle).

  **Web.** NEW `/audiences` (Khundi builder: list + create/edit/delete modal with the `<FilterBar>` over `MEMBER_AUDIENCE_FILTER_CONFIG` + a live `POST /audiences/preview` head-count) and `/platform/audiences` (OMJ builder; no preview — a definition has no single roster at OMJ altitude, it resolves per Khundi at broadcast). Saved-audience pickers added to the send composer (`custom` audience → `audienceId`) and the OMJ broadcast composer (`saved` type → `audienceId`). Nav: `/audiences` (gated `notifications.send`) + `/platform/audiences` (gated `announcements.broadcast`), `Users` icon.

  **Acceptance (spec §4).** (1) build a filter + save → appears in both composers ✅; (2) resolving runs LIVE against the current roster (membership changes reflect) ✅ (service spec); (3) reuses the build-step-56 engine — one filter language ✅; (4) OMJ saves a cross-Khundi audience resolved per Khundi at send, isolation absolute ✅ (broadcast spec: read-once + fan-down + skip-not-abort); (5) migration regression + isolation + i18n green ✅.

  **Gates.** typecheck (shared+api+web) ✅ · lint (web, 0 warnings) ✅ · api build (`nest build`) + web build (`next build`, `/audiences` + `/platform/audiences` emitted) ✅ · `prisma validate` ✅ · `npm test -w apps/api` **1532/1532 / 187 suites** ✅ · i18n parity + web-coverage ✅ · isolation REQUIRED + delivered (`saved-audiences.isolation.spec.ts` on the REAL migration chain through 78 as a non-superuser role: additive, isolation holds, OMJ null-tenant rows invisible to a Khundi + WITH-CHECK refuses cross/OMJ INSERT, deny-by-default, platform sees all, cascade) ✅ · zero physical-direction CSS in new files ✅ · 41 new `t()` keys both locales (delta `audience-builder.json` + `messages-extra.ts`).

  **Notes / decisions.** Married-in was dropped from the filter set: `MaritalResidence` has no `married_in` value (it is relationship-derived, build-step 61, passed in by the mapper) — so the builder mirrors the build-step-56 roster filters exactly (gender/status/votingEligible) rather than ship a half-derived field. NO new permission key/module — saved audiences ride the existing notifications + broadcast keys (§9/§17 intact). The store holds the FILTER, not a member-id list, so resolution is always live.

- **Build-step 77 — Announcement landing pages + OMJ cross-Khundi** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/77-announcement-pages-v31` (off the staging head after 76); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE.** spec `specs/77-announcement-pages-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/76-82-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 5 / item 2.** tests **1507/1507** (184 suites; **+22** net — 3 NEW announcement specs: content-guard ×6, service ×7, isolation+migration ×9). **SCHEMA + ISOLATION (REQUIRED + delivered, incl. a PUBLIC-exposure path).**

  **Problem (spec §1, C-announce/N-announce).** Notifications are push/SMS/WhatsApp messages; the community also wants richer **landing pages** (title/body/media) reachable by a link, in two visibilities — **login-gated** (members only) and **public-shareable** (anyone with the link) — with URL shortening, plus an **OMJ-level cross-Khundi** broadcast (OMJ → all members / specific Khundis / by-gender / by-role).

  **Schema (migration `20260720000000_announcement_pages`).** ONE ADDITIVE table `announcement_pages` (TENANT DATA, RLS ENABLE+FORCE with the standard isolation policy + tenant FK cascade) — but `tenant_id` is **NULLABLE**: a null row is an OMJ-LEVEL page at OMJ altitude (build-step 49 pattern). Under the policy a NULL tenant_id matches no `app_current_tenant_id()`, so a Khundi context can neither READ nor INSERT an OMJ row (proven by tests); OMJ rows + the public path flow only through `runAsPlatform`. `slug` is **GLOBALLY** unique (the public path resolves by slug alone across every tenant+OMJ; the DB enforces it regardless of RLS visibility). Columns: `title, body, media JSONB?, visibility TEXT('login_gated'|'public'), slug UNIQUE, audience JSONB?, published, published_at, expires_at?, created_by, timestamps`. No enum added (TEXT discriminator, app-validated, like `funds.kind`). Prisma model `AnnouncementPage` (+ Tenant back-relation `announcementPages`). `npx prisma validate` ✅.

  **Shared.** `AnnouncementVisibility`/`ANNOUNCEMENT_VISIBILITIES`, `AnnouncementScope`, `AnnouncementPageView` (author/manager view incl. ids/audience/lifecycle + `shortPath`), `PublicAnnouncementView` (SANITIZED public contract — title/body/media/publishedAt only), slug helpers (`ANNOUNCEMENT_SLUG_ALPHABET`/`_LENGTH`, `isValidAnnouncementSlug`, `announcementShortPath`). **The privacy heart — the PUBLIC content guard:** `findRestrictedPublicContent({title,body,media})` + `isPublicContentSafe` (PURE, exported) deny (a) a CNIC anywhere in text (`\b\d{5}-?\d{7}-?\d\b`), (b) a restricted data-embed ref `{{domain:…}}`/`[[domain:…]]` for `member/welfare/cnic/financial/donation/account/confidential/…` (`RESTRICTED_EMBED_DOMAINS`), (c) a media key under a restricted storage category (`RESTRICTED_MEDIA_PREFIXES` — `welfare/`, `cnic/`, `financial/`, `confidential/`, `members/`). NEW perm `announcements.broadcast` (MODULES.OVERSIGHT) in the catalog + `NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS` + `OMJ_ADMIN_KEYS` seed (ALL_TENANTS, OMJ-only — a tenant authors only its OWN pages with `notifications.send`).

  **API module `apps/api/src/announcements/`.** `AnnouncementsService` — **Khundi side (OWN_TENANT, runWithTenant):** `listForTenant`/`createForTenant`/`updateForTenant`/`deleteForTenant` + `getForMember` (login-gated read: published+unexpired, RLS-scoped, audience match via build-step-76 `resolveAudienceMemberIds` mapping the user's `omjCardNumber`→member; 403 if outside the audience, 404 otherwise). **OMJ side (ALL_TENANTS, runAsPlatform, tenant_id=null):** `listOmj`/`createOmj`/`updateOmj`/`deleteOmj` + `broadcast`. **Public (runAsPlatform):** `getPublicBySlug` returns the SANITIZED view only for a public+published+unexpired page that re-passes the content guard at the boundary, else 404 — never joins member/welfare/financial. `assertPublicSafe` enforces the guard on create/update whenever `visibility==='public'` (rejects with human reasons). Slug gen = `randomInt` over the alphabet, retried on the P2002 global-unique collision. **OMJ broadcast fan-out:** reads only OMJ's OWN tenant REGISTRY (display names) cross-tenant; then per target Khundi resolves the per-Khundi audience INSIDE that Khundi's context (`all_members` → selector; `gender` → tenant-scoped member ids → `custom`; `roles` → tenant-scoped role-ids-by-name → `custom`) and calls build-step-76 `send(tenantId, …)` — isolation absolute, broadcast-DOWN; a per-Khundi failure (no active channel / no recipients) is recorded as `skipped`, never aborting the broadcast. Controllers: `AnnouncementsController` (`announcements`, JwtAuth+ModuleEnablement(NOTIFICATIONS)+Permission; view=`notifications.view`, manage/publish=`notifications.send`), `AnnouncementViewController` (`announcements/view/:slug`, JwtAuth only — member read), `AnnouncementsPlatformController` (`platform/announcements*`, JwtAuth+Permission `announcements.broadcast`@ALL_TENANTS — CRUD + `/broadcast`), `AnnouncementsPublicController` (`public/announcements/:slug`, NO auth + `PublicRateLimitGuard` per-IP fixed-window 60/min — abuse control, not a data control). Module imports NotificationsModule (exports `NotificationsService`); wired into AppModule.

  **Web.** `/announcements` (Khundi manager — list, create with public/login-gated + live `isPublicContentSafe` warn/disable, publish/unpublish, delete; `Megaphone` nav under Operations, `anyOf notifications.view`, mode key NOTIFICATIONS), `/a/[slug]` (STANDALONE unauthenticated public landing page — direct `fetch('/api/public/announcements/:slug')`, plain not-found, no AppShell/token), `/platform/announcements` (OMJ — cross-Khundi broadcast composer with all/gender/roles audience + per-Khundi result table, and OMJ-level page authoring/list/delete; nav under Platform & OMJ, `anyOf announcements.broadcast`). 49 new `t()` keys both locales in `messages-extra.ts` (+ delta `i18n-deltas/announcement-pages.json`).

  **Acceptance.** #1 login-gated served only to authed+tenant-eligible+audience-matching (service spec: in-audience→served, out→403); public served unauth by slug. #2 a public page can NEVER expose restricted data — content-guard spec (CNIC/embed-ref/media-prefix, collects all reasons) + service spec (createForTenant public+CNIC/welfare-ref/welfare-media all `BadRequestException`). #3 URL shortening (`/a/<slug>`); expired/unpublished/non-public/unknown → 404 (service spec). #4 OMJ broadcast fans out per Khundi, isolation absolute, skip-not-abort, gender resolves to `custom` member ids per Khundi (service spec). #5 migration regression + isolation + public-exposure — `announcement-pages.isolation.spec.ts` on real PGlite proves additive migration (RLS ENABLE+FORCE, global-unique slug), Khundi sees only own (not other Khundi, not OMJ-null), cross read/update/delete=0 rows, cross-tenant + OMJ-null INSERT refused by WITH CHECK, global slug-collision refused, deny-by-default + platform/public sees all, tenant-delete cascades own pages (OMJ-null survive).

  **Do-not-break.** Tenant isolation absolute (public pages are sanitized artifacts, not data windows; OMJ broadcasts down, never cross-reads — both tested); §17 secret/PII discipline (no member/welfare/financial join on the public path; content guard at authoring + read boundary); build-step-76 engine reused for fan-out (no change to `send`); no new tenant permission key/module (creds stay behind `messaging_key.manage`).

  **Gates.** Tests **1507/1507** (184 suites). shared typecheck ✅ · API typecheck ✅ · API build (`nest build`) ✅ · web typecheck ✅ · web lint (no ESLint warnings) ✅ · web build (incl. `/announcements`, `/a/[slug]`, `/platform/announcements`) ✅ · `prisma validate` ✅ · i18n parity (en⇔ur) + web-coverage ✅ · zero physical-direction Tailwind in new web files (RTL-safe). Isolation REQUIRED + delivered (incl. nullable-tenant OMJ rows + PUBLIC-exposure path). No-auto preserved (publishing is an explicit human act; the build-step-76 scheduler unchanged). Ends `[CHECKPOINT]`.

- **Build-step 76 — Notification/Announcement engine** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/76-notif-engine-v31` (off the staging head after 75); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE/FIX** (deepens the build-step-35/52 notification engine — the Wave-5 comms foundation 77/78 build on). spec `specs/76-notif-engine-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/76-82-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 5 / item 1.** tests **1485/1485** (181 suites; **+27** net — 4 NEW notif-engine specs: shared-helpers ×10, dispatcher media ×3, isolation ×7, service ×7). **SCHEMA + ISOLATION (REQUIRED + delivered).**

  **Problem (spec §1, C-notifications).** A solid base existed (`Notification` + `recipients`/`scheduledFor`/`templateId`, `MessageTemplate` per-channel, `MessagingChannelConfig` encrypted creds, `PushSubscription`, `resolveAudience`/`send`). Gaps: (1) sends were text-only — no media; (2) the composer offered channels with no configured provider; (3) targeting "multiple members + multiple roles + a saved audience" wasn't unified; (4) no per-type→default-channel routing or per-channel template selection; (5) scheduler reliability; (6) push tenant-scope assurance.

  **Schema (migration `20260719000000_notif_engine`).** Two ADDITIVE changes, neither touches an existing table's RLS: (a) `notifications.attachments JSONB` (nullable) — media attachment REFS only (`[{key, name?, contentType?}]` pointing at build-step-46 vault objects; NEVER a raw URL/PII). (b) NEW TENANT-DATA table `notification_routing` (per-(tenant,kind) `default_channel`, `@@unique([tenant_id,kind])`, RLS ENABLE+FORCE with the docs/MULTITENANCY.md isolation policy + tenant FK cascade). Prisma model `NotificationRouting` + `Notification.attachments` + Tenant back-relation. `npx prisma validate` ✅.

  **Goal 1 — media (acceptance #2).** Shared `NotificationAttachment` + `normalizeAttachments` (drops blank keys, trims, first-occurrence de-dupe, caps at `NOTIFICATION_MAX_ATTACHMENTS=10`) + `channelSupportsMedia`/`CHANNEL_SUPPORTS_MEDIA` (whatsapp+push true, sms false). `send`/`sendPush` normalize + persist attachments on the log row and thread them to dispatch. `MessagingDispatcher.dispatch` degrades by channel — WhatsApp/push carry the refs on the `OutboundMessage`, **SMS gets `[]`** (text-only; no PII-bearing link fabricated); `WebPushSender.dispatch` carries refs in the push payload. The scheduled worker re-threads the row's snapshotted attachments at dispatch.

  **Goal 2 — active-channels-only (acceptance #1).** Shared pure `computeActiveChannels({channelConfigs, legacy, hasPushSubscriptions})` (a channel is active iff an enabled provider exists — per-channel with creds / generic_rest / push-with-≥1-device — or the legacy single config for sms/whatsapp). API `GET /notifications/active-channels` (`NotificationsService.activeChannels`). The composer offers ONLY active channels (falls back to the full set when none are configured so the dropdown isn't empty + the setup banner guides). `send` refuses an inactive channel ("The {channel} channel is not active — configure and enable a provider first.").

  **Goal 3 — composite audience (acceptance #1).** Shared `NotificationAudienceType += 'custom'` + selector fields `memberIds[]`/`roleIds[]`/`audienceId?`. New private `collectCustomMemberIds(tx, tenantId, sel)` unions explicit members ∪ every holder of each role (tenant-scoped role→userRole→user.omjCardNumber→member) ∪ a saved `audienceId` (accepted forward-compat, resolves to nobody until build-step 78), DEDUPED by member; wired into both `resolveAudience` (phone-deduped recipients) and `resolveAudienceMemberIds` (push). DTO `AudienceDto` gains the three fields.

  **Goal 4 — per-kind routing + per-channel templates (acceptance #3).** Shared `DEFAULT_CHANNEL_FOR_KIND` (OMJ defaults — push for announcement/whatsapp for welfare/sms for lawazim, …) + `resolveDefaultChannel`/`buildRoutingTable`/`NotificationRoutingView`. `SendNotificationDto.channel` is now OPTIONAL — an omitted channel routes to the kind's effective default (Khundi `notification_routing` override → OMJ default) via `resolveKindChannel`. `GET /notifications/routing` (`listRouting`, every kind + override flag) + `PUT /notifications/routing/:kind` (`setRouting`, gated `notifications.config`). Per-channel template selection: shared `templateCategoryForKind` + `pickChannelTemplate(templates, kind, channel)` (exact (category,channel) → generic `custom`-on-channel → null; never substitutes a mismatched category); token resolution stays at dispatch (`resolveMessageTokens`).

  **Goals 5–6 — scheduler + push tenant-scope (acceptance #4, #5).** No-auto-fire scheduler unchanged (still only dispatches human-scheduled `queued` rows; attachments now threaded through). Push tenant-scope re-asserted on the real migration chain: a tenant selects only its own `push_subscriptions` (a cross-tenant push target is impossible).

  **Permissions/§17.** NO new permission key/module — reads `notifications.view`, sends/routing-read `notifications.send`/`notifications.view`, routing-write `notifications.config`, secret creds stay behind `messaging_key.manage`. Provider credentials remain AES-256-GCM, never returned/logged (unchanged; existing secret tests pass).

  **Web (`apps/web/app/notifications/page.tsx`).** Composer offers active channels only; selecting a kind pre-selects its routing default channel; NEW `custom` composite audience (Pro) with role checkboxes; NEW Pro media-refs input (storage keys → attachments); NEW Pro+config per-kind routing editor (kind→channel `<Select>`, `PUT /routing/:kind`). 10 new `t()` keys both locales in `messages-extra.ts` + delta `i18n-deltas/notif-engine.json` (`notif.media`/`mediaPlaceholder`/`mediaHint`/`customRoles`/`customNoRoles`/`customHint`/`routing`/`routingHint`/`routingDefault`/`routingSaved`); `custom` added to the `notification_audience` formatLabel map (en+ur).

  **Files.** schema.prisma (+`attachments`, +`NotificationRouting`, Tenant relation) · migration `20260719000000_notif_engine/migration.sql` · `packages/shared/src/index.ts` (attachment + routing + active-channel + template helpers; `custom` audience; view `attachments`) · api notifications: `notifications.dto.ts`, `notifications.service.ts`, `notifications.controller.ts`, `notifications-mapper.ts`, `messaging/messaging-adapter.ts`, `messaging/messaging.dispatcher.ts`, `messaging/web-push.sender.ts` · NEW specs `notif-engine-shared.spec.ts`, `messaging-dispatcher.spec.ts`, `notif-engine.isolation.spec.ts`, `notif-engine.service.spec.ts` · fixed `notifications-helpers.spec.ts` (view `attachments: []`) · web `notifications/page.tsx` + `messages-extra.ts` + delta.

  **Decisions.** (1) Added a dedicated `notification_routing` table (CODEREF flagged only `attachments` but spec §2.4 requires Khundi-configurable routing with OMJ defaults — a per-config table matches every other config in the project and rides the standard RLS policy). (2) Composite audience modeled as a NEW `custom` type (clean, leaves the existing single-source types untouched) rather than overloading every type. (3) `audienceId`/saved-audience accepted but resolves to nobody until build-step 78 (forward-compatible, logged in code). (4) SMS media-degrade DROPS attachments from the payload (no link fabricated) — keeps §17/77 public-content discipline; the log row still records what was composed. (5) `pickChannelTemplate` never substitutes a category-mismatched template (returns null → body used) so an event invite never ships welfare copy. (6) Composer offers all channels when none are active so the UI isn't dead in a fresh tenant; the API is the real enforcement.

  **Gates.** typecheck (web ✅ + shared ✅ + api ✅) · lint (web ✅, no warnings) · web-build ✅ (all routes) · prisma-validate ✅ · `npm test` **1485/1485** (181 suites) incl. i18n parity + web-coverage ✅ · isolation REQUIRED + delivered (`notif-engine.isolation.spec.ts` — real chain through step 76 on PGlite, non-superuser: attachments col, `notification_routing` RLS ENABLE+FORCE + read/update/delete/insert isolation + deny-by-default + platform bypass + cascade; push tenant-scope) · media-degrade proven (`messaging-dispatcher.spec.ts`, live spy adapters) · zero physical-direction Tailwind · RTL-safe · no raw enums on screen. **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (branch `feat/76-notif-engine-v31`).

- **Build-step 75 — Accounting/reconciliation UI cleanup: tabbed IA + match/clear reconciliation** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/75-accounting-reports-cleanup-v31` (off the staging head after 74); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (UI/UX cleanup of the accounting surface; closes Wave 4). spec `specs/75-accounting-reports-cleanup-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/70-75-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 4 / item 6 — closes Wave 4 (70–75).** tests **1458/1458** (177 suites; **+0** net — pure front-end, the change is covered by the existing i18n parity + web-coverage gates). **NO SCHEMA · Isolation ➖.**

  **Problem (spec §1, C-accounting-ui).** The accounting module packed cashbook, ledgers, vouchers, bank reconciliation, COA and funds (build-step 70) onto crowded long-scroll screens. The review wanted it split into clear tabs, with the deep Pro tools (reconciliation, full ledger, voucher register, COA tree) surfaced cleanly in Pro and a clean cashbook+funds view in Simple.

  **Isolation reason (➖).** Pure presentation re-organization of `apps/web/app/accounting/page.tsx`. No API, no new query, no schema/migration — every read still flows through the existing tenant-scoped accounting endpoints (`/accounting/cashbook|entries|summary|trial-balance|balance-sheet|reconciliations|...`) under unchanged RLS. The double-entry engine is untouched. (Wave-4 CODEREF marks 75 as light/➖ — existing tenant reads.)

  **Goal 1 — tabbed accounting (build-step-38 IA via `ModuleTabs`).** Replaced the long-scroll body with 8 tabs in the spec §2.1 order: **Overview** (KPI StatCards + income-vs-expense `BarsChart`, both modes — de-crowded summary only) / **Cashbook** (the record-money-in/out form + running cashbook table + CSV export — the heart of the Simple face, both modes; Pro adds the head + cash/bank selectors) / **Funds & Donations** (the build-step-70 `FundsPanel`, both modes, self-gated by `funds.*`) / **Ledger** (trial balance / per-head ledger `DataList`, Pro) / **Vouchers** (printable journal/voucher register `DataList` + Print row-action + badge count, Pro) / **Banks & reconciliation** (bank/cash accounts + add-bank + statement + reconciliation open/detail, Pro) / **Chart of accounts** (build-step-70 COA tree with Flat/Tree toggle + add-head, Pro) / **Reports** (financial report by head, Pro). Each Pro-depth tab carries `hidden: mode !== 'pro'`.

  **Goal 2 — reconciliation cleanup (spec §2).** NEW `reconFilter` state (`'all'|'matched'|'uncleared'`). On the reconciliation detail card, a 3-button filter (All / Cleared / Uncleared) with live counts (`reconMatchedCount`/`reconUnclearedCount`) narrows the line table to just the lines that still need ticking on a long statement. "Cleared" = the line carries THIS reconciliation's id (the `JournalLine.reconciliationId` clear flag, `l.reconciliationId === detail.id`); "Uncleared" = it does not. The filtered `reconLines` drives the table render + the empty state ("No lines match this filter." vs "No bank movements to reconcile."), while `toggleCleared` still computes its next cleared-set over the FULL `detail.lines` — so filtering is view-only and never drops a tick.

  **Goal 3 — mode discipline (build-step 60).** The Pro-depth tabs are PRESENTATION-density only: a permitted user switches to Pro to reach Ledger/Vouchers/Banks/COA. No admin capability is HIDDEN by mode (the permission gate, not the mode, governs access) — `ModuleTabs` simply filters `hidden` tabs out of the Simple density view, and auto-reselects a visible tab if the active one disappears on a mode switch (existing `module-shell` behaviour).

  **Files.** `apps/web/app/accounting/page.tsx` (the whole tab re-organization + `reconFilter`/`reconLines`/counts + the filter UI). `packages/shared/src/messages-extra.ts` (9 new keys both `MESSAGES_EXTRA_EN`/`_UR`: `acct.tabCashbook`/`tabVouchers`/`tabCoa`/`tabBanks`/`reconFilterAll`/`reconFilterMatched`/`reconFilterUncleared`/`noLinesForFilter`, + `acct.tabLedger` retitled "Ledger / entries" → "Ledger"). NEW delta `packages/shared/src/i18n-deltas/accounting-cleanup.json` (en+ur, the source-of-truth pairs). No API/prisma/test files changed.

  **Decisions.** (1) Kept the WIP tab split that was already in the working tree, completed the unfinished `reconFilter` (declared-but-unused → would have failed lint) into the spec §2 match/clear surface. (2) Tab order follows spec §2.1 exactly (Banks & reconciliation before Chart of accounts) — reordered the COA tab to sit after Banks. (3) Cashbook split into its own tab so Overview stays a de-crowded KPI/chart glance; both remain visible in Simple (Simple = cashbook + funds overview, per acceptance #1). (4) "Cleared"/"Uncleared" filter labels reuse the screen's existing reconciliation vocabulary (the column header is "Cleared", `clearedBalance`/`clearedCount`) rather than the spec's "matched" wording, for on-screen consistency. (5) No new tests — a pure UI change; correctness is enforced by the i18n parity gate (`i18n.spec.ts`, en⇔ur key parity) + the web-coverage gate (`i18n-web-coverage.spec.ts`, every static `t('key')` resolves), both of which exercise the 9 new keys and passed.

  **Gates.** typecheck (web ✅ + shared ✅) · lint (web ✅, no unused `reconFilter`) · web-build ✅ · prisma-validate ✅ (no schema change; valid with a dummy `DATABASE_URL`) · `npm test` **1458/1458** (177 suites) incl. i18n parity + web-coverage ✅ · zero physical-direction Tailwind in the edits (logical `ms-`/flex/gap only) · RTL-safe · no raw enums on screen (all labels via `t()`/`formatLabel`/`StatusChip`). **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (branch `feat/75-accounting-reports-cleanup-v31`).

- **Build-step 74 — Graveyard registry: OMJ-standard + Khundi-local + merge-on-remove** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/74-graveyard-registry-v31` (off the staging head after 73); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (replaces the free-text graveyard with a managed registry). spec `specs/74-graveyard-registry-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/70-75-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 4 / item 5.** tests **1458/1458** (177 suites; **+25** net — 4 NEW graveyard specs: service ×7, access ×7, isolation ×7, migration ×4). **SCHEMA + ISOLATION (REQUIRED + delivered).**

  **Problem (spec §1, C-graveyard).** `DeathRecord` stored the graveyard as FREE TEXT (`graveyardName` + `graveyardSource` 'omj'|'external' + `graveNumber`). Free text means typos, no canonical OMJ-graveyard list, and removing/renaming a graveyard orphaned records. Decision: a MANAGED registry — an OMJ-managed dropdown of OMJ graveyards + free entry for external — with MERGE-ON-REMOVE so removing a graveyard re-points its death records rather than orphaning them.

  **Altitude / isolation design (build-step-66 "OMJ governs / Khundi consumes", isolation ABSOLUTE).** Two tables, mirroring `taxonomy_standard`/`taxonomy_local`: (a) **`graveyard_standard`** — the OMJ canonical list, GLOBAL reference data with **NO `tenant_id` and NO Row-Level Security** (like `permissions`/`taxonomy_standard`); only this list flows DOWN, read by every Khundi on its tenant path. (b) **`graveyard_local`** — a Khundi's own EXTERNAL graveyards, **FULL TENANT DATA: tenant_id FK ON DELETE CASCADE + RLS ENABLE + FORCE** with the docs/MULTITENANCY.md `graveyard_local_isolation` policy (`app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()`, USING + WITH CHECK). A Khundi can NEVER read/write another's locals; the OMJ platform path (`runAsPlatform` → `app_rls_bypass()`) is the ONLY cross-Khundi reach, gated `graveyard.govern` @ ALL_TENANTS. This is the build-step-49 OMJ-centralized pattern, NOT a v4 cross-org data read.

  **Schema (`apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma`).** NEW `GraveyardStandard {id, name @@unique, location?, active, createdBy?, createdAt, updatedAt}` (`@@map graveyard_standard`, no tenant). NEW `GraveyardLocal {id, tenantId, name, location?, active, createdBy?, ts; @@unique[tenantId,name]; @@index[tenantId]; tenant FK Cascade}` (`@@map graveyard_local`). `DeathRecord += graveyardId String? @db.Uuid` — a **SOFT ref (no DB FK)** because it may point at EITHER table (a relational FK can't span both). `graveyardSource`/`graveyardName`/`graveNumber` RETAINED for back-compat + true one-off external free entries (denormalised label kept in step with the pick). `Tenant += graveyardLocals GraveyardLocal[]`.

  **Migration (`20260718000000_graveyard_registry`).** Creates both tables + the RLS policy on `graveyard_local`; `ALTER TABLE death_records ADD COLUMN graveyard_id`. **Backfill (no loss):** distinct `external` free-text `graveyard_name` per tenant → inserted into that Khundi's `graveyard_local` (`ON CONFLICT (tenant_id,name) DO NOTHING`), then each matching `death_records` row re-points `graveyard_id` to it. OMJ-source free-text stays free text (`graveyard_id` null) until OMJ creates the standard list + re-points via merge-on-remove — a Khundi never auto-owns an OMJ graveyard. Runs on the migration connection (RLS bypass) so it spans every Khundi's own rows without crossing isolation at runtime.

  **Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`, pure).** `GraveyardSource = 'omj'|'external'` + `GRAVEYARD_SOURCES`; `GraveyardScope = 'standard'|'local'` + `graveyardScopeSource(scope)` (standard⇒omj, local⇒external — source DERIVED from table identity, never stored); `GraveyardView {id,name,location,active,scope,source,createdAt}`; `GraveyardRegistryView {standard[],local[]}`; `GraveyardOption {id,label,scope}` + `buildGraveyardOptions(standard,local)` (active-only, standard-first, name-sorted — the death-record picker source); `DeathRecordView`/`DeathRecordInput += graveyardId`.

  **API (`apps/api/src/graveyard/` NEW module).** `GraveyardService` (mapper `toGraveyardView(row, scope)`): **Khundi side (`runWithTenant`/RLS):** `listForKhundi` (active standard + all own locals), `addLocal` (immediately usable; idempotent on own name; rejects a name that is an OMJ standard — pick it instead), `updateLocal` (name/location/active; rename collision-checked vs standard + own locals), `removeLocal(id, targetId)` = MERGE-ON-REMOVE (re-point this Khundi's `DeathRecord.graveyardId` + denormalised name/source onto target, then delete; target = a standard or another own active local; refuses self-merge / inactive / unknown). **OMJ side (`runAsPlatform`):** `listStandard` (incl. inactive), `createStandard` (dup-name rejected), `updateStandard`, `removeStandard(id, targetId)` = MERGE-ON-REMOVE across ALL Khundis (target must be another active standard; re-points every Khundi's records then deletes). All audited (`graveyard.*` log lines). Two controllers: `GraveyardController` @ `/graveyard` (Khundi — GET list gated `death.view`; POST/PATCH/POST :id/merge-remove `local` gated `death.record`, OWN_TENANT) + `GraveyardPlatformController` @ `/platform/graveyard` (OMJ — GET/POST/PATCH/POST :id/merge-remove gated `graveyard.govern` @ ALL_TENANTS). `GraveyardModule` wired into `app.module.ts`.

  **Bereavement integration (`apps/api/src/bereavement/`).** Create + update DENORMALISE the picked registry graveyard: `resolveGraveyard(tx, graveyardId)` looks up standard then local (BadRequest if neither — "not in the registry for this Khundi"), and writes `graveyardId` + `graveyardSource`/`graveyardName` FROM the row (label kept in step). Omitting `graveyardId` keeps whatever free-text the form supplied (one-off external). `bereavement.dto` + `bereavement-mapper` carry `graveyardId`.

  **Web.** Bereavement form (`apps/web/app/bereavement/page.tsx`): graveyard `<Select>` with optgroups — "OMJ graveyards" (active standard) + "Your external graveyards" (active locals) + an "Other / not listed (free text)" first option; when "Other" is chosen the legacy `graveyardSource` + free-text `graveyardName` inputs show, with a "Save to my graveyards & use" button (`addExternalGraveyard` → `POST /graveyard/local`, gated `death.record`) so the next burial in the same graveyard picks it from the dropdown. NEW `/platform/graveyard` OMJ management screen (oversight area, `anyOf:['graveyard.govern']` nav entry "Graveyard Registry"): list/create/edit standard graveyards + merge-on-remove with a target picker. `death.record` reused for Khundi graveyard management (no `bereavement.manage` key exists — same documented call as build-step-73's `prize.approve`).

  **Decisions.** (1) Two-table split (not one tenant-attributed table with OMJ rows) — chosen per CODEREF's preferred option, keeps RLS trivial (standard = no RLS reference; local = standard tenant policy) and matches `taxonomy_standard`/`taxonomy_local`. (2) Soft ref (no FK) on `DeathRecord.graveyardId` because it spans two tables. (3) Khundi gate = existing `death.view`/`death.record` (no `bereavement.manage` in the catalog — managing graveyards is part of recording a burial; same precedent as build-step 73). (4) `source` derived from scope, never stored. (5) Backfill only maps `external` free-text (OMJ-source left for OMJ to govern) — no Khundi auto-owns an OMJ graveyard. (6) Standard merge target must itself be a standard graveyard (the re-point spans all Khundis, so a local can't be the cross-Khundi target). (7) `graveyard.govern` permission + the OMJ default-role grant already existed in the catalog (added speculatively earlier) — wired here.

  **Files.** schema.prisma; `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260718000000_graveyard_registry/migration.sql`; `apps/api/src/graveyard/{graveyard.module,graveyard.service,graveyard.controller,graveyard.dto,graveyard.mapper}.ts` + specs `{graveyard.service,graveyard.access,graveyard.isolation,graveyard.migration}.spec.ts`; `apps/api/src/app.module.ts`; `apps/api/src/bereavement/{bereavement.service,bereavement.dto,bereavement-mapper}.ts`; `apps/api/src/provisioning/default-roles.ts`; `apps/web/app/bereavement/page.tsx`; `apps/web/app/platform/graveyard/page.tsx` (NEW); `apps/web/app/ui/nav.ts`; `packages/shared/src/index.ts` + `messages-extra.ts` (+ NEW `i18n-deltas/graveyard-registry.json`).
