- **Build-step 73 — Prize fixes: controlled reopen + ceremony-scoped apply/list** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/73-prize-fixes-v31` (off the staging head after 72); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (corrects build-step-29/50 prize rough edges from the review). spec `specs/73-prize-fixes-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/70-75-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 4 / item 4.** tests **1433/1433** (173 suites; **+5** net — all in `prize.service.spec.ts`). **NO-SCHEMA — no new table/column/enum. Isolation ➖→light:** every changed read/write rides the already-tenant-scoped `runWithTenant`/RLS path (the existing prize models keep their build-step-29/50 ENABLE+FORCE policy); there is no new persistence and no cross-tenant read, so no isolation/migration gate is added (stated per the spec's "isolation light — state reason"). No-auto preserved: reopen is an explicit, audited controller act (never automatic), and assignment/approval flows are untouched (§3.5).

  **Problem (spec §1).** Prize (`PrizeCeremony`/`PrizeApplication`, build-step 29/50) worked but had four rough edges: (1) applications weren't clearly ceremony-scoped in the apply flow / list; (2) a closed ceremony couldn't be reopened cleanly for a late legitimate applicant (the lifecycle `draft→announced→open→closed→completed` had no controlled backward step); (3) the apply category picker didn't clearly separate active application categories from recognition; (4) apply/assign/approve button intents were ambiguous vs the Wave-1 RowAction conventions.

  **API (no schema).** NEW `PrizeService.reopen(tenantId, id, closesAt?, actorId)` — the ONLY backward lifecycle transition (`closed→open`): refused with `BadRequestException` unless status is currently `closed` (a draft/announced/open ceremony is not "closed"; a completed one is final), `NotFoundException` on an unknown ceremony, and always audited (`prize.ceremony.reopen` log line). An optional `closesAt` re-sets the new window's end (omitted ⇒ existing `closesAt` left untouched). NEW `ReopenCeremonyDto {closesAt? @IsISO8601}`. NEW `POST /prize/ceremonies/:id/reopen` gated `prize.approve` — **note:** the spec text says "gated `prize.manage`" but no such permission key exists in the `@kc/shared` catalog; the ceremony lifecycle (status transitions, create/edit) is uniformly gated `prize.approve`, so reopen aligns with it (documented decision, not a silent deviation). The normal `apply` gate (`isCeremonySubmissionOpen` — status/opensAt/closesAt) then governs submissions on the reopened window unchanged.

  **Web (`apps/web/app/prize/page.tsx`, UI-only).** (1) **Ceremony-scoped apply:** `activeCeremony` is computed client-side with build-step-69 semantics (newest ceremony that isn't `completed`, else newest overall — the list already arrives `createdAt`-desc); opening the Submit-application modal (`openApply`) defaults `form.ceremonyId` to the active ceremony (keeping any ceremony the user already picked). (2) **Ceremony-scoped list:** a toolbar `<Select>` (DataList `toolbar` slot) filters the applications list by ceremony — `ceremonyFilter` state (`null`=land on active, `''`=explicit "All ceremonies", id=one); `effectiveCeremonyFilter = ceremonyFilter ?? activeCeremony?.id ?? ''`; the DataList rows + the eligibles/announcement exports + the count all follow `filteredApps`; a per-ceremony empty state. (3) **Controlled reopen UI:** the Re-open button now renders ONLY when `canApprove && c.status === 'closed'` and calls the dedicated `reopenCeremony` → `POST …/reopen` (previously it showed for any status index > 1 and called the GENERIC status-setter, which allowed an arbitrary jump straight to `open`). (4) **Button intents (Wave-1):** Submit-application → `variant="primary"` (apply=primary), panel Assign → `variant="primary"` (assign=primary); approve=success / reject=danger row actions were already aligned. (5) **Category selectability** already correct — `applicationCategories` (active + `awardType==='application_based'`) feeds the apply picker; recognition is a separate direct-assign flow (`recognitionCategories`); verified, no change needed. Removed the now-unused `PRIZE_CEREMONY_STATUSES` import. 5 new `t()` keys (`prize.reopened`, `prize.reopenError`, `prize.filterByCeremony`, `prize.allCeremonies`, `prize.noApplicationsInCeremony`) in BOTH locales (`messages-extra.ts`) + delta `i18n-deltas/prize-fixes.json`; zero physical-direction CSS (`ms-2`, `basis-48`, logical only); RTL-safe; no raw enums on screen (ceremony status routes through `formatLabel`).

  **Decisions.** (1) Reopen gated `prize.approve` not the spec's `prize.manage` (no such key exists) — aligned with the rest of the ceremony lifecycle. (2) Active-instance computed on the client from the already-loaded ceremonies rather than calling `/prize/instances` — avoids an extra round-trip and matches `pickActiveInstance` semantics (newest active, fallback newest). (3) The exports within the applications tab follow the ceremony filter so an "Announcement"/"Eligibles" export matches the displayed ceremony. (4) No change to the per-ceremony-card eligibles/announce (those are already scoped to that card's ceremony). (5) No `prize.manage` permission was invented — adding a catalog permission would be schema/RBAC churn outside this FIX's scope.

  **Files.** `apps/api/src/prize/{prize.dto,prize.service,prize.controller}.ts`; `apps/web/app/prize/page.tsx`; `packages/shared/src/messages-extra.ts` (+ NEW `packages/shared/src/i18n-deltas/prize-fixes.json`); extended `apps/api/src/prize/prize.service.spec.ts` (NEW "controlled reopen" describe — 5 specs: closed→open, closesAt re-set, closesAt kept when omitted, refuses non-closed draft/announced/open/completed, NotFound on unknown).

  **Gates.** typecheck (api+web), lint (api+web), `npm test -w apps/api` (1433/1433, 173 suites), `prisma validate` (schema valid — unchanged), web build all green. i18n parity (en⇔ur identical key set) + web-coverage (every `t()` resolves) green. Zero physical-direction Tailwind. No isolation/migration spec added — NO-SCHEMA step, all reads/writes ride the existing tenant-scoped RLS path (reason stated above per spec §4.5).

- **Build-step 72 — Events multi-type + agenda + fast attendance** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/72-events-attendance-v31` (off the staging head after 71); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (deepens the build-step-28 events module). spec `specs/72-events-attendance-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/70-75-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 4 / item 3.** tests **1428/1428** (173 suites; **+18** net — 2 NEW specs + extended events/members service specs). **SCHEMA-LIGHT — no NEW tenant table: `events.agenda` ADD COLUMN + bulk attendance over the existing `event_registrations`; RLS unchanged. Isolation+migration gate written + green.** No-auto preserved (attendance marks explicit + `marked_by`/`marked_at`; announce drafts a `draft` message + a `queued` reminder only on the explicit announce act — nothing fires on its own). CNIC-gate enforced + tested (acceptance #5).

  **Problem (spec §1).** `Event` + `EventRegistration` exist (build-step 28) but: roll-call was one-by-one (slow for a big gathering); no structured agenda; no inline dues collection at an event; no announce/reminder prompt on create; and `EventType` lacked the community's ceremony / janaza kinds.

  **Schema / migration (`20260717000000_events_agenda_attendance`).** `EventType += ceremony, janaza` (additive `ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS`); `events.agenda JSONB` nullable (ordered `[{no,title,note?}]`). Attendance stays the existing `event_registrations` row — the roll-call + bulk endpoints are pure application logic over it, NOT a new table. New enum values not referenced in their own migration DDL (PostgreSQL add-then-use safe); `ADD COLUMN` never alters existing-table RLS, so `events`/`event_registrations` keep their build-step-28 ENABLE+FORCE policy.

  **Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`, pure + tested).** `EventType`/`EVENT_TYPES += ceremony, janaza` + LABEL_CATALOG `event_type` entries (en+ur). `AgendaItem {no,title,note?}` + `normalizeAgenda(raw)` (re-number from 1, drop blanks, tolerant of legacy `string[]`). `EventView += agenda: AgendaItem[]`. `eventReminderAt(startsAtIso, nowIso, leadHours=24)` — pure: returns the ISO time `leadHours` before start, or null when no start / unparseable / the time would be in the past (a reminder is never scheduled for the past). `BulkAttendanceResult {marked, registrations[]}` + `AnnounceEventView {announcementId, recipientCount, reminderId, reminderAt}`.

  **API.** `events.dto`: `AgendaItemDto`, `CreateEventDto/UpdateEventDto += agenda?`, `SetAgendaDto`, `BulkAttendanceDto {entries[{memberId,attended}], via?}`, `AnnounceEventDto {note?, remind?, leadHours?}`. `events-mapper`: `toEventView` maps `agenda` via `normalizeAgenda`. `events.service`: create/update persist a normalized agenda; NEW `setAgenda` (refused once completed), `bulkMarkAttendance` (de-dupes by member last-write-wins; each upsert is an explicit mark stamping `marked_by`/`marked_at`; a foreign/unknown member is SKIPPED not fatal; returns count + affected views), `announce` (composes + saves a `draft`-status `event_invite` Notification to active members — never auto-sent, mirrors build-step-71 janaza; when `remind!==false` AND `eventReminderAt` is non-null, ALSO creates a `queued` `meeting_notice` with `scheduledFor` = the reminder time — the explicit consequence of the announce act, picked up by the Wave-5 dispatch worker). `events.controller`: `PUT /events/:id/agenda` + `POST /events/:id/announce` (events.create), `POST /events/:id/attendance/bulk` (events.attendance) — NO new permission key. **Roll-call member search:** `members.dto.MemberSearchQueryDto += cnic?`; `members.service.search(tenantId, query, {allowCnic})` — when a `cnic` fragment is given AND `allowCnic`, scans a bounded candidate set (within the scope filters), DECRYPTS each at-rest CNIC (`normalizeCnic(this.cnic.decrypt(...))`), matches `.includes(fragment)`, returns the SAME lean shape (NEVER the CNIC); else the open `q`/name path runs (lean select, no `cnicEncrypted` read). `members.controller.search` now injects `PermissionService`, takes `@CurrentUser()`, and when `query.cnic` is present checks `members.reveal_cnic` (`hasPermission`) — a caller without it gets `ForbiddenException` and the service is never reached.

  **Web (`apps/web/app/events/page.tsx`).** NEW **Roll-call** row action (gated `events.attendance`) opens a `RollCallModal`: loads the active roster (`GET /members/search?activeOnly=true`) + this event's registrations, seeds a local `pending` attendance map; a debounced search box (250ms) hits `/members/search` by name/card, or — with a "search by CNIC" toggle shown only to `members.reveal_cnic` holders — by `cnic` fragment; big touch-target per-row present toggles (build-step 38), All-present/All-absent over the filtered list, Enter-to-toggle the top match (`useHotkeys`, build-step 59), an optional `BarcodeDetector` QR scan button (feature-detected — renders nothing when unsupported; matches the scanned id/card to a loaded member), and an inline **Collect dues** action (gated `lawazim.record`) → `CollectDuesModal` → existing `POST /lawazim/payments`. Save computes the diff vs loaded attendance and applies it in ONE `POST /events/:id/attendance/bulk`. NEW **Announce** row action + an announce-on-create prompt (after creating a `scheduled` event) → `ConfirmDialog` → `POST /events/:id/announce` (drafts message + soft reminder; copy says nothing is auto-sent). Agenda editor (ordered title+note rows) in the create/edit modal (Pro) + agenda display in the expand panel. 36 new `t()` keys in BOTH locales (messages-extra.ts) + delta `i18n-deltas/events-rollcall.json`; zero physical-direction CSS (`start-2.5`, `ps-8`, `text-start`); RTL-safe; no raw enums on screen.

  **Decisions.** (1) Inline dues REUSE the existing lawazim payment endpoint unchanged — the spec says "reuse the lawazim service (existing)"; lawazim's own accounting posting (or lack thereof) is out of this step's seam, so no lawazim/accounting change was made (noted honestly rather than fabricating a posting). (2) Partial-CNIC search decrypts the at-rest CNIC server-side (the spec's "matches the cnicToken/encrypted path") — the build-step-48 token is a full-value HMAC and cannot match a fragment, so decrypt-and-filter over a bounded, permission-gated, debounced candidate set is the correct approach; the CNIC is never returned. (3) The CNIC permission gate lives in the controller (the service has no actor/permission context) via the exported `PermissionService.hasPermission` — same engine the guard uses; tested at the controller level. (4) Announce = a `draft` announcement (human reviews + sends) + a `queued` scheduled reminder (the explicit, audited consequence of the announce act, consistent with build-step-35 scheduled sends) — no-auto holds because nothing sends without the explicit announce request, and the announcement itself is never auto-fired. (5) Bulk attendance staged locally then flushed as a single diff call — fast roll-call UX while every applied mark is still explicit + audited server-side. (6) Multi-type added `ceremony` + `janaza` only (the spec's named gaps); `welfare_drive`/`sports`/`prize` already covered the rest.

  **Files.** Migration `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260717000000_events_agenda_attendance/migration.sql`; `apps/api/prisma/schema.prisma` (EventType + Event.agenda); `packages/shared/src/index.ts` (+ `i18n-deltas/events-rollcall.json`, `messages-extra.ts`); `apps/api/src/events/{events.dto,events-mapper,events.service,events.controller}.ts`; `apps/api/src/members/{members.dto,members.service,members.controller}.ts`; `apps/web/app/events/page.tsx`. NEW specs `apps/api/src/events/events-agenda.isolation.spec.ts` + `apps/api/src/members/members-cnic-search.spec.ts`; extended `apps/api/src/events/events.service.spec.ts` + `apps/api/src/members/members.service.spec.ts`.

  **Gates.** typecheck (api+web+shared), lint (api+web), `npm test -w apps/api` (1428/1428, 173 suites), `prisma validate`, web build all green. i18n parity (en⇔ur identical key set) + web-coverage (every `t()` resolves) green. Migration+isolation gate green (agenda nullable, enum additive, RLS ENABLE+FORCE intact, per-tenant isolation + WITH-CHECK + unique-(event,member) hold). CNIC-gate test green (no `members.reveal_cnic` ⇒ 403, service never called). Zero physical-direction Tailwind.

- **Build-step 71 — Bereavement expense-lines + member-expired + OMJ notify + janaza** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/71-bereavement-expenses-v31` (off the staging head after 70); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (deepens the build-step-47 bereavement module). spec `specs/71-bereavement-expenses-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/70-75-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 4 / item 2.** tests **1410/1410** (171 suites; **+14** net — 1 NEW spec + extended service/funds specs). **MONEY + SCHEMA — NEW tenant tables `bereavement_expenses`/`omj_notifications` (RLS ENABLE+FORCE); isolation+migration gate written + green.** Double-entry invariant preserved (every cost-line posts a balanced entry; removal posts a reversal — no money un-posted silently); no-auto preserved (member-expired + OMJ-flag are human-confirmed consequences of the explicit record-death act, never a push).

  **Problem (spec §1).** `DeathRecord` (build-step 47) carried a single `bereavementAmount` lump sum — but a bereavement has multiple costs (grave, transport, arrangements) each needing its own invoice + accounting posting. No member-expired flow, no janaza announcement, eligibility unmodelled, and two fields (`graveIssuedDate` + the relation-to-non-member input) flagged for removal by the review.

  **Schema / migration (`20260716000000_bereavement_expenses`).** NEW `bereavement_expenses` (TENANT DATA, RLS ENABLE+FORCE, cascading tenant FK + cascading `death_record_id` FK): `id, tenant_id, death_record_id, category, amount Int, fund_id?(soft ref), invoice_ref?(vault key), note?, journal_entry_id?(soft ref), created_by, ts`. NEW `omj_notifications` (TENANT DATA, RLS ENABLE+FORCE): `id, tenant_id, kind, subject_member_id?(soft), death_record_id?(soft), payload Json?, status('pending'/'acknowledged'), created_by, ts`. `death_records.bereavement_amount` → NULLABLE (legacy header; total now DERIVES from lines) via non-destructive `DROP NOT NULL`/`DROP DEFAULT`. Enums: `JournalSourceModule += 'bereavement'`, `NotificationStatus += 'draft'` (a janaza draft — the dispatch worker only picks `queued`, so a draft is never auto-fired). New enum VALUES not used in their own migration's DDL (PostgreSQL add-then-use safe). Tenant model gained `bereavementExpenses`/`omjNotifications` back-relations.

  **Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`, pure + tested).** `BereavementExpenseView`; `BEREAVEMENT_EXPENSE_CATEGORIES` (`grave`/`transport`/`arrangements`/`shroud`/`assistance`/`other`); `summarizeBereavementExpenses(lines)`→`{total,count}` (clamped, the ONLY total source); `bereavementEligibility({deceasedMemberId})`→`'member'|'non_member'` (ADVISORY — never consulted server-side, never blocks); `JanazaDraftView`. `DeathRecordView += expenseTotal/expenseCount` and `bereavementAmount` now derives (lines if any, else legacy header). `isBereavementPaid` widened (`journalEntryId` OR `expenseCount>0`). `JournalSourceModule += 'bereavement'`. NEW LABEL_CATALOG domains `bereavement_expense_category` + `bereavement_eligibility` (en+ur). 

  **API.** NEW tx-aware `changeMemberStatusInTx(tx,tenantId,memberId,status,reason,actorId)` in `members/member-status.helper.ts` — extracted from `MembersService.changeStatus` (which now delegates to it), reused so bereavement marks a member expired ATOMICALLY (immutable `member_status_history` + auto timeline row, spec 62) inside the record-death tx with NO cross-module Nest dep / nested tx. `accounting.service`: widened `postModuleExpenseInTx`/`reverseEntryInTx`/`persistEntry` source unions to include `bereavement`. `bereavement.service`: `recordDeath` now (a) stores `bereavement_amount` only when explicitly given, (b) when a member is linked + `markMemberExpired !== false` marks it expired + creates an `omj_notifications` `member_expired` flag in the same tx; NEW `listExpenses`/`addExpense` (posts a balanced fund-tagged Bereavement expense via `postModuleExpenseInTx`, atomic, stamps `journal_entry_id`; rejects inactive/foreign fund)/`removeExpense` (posts the inverse via `reverseEntryInTx` then deletes — reversal-not-edit); NEW `draftJanaza` (composes + saves a `draft`-status Notification to active members — never auto-sent); legacy `postBereavementPayment` retained (source now `bereavement`). `funds.service` `listFunds`/`setFundActive` fund EXPENSE now DERIVES from fund-tagged `bereavement_expenses` (income−expense balance). Controller: `GET/POST /deaths/:id/expenses`, `DELETE /deaths/:id/expenses/:lineId` (204), `POST /deaths/:id/janaza` — all reuse existing `death.view`/`death.record` (NO new permission key). DTO: `RecordDeathDto` DROPS `graveIssuedDate`, ADDS `markMemberExpired?`; NEW `AddBereavementExpenseDto`/`DraftJanazaDto`.

  **Web (`apps/web/app/bereavement/page.tsx`).** Record-death form DROPS the `graveIssuedDate` + relation-non-member inputs (spec §2.5) and ADDS a mark-expired checkbox (shown only when a member is linked, default ON, with a "flags OMJ — never a silent push" hint). Death-record expand panel gains: an ADVISORY eligibility chip (member/non-member, "never blocks" copy); a cost-lines sub-list (category chip + Money + fund + note + per-line Remove) with an add-line modal (category select / amount / optional fund / optional invoice upload / note) + an itemised-total line; a Remove confirm (ConfirmDialog, posts a reversal); a janaza-draft action (modal + optional note). Funds fetched best-effort for the fund tag (a user without funds access records lines untagged). Legacy lump-sum payment offered only when there are NO itemised lines. 30 new `t()` keys in BOTH locales (messages-extra.ts) + delta `i18n-deltas/bereavement-expenses.json`; zero physical-direction CSS (`ms-auto`, logical borders); RTL-safe; no raw enums on screen (all via `formatLabel`/`StatusChip`).

  **Decisions.** (1) Member-expired uses a shared tx-aware primitive rather than calling `changeStatus` (which opens its own tx) — keeps it atomic with the death record + single-source-of-truth for the history/timeline write. (2) OMJ notify modelled as a NEW tenant-scoped `omj_notifications` queue (RLS) — the OMJ cross-tenant READ side is build-step 49's domain / a future step; here it is the FLAG write + isolation only. (3) Janaza persisted as a `draft`-status `Notification` (new enum value) rather than a bespoke table — reuses the existing model; `draft` is never picked by the dispatch worker (`queued`-only), so no-auto holds. (4) Expense-line CRUD is add + remove-with-reversal (NO edit) — reversal-not-edit (§3.5); editing = remove + re-add. (5) `graveIssuedDate` kept as a nullable column + view field (back-compat) but removed from the DTO + all UI ("stop-using + later drop", spec §2.5); `relationNote` column + display kept, only the form input removed.

  **Gates.** typecheck (6 pkgs) ✅ · lint (3) ✅ · web build ✅ · `prisma validate` ✅ · API tests **1410/1410** / 171 suites ✅ (NEW `bereavement-expenses.isolation.spec.ts` proves nullable `bereavement_amount` + both new enum values + RLS ENABLE+FORCE + per-tenant read/insert(WITH CHECK)/delete isolation + death→lines cascade; extended `bereavement.service.spec` covers expense-line posting/reversal, member-expired+OMJ flag, `markMemberExpired:false` opt-out, janaza draft; extended `funds.service.spec` proves fund expense derives from fund-tagged lines) · i18n parity + web-coverage ✅. Isolation gate REQUIRED + delivered. WORK-TYPE: FEATURE (branch `feat/71-bereavement-expenses-v31`). Ended `[CHECKPOINT]`.

- **Build-step 70 — Accounting COA Surfacing + Funds & Donations** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/70-accounting-coa-funds-v31` (off the staging head after 69); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (surfaces the existing hierarchical chart of accounts in Pro + adds a first-class Funds & Donations subsystem). spec `specs/70-accounting-coa-funds-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/70-75-CODEREF.md`. **Wave 4 / item 1 — the finance foundation 71–75 post into.** tests **1396/1396** (170 suites; **+36** net — 5 NEW specs). **MONEY + SCHEMA — NEW tenant tables `funds`/`donors`/`donations` (RLS ENABLE+FORCE); isolation gate written + green.** Double-entry invariant + Zakat-distinct rule preserved; no parallel money store (fund balance DERIVED).
  - **The problem (spec §1).** The double-entry core was already solid (`Account` hierarchical via `parentId`/`children`, balanced `JournalEntry`/`JournalLine`, vouchers, reconciliation, Simple/Pro). Two gaps: (1) the COA hierarchy was NOT surfaced — Pro read as a flat badge list; (2) no first-class **Funds & Donations** — OMJ runs core funds (Business Aid / Ration Aid / Zakat / General / Donations / Dowry / Educational) money is raised into + spent from, plus member/outsider donations, but welfare's `WelfareFundSource` enum is welfare-internal, not a Khundi-wide fund ledger, and there was no donor record.
  - **A. Surface the hierarchical COA (Pro) — no schema change.** Shared NEW `AccountTreeNode {id,name,type,isDefault,parentId,ownBalance,rolledBalance,children[]}` + pure `buildAccountTree(accounts, balances)` — nests the flat chart by `parentId` and rolls each head's own signed balance (from `computeLedger`) UP to parents (post-order DFS); a `parentId` pointing outside the set — or at the node itself — is treated as a root so nothing is dropped, a `seen` guard makes the roll-up terminate, roots + child lists sorted by name. API: `accounting.service.listAccountTree(tenantId, period)` loads accounts + period entries, runs `computeLedger` → balances map → `buildAccountTree`; `GET /accounting/accounts/tree` (`accounting.view`). Web: the Pro chart-of-accounts section gets a **Tree/Flat** toggle (NEW `coa-tree.tsx` — recursive rows with logical indent `paddingInlineStart`, rolled-up subtotal at parents, "add a head UNDER a parent" picker built from the flattened tree). Simple mode unchanged (cashbook stays flat).
  - **B. Funds & Donations (NEW subsystem).** **Schema (migration `20260715000000_funds_donations`):** `funds` (`id, tenant_id, name, code, kind 'standard'|'custom', zakat, active, account_id?, created_by, ts`; `@@unique([tenant_id, code])`), `donors` (`id, tenant_id, name, contact Json?, is_member, member_id? SetNull, note?, ts`), `donations` (`id, tenant_id, fund_id Cascade, donor_id? SetNull, amount Int, date, method?, note?, journal_entry_id? soft-ref, recorded_by, ts`) — all TENANT DATA with the standard isolation policy (ENABLE+FORCE, `app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()`); `JournalSourceModule += donation` (ALTER TYPE ADD VALUE, not used in same migration's DDL → no add-then-use restriction). **Shared:** `FundKind`+`isFundKind`, `STANDARD_FUNDS` (the OMJ core set, exactly one `zakat:true`) + `STANDARD_FUND_CODES`/`isStandardFundCode`, `FundView`/`DonorView`/`DonationView`, `FundBalance` + pure `fundBalance(movements)` (income − expense, each clamped non-negative + truncated — the ONLY way a balance is computed, no stored total), `FundsSummary` + `summarizeFunds(funds)` (Zakat kept ISOLATED: `zakatBalance` + `nonZakatBalance` never overlap), NEW LABEL_CATALOG `fund_kind` + `donation_method`. **Permissions:** NEW `funds.view`/`funds.manage`/`donations.record` under `MODULES.CORE` (always-on, like `forms.manage`), OWN_TENANT → added to Accountant (full set), President (`funds.view`), General Secretary (`funds.view`+`donations.record`); auto-held by Khundi Super Admin (not in `NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS`). **API:** NEW `funds` module (`FundsModule` imports `AccountingModule` for the posting seam) — `GET/POST /funds`, `PUT /funds/:id` (activate/deactivate), `GET/POST /funds/donors`, `GET/POST /funds/donations`; `ensureStandardFunds` lazy-seeds the OMJ set on first read (idempotent, `skipDuplicates`, like `ensureDefaultChart`); `recordDonation` posts a balanced INCOME entry via the (widened) `postModuleIncomeInTx(... sourceModule:'donation')` IN THE SAME TRANSACTION, then stores the donation with its `journal_entry_id` (so no fund money exists without a posting — AC §5), refuses an inactive/foreign fund; a member donor verifies the member belongs to the Khundi. Fund balance derives from summing the fund's donations (income); expense stays 0 until build-step 71 tags fund-scoped expenses.
  - **Posting + Zakat (spec §3).** Every donation → balanced income entry (credits the `Donations` income head, debits Cash & Bank) — atomic with the donation row. Zakat isolation is enforced at the FUND level (`summarizeFunds` keeps `zakatBalance` separate; the donation narration tags `[Zakat]`); the COA income head stays `Donations` to avoid a fallback-to-default-income mis-route (matches the welfare allocation pattern). No parallel store — a fund's balance is DERIVED on read.
  - **C. Web.** Accounting page gets a NEW **Funds & Donations** tab (`funds-panel.tsx`, self-contained so the big page stays untouched): totals StatCards (Zakat shown on its own line, out of the general total), fund cards (Zakat-distinct border + chip, kind badge, received/spent/available, activate/deactivate), add-custom-fund form, record-donation form (fund + donor + amount + method + note), donor quick-add, and a donations **DataList** (NEW registry key `donations` — date/fund/donor/amount/method/note, Pro adds method+note). Toast + inline messages, RTL/Urdu, human labels (`formatLabel` for `fund_kind`). 50 new `t()` keys in BOTH locales (`messages-extra.ts` EN+UR + NEW delta `i18n-deltas/funds-donations.json`; incl. `col.donor`/`col.note`/`col.donations` for the new DataList headers).
  - **AC check (spec §5).** (1) Pro shows the COA as a manageable tree (create under parent, balances roll up); Simple unchanged ✅; (2) standard OMJ funds seeded, a Khundi adds a custom fund, Zakat flagged + never co-mingled in balances/reports ✅; (3) a donation records + posts a balanced income entry atomically (sets `journal_entry_id`); a fund's balance derives from its donations (no stored running total) ✅; (4) a donor (member or outsider) attributes a donation; member donor links to the member ✅; (5) every fund movement has a balanced journal entry — asserted no donation row without `journal_entry_id` ✅; (6) migration regression + isolation absolute; gates incl. i18n green ✅. Do-NOT-break: double-entry invariant (balance derived, never stored), `postModuleIncomeInTx`/`postModuleExpenseInTx` reused (union widened, not forked), Simple/Pro as a VIEW, welfare `WelfareFundSource` untouched (the new Fund subsystem is the Khundi-wide ledger), reversal-not-edit, voucher numbering — all preserved.
  - **Gates.** API tests **1396/1396** (170 suites; +36 — NEW `funds-shared.spec.ts` (fund maths + Zakat isolation + COA tree rollup/orphan/self-parent), `funds.service.spec.ts` (standard-fund seed idempotent, custom code dedupe, donation posts+links atomically, balance derived, inactive/foreign fund refused, member-donor link + foreign-member refusal, Zakat distinct), `funds.isolation.spec.ts` (RLS — cross-tenant read/insert/update/delete denied, no-context blind, platform sees all), `funds.migration.spec.ts` (3 tables RLS ENABLE+FORCE + policies + unique key + enum `donation` + FK cascade/SetNull), `funds.access.spec.ts` (CORE/OWN_TENANT, isolation, Accountant default)). typecheck (api+web+shared) ✓ · lint ✓ · web `next build` ✓ · `prisma validate` ✓ · i18n parity + web-coverage ✓ · zero physical-direction CSS · RTL/Urdu copy for all 50 new keys.

NEW mappers `censusSnapshotToInstance` (open→active / finalized→archived) and `prizeCeremonyToInstance` (completed→archived else active; `openedAt = opensAt ?? announceAt ?? createdAt`, `finalizedAt = closesAt` when completed). - **Build-step 68 — Polished Census PDF Report (branded cover · inline-SVG charts · Gatta-G sections · RTL/Urdu · presentation view)** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/68-census-report-pdf-v31` (off the 67 head); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (turns the build-step-53 census report into a polished, shareable, presentation-grade document). spec `specs/68-census-report-pdf-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/65-69-CODEREF.md`. tests **1345/1345** (164 suites; **+11** net). **Wave 3 / item 4 — depends on 67.** **Tenant isolation ✅ (read-path)** — NO schema change; the report + branding are both read on the tenant-scoped `runWithTenant` path (RLS), so a Khundi can only ever export its own round + its own branding. `buildCensusReport`/`deriveVulnerability` purity + the derived-not-stored aggregate-only vulnerability rule preserved (no recompute, no names).
  - **The problem (spec §1).** Build-step 53 already produced a `CensusReportView` (pure `buildCensusReport`/`deriveVulnerability`) + an `/report/export` endpoint, but the export was a bare data structure / minimal HTML — not a Gatta-G-quality document the Khundi can present or share. Missing: cover page, branding, charts-as-images, polished layout, and a presentation-grade on-screen view, all RTL/Urdu-correct.
  - **Dependency decision (spec §3, CODEREF — RECORDED).** **Shipped path: a server-rendered, self-contained polished HTML deck that the browser prints to a presentation-grade PDF** (the documented fallback in spec §3). Rationale: (1) no heavy headless renderer (puppeteer/Chromium) is guaranteed to install offline on the ARM VPS; (2) a pure-JS PDF lib (pdfkit / @react-pdf) cannot do correct Urdu **complex-script shaping + RTL** — which is a hard acceptance criterion (AC1/AC4) — whereas the browser's own text engine shapes Urdu correctly when it renders/prints the HTML; (3) zero new dependencies keeps the gates + ARM install clean. **Charts are embedded as inline SVG** (pure, deterministic, generated server-side) so the deck is fully self-contained and prints identically with no chart library. A real binary-PDF endpoint can be layered on later (same pure renderer feeding a headless print) without changing the report core. The web "Download"/"Present" buttons both consume this one deck; Present opens it in its own window (on-screen presentation + the browser's Print → Save-as-PDF).
  - **A. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`) — pure, tested (`apps/api/src/census/census-report.spec.ts`, +11).** NEW `CensusReportBranding {brandName?, logoUrl?, colors?{primary,secondary,accent}}`. NEW `safeColor(value, fallback)` — accepts only `#rgb`/`#rrggbb`, so branding flowing into CSS/SVG can't inject. NEW pure chart helpers: `svgBarChart(items, {color, dir})` — self-contained horizontal-bar SVG, drops zero-value rows, scales to the max, and **mirrors anchors/bar growth for `dir:'rtl'`** so Urdu reads correctly (labels arrive already-localized); `svgDonutChart(items, {centerLabel})` — rotation-symmetric donut + legend (used for the gender split, center = total people), all-zero → ''. `renderCensusReportHtml(report, {locale, branding})` **rewritten** into a polished multi-page deck: a **branded cover page** (logo, brand name in the theme color, round label + localized status, generated date, at-a-glance totals families/people/children/adults/seniors), then per-section cards with inline-SVG charts (Our people = gender donut + age bars; How we live = home-ownership + transport bars; Our children = staged-education in/out + retention table; Our skills & income = education + income bars; What families asked for = needs bars) + the Gatta-G honest findings + the **AGGREGATE-ONLY derived vulnerability COUNT** (never a list/name) + a privacy footer ("Aggregate community report — no individual or CNIC data"). Styling: `@page size:A4`, `page-break-after` per page, **logical-property CSS only** (`padding-inline`/`border-block-end`/`text-align:start` — zero physical-direction), `print-color-adjust:exact`, theme color from branding (default teal `#0d9488`). Backward-compatible signature (branding optional); the existing build-step-53 deck test (EN ltr / UR rtl / `Census 2026` / `مردم شماری`) still passes.
  - **B. - **Build-step 66 — Taxonomy Governance (OMJ standard taxonomy · Khundi locals · review queue: promote/alias/remap)** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/66-taxonomy-governance-v31` (off the 65 head); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (new OMJ-altitude governance over option taxonomies, ARCHITECTURE §32; the build-step-49 "OMJ governs / Khundi consumes" pattern). spec `specs/66-taxonomy-governance-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/65-69-CODEREF.md`. tests **1320/1320** (163 suites; **+35** net). **Wave 3 / item 2 — depends on 65; foundation for 67 (census governed-domain fields) + 68/69 aggregation.** **Tenant isolation ✅ + OMJ-scope test ✅** — NEW tenant table `taxonomy_local` (RLS ENABLE+FORCE, tenant FK Cascade) + NEW global reference table `taxonomy_standard` (NO tenant_id, NO RLS, like `permissions`/`module_registry`); the ONLY cross-Khundi path is the OMJ review queue on the audited platform path, permission-gated `taxonomy.govern` @ ALL_TENANTS.
  - **The problem (spec §1).** Option sets are per-Khundi, so "education"/"occupation"/"income_band"/"relationship" values diverge across Khundis ("MBBS" vs "Doctor" vs "doctor") — OMJ-wide aggregation is noisy. The fix governs a taxonomy WITHOUT blocking a Khundi or editing any submission: OMJ owns a STANDARD list per domain; a Khundi adds a LOCAL value INSTANTLY (no approval to USE); every local surfaces to an OMJ REVIEW QUEUE where OMJ can PROMOTE (make standard), MERGE-ALIAS (point at an existing standard) or RE-MAP it — a read-time mapping the aggregation applies, never an edit of stored answers.
  - **Data-model decision (spec §3 / CODEREF — "fold mapping into local").** TWO tables, not three: `taxonomy_standard` (global reference: `domain, value, label, order, active`; unique `(domain,value)`) + `taxonomy_local` (tenant data: `tenant_id, domain, value, label, status('local'|'promoted'|'aliased'|'remapped'), mapped_standard_value?, mapping_kind?('alias'|'remap'), created_by, decided_by, decided_at`; unique `(tenant_id,domain,value)`). The OMJ mapping is FOLDED into `taxonomy_local` so the only RLS surface is one tenant table — simpler + isolation-absolute. Migration `20260714000000_taxonomy_governance`.
  - **A. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** `TAXONOMY_DOMAINS` (education/occupation/income_band/relationship) + `isGovernedTaxonomyDomain`; `TAXONOMY_LOCAL_STATUSES` + `TAXONOMY_MAPPING_KINDS`; views `TaxonomyStandardView`/`TaxonomyLocalView`/`TaxonomyDomainView`/`TaxonomyReviewItem`; `TAXONOMY_STANDARD_SEED` (code-seeded canonical lists, 8/9/5/11 values per domain). NEW pure, tested helpers: `resolveTaxonomyValue(value, locals)` (a decided local→its standard; un-decided/standard→itself — read-time, never edits submissions); `applyTaxonomyMapping(values, locals)` (aggregation roll-up — aliased/remapped fold under standard); `buildTaxonomyOptions(standard, locals)` (option-editor merge: active-standard-first, non-promoted locals, de-duped so a promoted local never doubles); `validateTaxonomyMapping(local, target, standard)` (rejects self-ref/unknown/inactive before any write). NEW permissions `taxonomy.contribute` (CORE, OWN_TENANT) + `taxonomy.govern` (OVERSIGHT, ALL_TENANTS — added to `NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS`). Label catalog += `taxonomy_domain`/`taxonomy_status`/`taxonomy_mapping_kind`/`taxonomy_option_origin` (EN/UR). `nav.taxonomy`/`nav.taxonomyGov` (EN/UR core catalog).
  - **B. Prisma + migration (`20260714000000_taxonomy_governance`).** `taxonomy_standard` CREATE — global reference, NO tenant_id, NO RLS. `taxonomy_local` CREATE — `tenant_id` FK `ON DELETE CASCADE`, RLS `ENABLE` + `FORCE` with the docs/MULTITENANCY.md isolation policy (`app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()`). `Tenant.taxonomyLocals` back-relation. Seed `seedTaxonomyStandard()` upserts `TAXONOMY_STANDARD_SEED` (idempotent, global).
  - **C. API (`apps/api/src/taxonomy/`).** `taxonomy.service.ts` — KHUNDI path (`runWithTenant`, RLS): `listDomain` (standard+own locals), `addLocal` (label-only; value auto-slugged via `slugifyFieldKey`; rejects standard-collision; idempotent on re-add; usable immediately). OMJ path (`runAsPlatform`, RLS bypass, gated `taxonomy.govern`): `reviewQueue` (pending locals across Khundis + tenant labels), `listStandard` (target picker), `promote` (upserts a standard row + stamps local promoted→self), `mapLocal` (validated alias/remap; records mapping + `decided_by`/`decided_at`). All audited (`Logger('Audit')`). `taxonomy.controller.ts` — `TaxonomyController` (`/taxonomy/*`, OWN_TENANT `taxonomy.contribute`) + `TaxonomyPlatformController` (`/platform/taxonomy/*`, ALL_TENANTS `taxonomy.govern`). `taxonomy.dto.ts` (`AddLocalDto` label-only — client can never set value/status/tenant; `MapLocalDto`), `taxonomy.mapper.ts`, `taxonomy.module.ts` (registered in `app.module.ts`). OMJ Admin seed role += `taxonomy.govern`; President/Gen-Sec/Councilor tenant roles += `taxonomy.contribute`.
  - **D. Web.** OMJ governance screen `apps/web/app/platform/taxonomy/page.tsx` (review queue; per-item Promote + standard-value picker + Merge/Re-map; toasts; gated `taxonomy.govern`). Khundi taxonomy panel `apps/web/app/taxonomy/page.tsx` (per-domain standard+local via `buildTaxonomyOptions`; add-a-local usable immediately; status chips; gated `taxonomy.contribute`). Nav entries: `/taxonomy` (Operations, `taxonomy.contribute`) + `/platform/taxonomy` (Platform & OMJ, `taxonomy.govern`). All labels via `formatLabel`; zero physical-direction Tailwind.
  - **Acceptance (spec §6):** (1) a Khundi adds a local + uses it immediately, no approval gate ✅. (2) the local surfaces in OMJ's queue; OMJ promotes/aliases/remaps; decision recorded; submissions never edited ✅. (3) aggregation rolls aliased/remapped locals under their standard while the Khundi keeps its local label ✅ (`applyTaxonomyMapping`/`resolveTaxonomyValue` pure+tested; census/insights/report wiring over governed domains lands with 67's governed-domain census fields). (4) standard = OMJ reference (no tenant_id); locals+mapping tenant-isolated; no Khundi reads another's locals; OMJ reads across via its altitude scope only ✅. (5) migration regression + isolation absolute; OMJ-scope is the only cross-path and is permission-gated ✅. (6) gates green incl. isolation + OMJ-scope permission test + i18n ✅.
  - **Scope note (option-editor binding).** Spec §4 / CODEREF call for the build-step-65 INLINE field option editor to read `taxonomy_standard`+`taxonomy_local` for a field bound to a governed domain. A FormField has no `taxonomyDomain` binding yet — that binding is introduced with the **build-step-67 census redesign** (Gatta-G census fields adopt governed domains, per CODEREF 67). This step ships the full governance backbone (shared contract + API + data model + both web surfaces: a dedicated Khundi taxonomy panel satisfying "Khundi sees standard+local + adds a usable local", and the OMJ governance screen); the per-field option-editor wiring lands in 67 where the domain-bound fields exist. The aggregation helpers (`applyTaxonomyMapping`) are shipped+tested so 67/68 apply them directly.
  - **Gates:** typecheck ✅ (shared/api/web), lint ✅ (api no warnings, web no errors), web build ✅ (both new routes `/taxonomy` + `/platform/taxonomy` static), prisma validate ✅, API tests **1320/1320** (163 suites) ✅ incl. i18n en⇔ur parity + web-coverage (35 new t-keys both locales + delta `i18n-deltas/taxonomy-governance.json`). NEW specs: `taxonomy-helpers.spec.ts`, `taxonomy.migration.spec.ts` (standard NO-RLS, local RLS ENABLE+FORCE, no tenant_id on standard, unique keys, cascade — real migration chain on PGlite), `taxonomy.isolation.spec.ts` (cross-tenant read/update/delete denied, no-context deny-by-default, platform path sees all, standard readable from any context), `taxonomy.access.spec.ts` (**OMJ-scope test** — `taxonomy.govern` ALL_TENANTS-only + in NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS + on OMJ seed role), `taxonomy.service.spec.ts` (add/idempotent/collision/ungoverned-reject/queue-spans-Khundis/promote/alias-validate/NotFound). **Isolation ✅ + OMJ-scope permission test ✅.**

- **Build-step 65 — Advanced Form Builder (inline options · auto-slug · new field types · conditional logic)** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/65-form-builder-advanced-v31` (off the staging head after 64); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (extends the build-step-20 form engine, ARCHITECTURE §32). spec `specs/65-form-builder-advanced-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/65-69-CODEREF.md`. tests **1285/1285** (158 suites; **+23** net). **Wave 3 / item 1 — foundation for 66 (taxonomy) + 67 (census).** **Tenant isolation ✅** — additive enum extension + one `form_fields` ADD COLUMN; new migration regression proves enum values added (no data loss), `visibility` column nullable JSONB, form-builder RLS preserved (ENABLE+FORCE), and a visibility rule is tenant-isolated (foreign tenant cannot read/write).
  - **What shipped (the 5 gaps in spec §1):** (1) **inline options** — an admin types choices right on a choice field; the engine creates/updates the field's `OptionSet` transparently (admin never meets "OptionSet"). (2) **auto-slug / no keys shown** — the builder is label-first; `slugifyFieldKey(label)` derives the machine key server-side (collision-suffixed, Urdu→stable hash fallback) and the key is NEVER shown. (3) **no raw enums** — field-type + operator pickers route through `formatLabel` (new `form_field_type` rows + new `visibility_op` domain, EN/UR). (4) **new field types** — `radio` (single-choice buttons), `checkbox` (multi-checkbox group), `member` (member picker → stores a member id), `searchable` (typeahead single-select). (5) **conditional/cascading logic** — a field shows only when its `visibility` rule passes; multi-level cascades resolve (a hidden parent's answer counts as unanswered).
  - **A. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** `FormFieldType` union + `FORM_FIELD_TYPES` += the four types; helpers `fieldTypeUsesOptions`/`fieldTypeIsMulti`. NEW pure, tested helpers: `slugifyFieldKey(label, taken)`; `FieldVisibility`/`VisibilityRule`/`VisibilityOp` + `VISIBILITY_OPS`; `evaluateFieldVisibility(field, answers)` + `visibleFields(fields, answers)` (fixpoint cascade resolution, bounded by field count); `validateVisibilityRefs(fields)` (unknown-ref / self-ref / bad-op / **cycle** via DFS colour map). `FormFieldView` += `visibility`. **`validateSubmission` now shares ONE evaluator with the web renderer** — a field hidden by its rule is neither required nor validated; the type switch groups `select|radio|searchable` (single choice) + `multiselect|checkbox` (multi) and adds `member` (non-blank id). Label catalog += 4 `form_field_type` rows + a `visibility_op` domain (both locales).
  - **B. Prisma + migration (`20260713000000_form_builder_advanced`).** `enum FormFieldType` += `radio|checkbox|member|searchable` (`ALTER TYPE … ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS` — purely additive, no rewrite). `form_fields` += nullable `visibility Json?` (ADD COLUMN — the `form_fields_isolation` RLS policy is untouched; NULL = always-shown, no backfill / no data loss).
  - **C. API (`apps/api/src/forms/`).** `forms.dto.ts`: `FieldInputDto.key` is now OPTIONAL (server derives), + inline `options`/`optionStyle`/`allowOther` + `visibility` (nested `FieldVisibilityDto`/`VisibilityRuleDto`, `value` whitelisted via `@Allow()`). `forms.service.ts` `replaceFields` resolves each field's key (explicit kept stable; keyless → `slugifyFieldKey` collision-suffixed), validates `validateVisibilityRefs` (rejects cycles/unknown refs **before** any write), upserts inline option sets via a new in-tx `upsertInlineOptionSet`, and persists `visibility`; `cloneDefinition` copies `visibility`. `forms-mapper.ts` returns `visibility`. Locked-core protection, non-destructive versioning, and `@@unique([formDefinitionId, key])` all preserved.
  - **D. Web.** `apps/web/app/forms/page.tsx` — a label-first `<FieldEditor>` (no machine key shown), human type picker (`FORM_FIELD_TYPES`), inline choice rows (admin types choice LABELS; value auto-slugged) + "Allow Other" toggle, and a Pro conditional-logic editor ("Show this field only when … [field] [op] [value]", add-rule, all/any; refs limited to already-keyed fields). `apps/web/app/census/census-form.tsx` (the canonical multi-step renderer) now evaluates `visibleFields` live (cascades hide downstream fields, drop their answers, exclude from required-checks) and renders the four new types (`member`→`<MemberPicker>`, `searchable`→`<SearchSelect>`, `radio`→button group, `checkbox`/`multiselect`→checklist). Prize/welfare/sharia keep their fixed surfaces but inherit the shared server-side evaluator + new-type validation.
  - **Acceptance (spec §5):** (1) admin builds typing labels only; keys auto-derive + stay unique; locked-core keys immutable ✅. (2) inline options create/update the OptionSet transparently; Other toggle works ✅. (3) radio/checkbox/member/searchable render + store; member→id; searchable typeaheads ✅. (4) conditional logic shows/hides live; multi-level cascades resolve; hidden field not required + ignored server-side; cycles rejected ✅. (5) web render + server validation share ONE evaluator ✅. (6) migration regression: enum extended, no data loss, RLS preserved, isolation absolute ✅. (7) gates green incl. isolation + i18n + web-coverage ✅.
  - **Decision noted:** the spec floated "`forbidNonWhitelisted` rejects a client-set key". Chosen instead: `key` is OPTIONAL on the DTO (server always derives for keyless fields; an explicit key is honored only to keep an EXISTING field's key stable so its option-set/visibility refs don't break on relabel). This satisfies acceptance #1 (admin never sees/types keys; keys auto-derive + stay unique; locked-core immutable) while keeping refs and the `@@unique` contract intact. New-field references in a condition require saving the draft once (a brand-new field has no stable key yet) — surfaced as a builder hint, not an error.
  - **Gates:** typecheck ✅ (shared/api/web), lint ✅ (api, no warnings), web build ✅ (all routes), API tests **1285/1285** ✅ (i18n en⇔ur parity + web-coverage green — `form_field_type` sweep now covers the 4 new types in both locales). NEW specs: `forms-helpers.spec.ts` (slugify, evaluate/visibleFields cascade, validateVisibilityRefs cycle/ref, validateSubmission honours visibility + new types), `forms.service.spec.ts` (auto-slug uniqueness, inline option upsert, visibility persist, cycle reject), NEW `form-builder-advanced.migration.spec.ts` (enum/column/RLS/isolation on the real migration chain). Zero physical-direction Tailwind; no new i18n `t()` keys (builder uses existing literal/`formatLabel` pattern). **Isolation ✅ (enum + field-meta on the RLS-FORCEd form-builder tables).**

- **Build-step 64 — Family-Tree Fix (marriage lens + two-lineage no-doubling)** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/64-family-tree-fix-v31` (off the staging head after 63); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (corrects the shipped build-step-45 family tree). spec `specs/64-family-tree-fix-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/61-64-CODEREF.md`. tests **1262/1262** (157 suites; **+6** net — all in `family-tree.spec.ts`). **Wave 2 / item 4 — closes Wave 2 (61–64).** **Tenant isolation ➖ (not required) — read-path/render fix ONLY: NO schema/Prisma/migration/RLS/`tenant_id`/permission-key/auth/endpoint/module change; `getFamily` still runs inside `runWithTenant` (RLS unchanged) and the de-dupe is a pure post-process on already-tenant-scoped data.**
  - **The two defects fixed (C-family-tree):** (1) under the **By-Marriage lens** the couple's **children** did not render (children were shown under `birth`/`both` only), so the marriage lens showed the spouse but never the family unit; (2) **two-lineage doubling** — a member reached through BOTH lineages (a cousin marriage: a spouse who is also a blood relative) could render as TWO cards.
  - **A. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** Pure helpers (one source of truth for API + web + tests): `childVisibleUnderLens(lens, hasSpouseLink)` — a child is a BIRTH relation so it always shows under `birth`/`both`; under `marriage` it shows ONLY when the other parent is present (`hasSpouseLink`), so the child renders beneath the couple. NEW `dedupeFamilyTree(view): FamilyTreeView` — keeps the focal (the pivot) always, then drops from every other band any ref whose id was already placed in a higher-priority band (source order: ancestors father→mother→grandparents → spouses → siblings → children), so an overlapping member keeps its most-structural placement and the **marriage slot wins over siblings/children** (preserves the end-marriage affordance + Married-In chip). Pure + idempotent. `FamilyTreeView` shape UNCHANGED (band layout preserved — no view-shape break).
  - **B. API (`apps/api/src/members/family.service.ts`).** `getFamily` builds the band view exactly as before (spouse slot already OPEN-SPOUSE_OF-only from build-step 61 — divorced links never show under the live lens) then `return dedupeFamilyTree(view)` — the API now returns a de-duped view so a two-lineage member surfaces ONCE. The "other parent" for children is the focal's open spouse, already resolved in `spouses` (so the web renders children under the couple without any new view field). `runWithTenant`/RLS, `toMemberRef`/`MemberRef`, the household overlay (`loadTreeHouseholds`), the paternal/maternal pivot, and the `husbandFacts` attached-fact node all untouched.
  - **C. Web (`apps/web/app/members/family-tree.tsx`).** Renamed the prop to `rawTree` and `const tree = useMemo(() => dedupeFamilyTree(rawTree), [rawTree])` — de-dupes by member id at layout (idempotent belt-and-braces over the API; guards stale/partial data) so **no card renders twice**. Children band now gated by `showChildren = childVisibleUnderLens(lens, hasSpouseLink) && tree.children.length > 0`, where `hasSpouseLink = tree.spouses.length > 0 || tree.husbandFacts != null` — so By-Marriage now shows the focal + open spouse(s) + their children as a unit (incl. when the other parent is the attached non-Okhai-husband fact); By-Birth = bloodline; By-Both = all (build-step-45 chips). Modal/focused view, household overlay + legend, click-to-refocus, RTL all preserved. **No new i18n keys** (reuses existing `members.*`/`genChildren`), so no dual-write needed.
  - **D. Tests (`apps/api/src/members/family-tree.spec.ts`, +6).** `childVisibleUnderLens` — always-children under birth/both; marriage shows children only with a spouse link. `dedupeFamilyTree` — a member that is BOTH an open spouse AND a blood sibling is kept once (in the marriage slot, dropped from siblings); focal never dropped + non-overlapping bands intact; idempotent. `FamilyService.getFamily` end-to-end — a fake-tx focal with SPOUSE_OF + SIBLING_OF to the SAME member returns the cousin once (in `spouses`, `siblings` empty), proving the wiring. The build-step-45 lens-classifier + household-overlay tests stay green.
  - **Acceptance:** (1) By-Marriage shows the focal's open marriage(s) WITH the couple's children beneath; By-Birth bloodline; By-Both all ✅. (2) a two-lineage member renders exactly once ✅. (3) a divorced (closed) marriage stays out of the open lens (build-step 61) — unchanged ✅. (4) build-step-45 behaviours (modal tree, household overlay, refocus, RTL, human labels) intact ✅. (5) gates green + family-tree spec extended ✅.
  - **Gates:** typecheck (all workspaces) ✅ + web build ✅ + lint ✅ (api eslint + web next-lint, no warnings) + api tests **1262/1262** ✅ + i18n parity + web-coverage GREEN (no new keys) + zero physical-direction Tailwind (RTL-safe). Shared rebuilt (`dist/`). Isolation ➖ (read-path only — reason above).

- **Build-step 60 — Mode-gating fix + Labels/Urdu pass + Hygiene** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode; presentation + authz-metadata-assertion only, NO schema/Prisma/migration/RLS/`tenant_id`/auth/permission-key/endpoint/module change).** branch `feat/60-mode-labels-hygiene-v31` (off `staging` head after 59); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (corrects shipped mode-gating behaviour + repo hygiene). spec `specs/60-mode-labels-hygiene-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/54-60-CODEREF.md`. tests **1216/1216** (150 suites; **+3** from the new permission-gate spec). **Closes Wave 1 (54–60).** **Tenant isolation ➖** — no data access path touched; instead the step's REQUIRED gate is an explicit **PERMISSION** assertion (below).

Removed the now-unused `useMode('settings')` import + `isPro`. A Simple-capped admin therefore still sees + uses every admin tab. (Each section ALSO gates internally via `useEffectiveAccess` + `<AccessRequired>`, so this is defence-in-depth, not the only gate.)

All bind a resolved URL. The one field NAMED like a ref — `certificate backgroundRef` — only ever holds a `publicUrl`: `file-upload.tsx` computes `ref = presign.publicUrl ?? presign.key` but calls `onChange(ref)` ONLY when `servable = Boolean(presign.publicUrl)`, so a bare storage key never reaches state/DB; the canvas + print paths therefore always render a URL. - **Build-step 59 — Modal submit shortcut + keyboard/ESC scoping** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode; presentation/keyboard only, NO schema/Prisma/migration/RLS/`tenant_id`/auth/permission-key/endpoint/module change).** branch `feat/59-modal-keyboard-v31` (off `staging` head after 58); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (completes the build-step-39 `<Modal>` primitive — spec header declares FIX; branch keeps the spec's `feat/59-…` name). spec `specs/59-modal-keyboard-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/54-60-CODEREF.md`. tests **1213/1213** (149 suites; no new api test — the change is web React with no web test harness, matching the build-step-58 precedent where only the shared pure logic was unit-tested; correctness covered by typecheck+build+the existing suite). **Tenant isolation ➖** (keyboard/overlay behaviour only; no data access path touched).
  - **NEW `apps/web/app/lib/hotkeys.ts` (the rush-time substrate, reused by build-step 72 attendance roll-call):** `useHotkeys(map, opts)` binds combo→handler on a target (default `window`), cleans up on unmount, and skips a bare single-key combo while the user is typing in an input/textarea/contenteditable UNLESS a command modifier is held (so type-to-find + single-key toggles coexist). Pure, DOM-light, exported helpers: `parseHotkey` (`'mod+enter'`→tokens; `mod` = Cmd OR Ctrl; aliases esc/enter/space/arrows/del), `matchesHotkey(combo, eventLike)`, `hasCommandModifier`, `isTypingTarget`. `useEscapeDismiss(active, onEscape)` — the ESC-scoping helper for custom dropdowns.
  - **`<Modal>`/`<Drawer>` (`ui/modal.tsx`): opt-in `onSubmitShortcut?: () => void`.** Threaded through `OverlayShell` → `useFocusTrap`; the existing capture-phase keydown handler now fires it on `Enter` **with** `metaKey||ctrlKey` (preventDefault+stopPropagation), so Cmd/Ctrl+Enter saves while **plain** Enter is never intercepted (textarea newlines + native form submit intact). Held in a ref so a fresh handler each render doesn't re-bind the trap (no focus-restore thrash). Build-step-39 ESC/focus-trap/Tab-wrap/scroll-lock/`dismissible`/drawer-slide all unchanged.
  - **ESC scoping (the core fix, C19):** `<SearchSelect>`/`<MultiSearchSelect>` (`search-select.tsx` `useDismiss`), `<MemberPicker>`, `<DateField>`, and `<ColumnsControl>` now close their own popover via `useEscapeDismiss` — a **window**-CAPTURE keydown listener that calls `stopPropagation()` + closes. Rationale (documented in `hotkeys.ts`): the modal traps ESC with a **document**-CAPTURE listener; the capture phase walks `window → document → … → target`, so a window-capture listener fires BEFORE the modal's document-capture one and stops the event from ever reaching it. Result: ESC with a dropdown open closes only the dropdown (modal stays); a second ESC (dropdown gone, its listener removed) reaches the modal and closes it. (Replaces the document-bubble `stopPropagation` columns-control shipped in 55, which couldn't actually preempt a document-capture listener.) Outside-click `mousedown` handlers left on `document` as before.
  - **Shortcut wiring (so acceptance #2 is live, not just opt-in):** `<ConfirmDialog>` (`onSubmitShortcut={busy?undefined:onConfirm}`); welfare (open-case / allocate / inquiry), events (create / minutes), prize (ceremony / application / recognition), roles editor — each `onSubmitShortcut` mirrors the `<ModalFooter>` primary action and is guarded by the same `busy`/required-field condition as `confirmDisabled`. Members form modal: NEW optional `submitRef` prop on `<MemberForm>` exposes `() => formRef.current?.requestSubmit()` (the same `formRef` from `useFieldErrors`), so the modal's Cmd/Ctrl+Enter runs the form's full validation path even from a textarea; page wires `onSubmitShortcut={busy?undefined:() => memberSubmitRef.current?.()}`.
  - **i18n:** none added (no new user-facing strings); both gates already green.
  - **Gates:** typecheck ✅, lint ✅ (no warnings), web build ✅ (all routes), api tests **1213/1213** ✅. Zero physical-direction Tailwind classes added; no `t()` keys added (web-coverage gate unaffected).

  - **Shared (`@kc/shared`, PURE + tested):** an in-house **E.164 phone library** (no npm phone lib added — couldn't be guaranteed to install offline, so a minimal layer, documented in the source): `PHONE_COUNTRIES` curated dial-code table (PK first, + Gulf/diaspora/East-Africa; locale-neutral flag emoji so the selector needs no translated country names), `DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY='PK'`, `isValidE164` (strict `^\+[1-9]\d{7,14}$`), `normalizePhoneE164(raw, defaultCountry='PK')` (forgiving on input: `+…`/`00…` keep the embedded code, otherwise national → drop a trunk `0` + prepend the selected country's dial code), `parsePhoneE164` (split a valid E.164 back to country+national, longest-dial-code-wins). **CNIC mask** `formatCnicMask` (`#####-#######-#`, presentation only — reuses build-step-48 `normalizeCnic`/`isValidCnic`/`CNIC_FULLY_MASKED`, no fork). **OMJ card** `normalizeOmjCard` (uppercase + drop whitespace), `isValidOmjCard` (`^OMJ-[A-Z0-9]+-\d{3,}$` — the seed shape `OMJ-<KHUNDI CODE>-<serial>`; variable-length code so no rigid positional mask, only normalize + shape check), `formatOmjCardMask` (uppercase + strip spaces as typed).
  - **Web primitives:** NEW `apps/web/app/ui/masked-input.tsx` (`<MaskedInput>` generic + `<CnicInput>`/`<OmjCardInput>` thin wrappers — controlled, re-formats through the shared pure formatter each keystroke; `onChange` emits the formatted string, the form/server still normalizes before storage). NEW `apps/web/app/ui/phone-input.tsx` (`<PhoneInput>` — country `<Select>` (flag + ISO + dial code, default PK) + national `<Input dir="ltr">`; emits E.164 once valid, raw national digits while incomplete so the parent can flag it on blur, '' when cleared; re-hydrates from an externally-changed value via a `lastEmitted` ref without clobbering typing; row uses logical `flex gap-2`, number always LTR — RTL-correct).
  - **Rollout (client side of the two-level validation):** `members/member-form.tsx` — cell/landline/whatsapp → `<PhoneInput>` (with inline `members.phoneInvalid` errors via the build-step-57 `useFieldErrors` pattern, submit gated), CNIC + husband-CNIC → `<CnicInput>`, OMJ card → `<OmjCardInput>`; `me/page.tsx` contact phone → `<PhoneInput>`; `settings/sections/providers-section.tsx` provider test number → `<PhoneInput>`. (Notifications bulk-manual-recipients box stays free text — it accepts a comma/newline LIST; each recipient is validated server-side on send.)
  - **Server (the other level — ONE shared rule, never two regexes):** NEW `apps/api/src/common/dto-validators.ts` — class-validator decorators `@IsPhoneE164`/`@NormalizePhone`, `@IsOmjCard`/`@NormalizeOmjCard`, `@IsCnic`, each DELEGATING to the shared pure function (the `@Normalize*` transform coerces national/legacy input to the canonical form, then the validator strictly checks; all treat empty as valid to compose with `@IsOptional`). Wired into `members.dto.ts` (`MemberContactDto` cell/landline/whatsapp; create+update `omjCardNumber`, `cnic`, `husbandCnic`) and `notifications.dto.ts` (`TestSendDto.phone`, `RecipientDto.phone`). `emergency` stays free text (often "name — number"). CNIC encrypt already stores the trimmed value while the dedup token normalizes, so the masked (dashed) form is safe; the global `ValidationPipe` already runs `transform:true`.

- **Current build-step:** **56 — Dynamic filter engine** 🟢 **complete — `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode; presentation + read, NO schema/RLS/permission change).** branch `feat/56-filter-engine-v31` (off `staging` head after 54+55); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (new shared subsystem, reused by the audience builder at build-step 78). spec `specs/56-filter-engine-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/54-60-CODEREF.md`. tests **1199/1199** (148 suites; +17 from the new `apps/api/src/ui/filter-engine.spec.ts`). **Tenant isolation ➖** (no data-model change; the server path only NARROWS within the existing tenant-scoped list endpoint — a filter param can never widen beyond the tenant since RLS + the endpoint's where-clause bound it).
  - **What shipped (spec 56):** a reusable, framework-agnostic **filter engine** in `@kc/shared` + a web **`<FilterBar>`** integrated into `<DataList>`, with **auto client-vs-server by row-count** and **debounced** text search. The filter STATE is the serializable `FilterState` (`Record<field, FilterValue>`) — the SAME shape the custom audience builder (build-step 78) will persist as a segment.
  - **Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`, after `resolveListView`):** new types `FilterType` (`select|multiselect|boolean|numberRange|dateRange|text`), `FilterOption`, `FilterSpec` (`field/label/type/options?/labelDomain?`), `ListFilterConfig` (`listKey/filters/clientRowCap?`, default cap `DEFAULT_CLIENT_ROW_CAP = 500`), `FilterRange`, `FilterDateRange`, `FilterValue`, `FilterState`. PURE helpers: `isActiveFilterValue`, `activeFilterCount`, `normalizeForMatch` (lowercase/trim/collapse-ws), `applyFilters(rows, config, state, accessor)` (AND across active fields; fuzzy text = normalized substring; select exact; multiselect membership; boolean true/false; numberRange + dateRange inclusive bounds; ISO dates compared on the date part so a `…THH:mm` value still falls inside a `yyyy-mm-dd` bound), `filtersToQuery(state)` / `queryToFilters(query, config)` (round-trip serialization: string→`field`, array→`field=v1,v2`, boolean→`field=true|false`, range→`field_min`/`field_max`, date→`field_from`/`field_to`; empty/inactive omitted), `shouldFilterServerSide(config, total)` (`total > cap`).
  - **Web — NEW `apps/web/app/ui/filter-bar.tsx`:** collapsible "Filters (N)" accordion; one control per `FilterSpec` (text → 300ms-debounced `<Input>`; select → `<SearchSelect>`; multiselect → `<MultiSearchSelect>`; boolean → `<CheckboxRow>` "only X"; numberRange → two number `<Input>`s; dateRange → two `<DateField>`s). Active filters always render as removable chips + "Clear all" (even when collapsed). Option labels route through `formatLabel` when `labelDomain` is set (no raw enum). Logical CSS only; RTL-ready.
  - **Web — `apps/web/app/ui/data-list.tsx`:** new props `filterConfig?`, `getFilterValue?(row,field)`, `onServerFilter?(query)`, `totalRowCount?`. Internal `filterState`; `serverSide = shouldFilterServerSide(config, totalRowCount ?? rows.length)`. Client path applies `applyFilters` inside the existing `filtered` memo (after the free-text search, so they compose); server path fires a guarded effect (callback held in a ref; keyed on the serialized query) that calls `onServerFilter`. Export still exports the FILTERED set. A list with no `filterConfig` behaves exactly as before.
  - **Consumer demo — `apps/web/app/members/page.tsx`:** replaced the hand-rolled "Filters" Card with a `memberFilterConfig` (gender `select`+`labelDomain:'gender'`, status `select`+`labelDomain:'member_status'`, votingOnly `boolean`) driving the `<FilterBar>`. `getMemberFilterValue` maps fields → row values for the client path; `onMemberServerFilter` mirrors the serialized query into the existing `?gender&status&votingOnly` fetch state (which the members API already filters by) — so above `clientRowCap` the **server genuinely receives the filter query** (acceptance #2), and at/below it the roster filters in-memory. The derived **age band** stays a separate client-side `<Select>` (passed via the DataList `toolbar` slot) since it's a bucket on `age`, not a server param.
  - **i18n:** new `filters.*` keys (filters/clearAll/any/min/max/from/to/searchPlaceholder) authored in BOTH locales in `packages/shared/src/messages-extra.ts` (`_EN`/`_UR`) + `packages/shared/i18n-deltas/filters.json`. Boolean chip shows just the filter label (no new yes/no key); reuses `common.remove`. Both i18n gates green (`i18n.spec.ts` parity + `i18n-web-coverage.spec.ts`).

- **(history) build-step 46 — Storage rework: Google Drive backend + per-Khundi quota + auto-compression** ✅ **complete — `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` (hard; changes the file-storage backend + adds a new tenant-DATA table + quota enforcement → manual approve)** — branch `feat/46-storage-drive-quota` (off `feat/45-family-tree`); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (Drive backend + quota + compression are NEW capability; extends `StorageService` = the FIX half); spec `specs/46-storage-drive-quota.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`. **DATA-MODEL CHANGE (migration `20260703000000_storage_quota_v2`, additive/non-destructive):** NEW tenant-DATA table **`storage_objects`** (the scope-agnostic usage LEDGER — one row per stored object across every upload scope; `ENABLE+FORCE` RLS `app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id=app_current_tenant_id()`, UNIQUE `(tenant_id, storage_key)`, FK→tenants CASCADE), plus nullable `tenants.storage_quota_mb` (per-Khundi cap override; NULL→default) + nullable `documents.original_size` (pre-compression bytes). **NO new permission-key / NO auth change** — reuses `settings.manage`@OWN_TENANT (tenant cap), `crossKhundi.view`@ALL_TENANTS (OMJ read) + `tenant.manage`@PLATFORM (OMJ cap write). **The `StorageService` CONTRACT is stable** (presign/publicUrl unchanged for R2) so the step-39 `<FileUpload>` + step-30 doc refs are untouched. **Five parts:** **(1) ENV-selectable backend** — NEW `backends.ts`: `StorageBackend` interface + `R2Backend` (existing presign logic extracted, behaviour-identical), `GoogleDriveBackend` (service-account JWT via `node:crypto` RS256 + Drive REST via fetch, one folder per Khundi, uploads/downloads PROXIED through the API since Drive has no S3 presign), `DevBackend` (placeholder URLs), `createStorageBackend(read)` selects by `STORAGE_BACKEND` (`r2`|`gdrive`|`dev`; default r2; unknown→r2). Every backend DEV-falls-back when its creds are unset (parity with R2's existing posture). `.env.example` gains `STORAGE_BACKEND` + `GDRIVE_CLIENT_EMAIL`/`GDRIVE_PRIVATE_KEY`/`GDRIVE_ROOT_FOLDER_ID`. **(2) Per-Khundi quota** — NEW `StorageQuotaService` (RLS-scoped): used-bytes = `SUM(storage_objects.byteSize)` (computed → no running-total drift; a delete removes the row), cap = `tenants.storage_quota_mb ?? DEFAULT_STORAGE_QUOTA_MB` (500). `recordObject` is idempotent on the key + does the quota check + write in ONE transaction on the DELTA (a replace never counts an object's old size against itself); `assertWithinQuota` enforces on presign (declared size, UX) + commit (stored size, authoritative); `removeObject` reclaims on delete. NEW shared (`@kc/shared`): `DEFAULT_STORAGE_QUOTA_MB`, `MB`, `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`, `mbToBytes`/`bytesToMb`/`effectiveQuotaMb`/`wouldExceedQuota`, `storageUsageView`, `StorageBackendKind`, `StorageUsageView`, `TenantStorageUsage`. **(3) Auto-compression** — server owns the POLICY (`compressionPlanFor` → processable JPEG/PNG/WebP re-encode to WebP, cap 1600px, q0.82; SVG/GIF/PDF/non-images stored as-is) + the GUARD (`MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`) + the ACCOUNTING (`original_size` vs stored `byteSize`); because the upload is presigned DIRECT-to-storage (and the build env has no native image codec), the actual re-encode runs CLIENT-side in `<FileUpload>` via `<canvas>` (downscale + re-encode, only kept if smaller), reporting the post-compression size to the server — documented split, the same `compressionPlanFor` policy can drive a future server-side codec on the proxied Drive path without a contract change. **(4) Surfaces** — `POST /storage/commit` (record stored size, idempotent), `GET /storage/usage`, `PATCH /storage/quota` (`settings.manage`, audited), `DELETE /storage/object` (reclaim), the Drive `PUT|GET /storage/proxy` byte-proxy (key re-checked in-tenant), + NEW `StoragePlatformController` (`GET /platform/storage/usage` `crossKhundi.view`@ALL_TENANTS, `PATCH /platform/storage/:tenantId/quota` `tenant.manage`@PLATFORM, both `runAsPlatform`). **Web:** Settings → Storage tab is now a real `<StorageSection>` (used/total bar, backend label, compression note, admin cap setter); the OMJ "Tenants & Modules" page gains a `<StorageCaps>` panel (per-Khundi usage + cap set); `<FileUpload>`/`<ImageUpload>` optimize→commit→reclaim (over-quota 403 → `StorageQuotaError` hint, blob reclaimed). The vault's document create/delete now record/decrement the ledger (server-side, the canonical decrement). Storage plumbing paths (`storage/upload-url`, `storage/commit`, `storage/proxy`) added to `AUDIT_SUPPRESSED_PATHS` (high-frequency churn; the meaningful `documents.upload` + `storage.set_quota` stay audited). **(5) Proof** — Gates: typecheck ✅ (shared/api/web 6/6), lint ✅ (web + api, no warnings), web build ✅ (all 33 routes; `/settings` 11.9 kB, `/platform/tenants` 4.42 kB), tests **1076/1076** ✅ (1057 + 19 NEW: `storage.isolation.spec.ts` ×8 — RLS read/insert-WITH-CHECK/delete isolation on `storage_objects`, per-Khundi SUM, replace-by-DELTA no-double-count, cap invisible cross-tenant, platform grouped usage; `storage-policy.spec.ts` ×11 — compression plan processable/as-is, quota math + boundary, usage view, backend selection + DEV fallback + live R2 presign + Drive proxy). i18n: en⇔ur parity + web-coverage gates GREEN (NEW `settings.storage*`/`upload.overQuota`+`optimizing`/`platform.storage*` keys authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` + `i18n-deltas/{common-ui,platform}.json`). Zero physical-direction Tailwind classes (logical `inlineSize`). **NOTE:** no live DB/Drive/staging in the build env — the abstraction + quota + compression policy + tenant isolation are proven on unit specs + the green `storage.isolation.spec.ts` (real migration SQL on PGlite as a non-superuser role); the GoogleDrive live path + the Drive proxy are STRUCTURED + DEV-fallback-safe and operator-exercised on staging (spec §38 allows proving via backend selection + DEV fallback). **Known best-effort (documented):** a member-photo/certificate REPLACE across a page reload can orphan a ledger row (client `committedKey` ref is per-mount; document delete decrements correctly server-side) — usage is recomputable from the ledger; the OMJ recompute/reconcile is future. **Operator runs the staging deploy + live screenshots** (an image upload stores a compressed, dimension-reduced version — stored < original; the ref is opaque/no raw URL; used-bytes increments + a delete decrements; an over-quota upload refused with the human message; Settings → Storage shows used/total + backend; `STORAGE_BACKEND` switch r2↔gdrive; cross-tenant file read blocked) per the spec before promotion. **✅ `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` — APPROVED (operator instruction, 2026-06-26)** (storage backend + new tenant-DATA table + quota enforcement = production-affecting). ⏭️ NEXT after approve: build-step 47 — Bereavement as its own module (spec `specs/47-*.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`). **End of v3-A.**

(4) **prize category** — hard-delete if unused, else ARCHIVE; (5) **prize gift** — always a clean hard-delete (assignments copy the label as free text, no FK); (6) **prize certificate template** — hard-delete if unused, REFUSE while a ceremony links it; (7) **event** — hard-delete a draft/scheduled one with no RSVPs, REFUSE a completed event or one with RSVP/attendance (archive instead); recorded spend stays in accounting regardless (no event FK); (8) **census snapshot** — hard-delete only an empty, still-open round, REFUSE a finalized one or one with submissions; (9) **document** — hard-delete the metadata row (non-financial; blob lifecycle owned by §46). **EDIT (reuses the step-39 create modals, pre-filled, permission-gated):** events (PATCH), welfare cases (PATCH, pre-disbursement fields only — backend already restricts to open/under-inquiry), prize ceremonies (PATCH), notification templates (PUT, edit-in-place author form). Khundi family / sub-group / group code are read from the tenant, never on the member. Adds the husband-side fact block for a female married to a NON-Okhai husband (KhundiConnect registers her; the OMJ Lawazim software does not). This is a schema + RLS rewrite over the existing `members`/`relationships` tables — migrate carefully, preserve all RLS, and re-run every isolation + voting-eligibility gate. Built build-step 17 — **Audit, backups, i18n/Urdu polish, accessibility (ARCHITECTURE.md §7.11, §17, §4 i18n, §13.2, §27#17)**. **Prisma:** 1 new table — `audit_log` (the immutable §7.11 audit log: nullable `tenant_id` [null = a platform-level action], `actor_user_id` [no FK — the log outlives a user], `actor_altitude` enum vendor/omj/tenant, `action`, `target_type`/`target_id`, sanitised `metadata` JSON, `at`) + enum `ActorAltitude` — hand-authored migration `20260617000000_audit`. **RLS is APPEND-ONLY** (the key property): unlike the §-template's one FOR-ALL policy, `audit_log` carries ENABLE+FORCE + **only a SELECT policy and an INSERT policy** — with no UPDATE/DELETE policy, those commands match nothing and are denied even to the table owner, so a row once written can NEVER be edited or erased (§7.11 "immutable"). Otherwise standard isolation (tenant reads/inserts own rows; platform path reads/writes all incl. null-tenant rows; deny-by-default). `tenant_id` SET NULL on tenant delete (the trail survives, detached). **`@kc/shared`:** the audit + i18n contracts as PURE FUNCTIONS — `sanitizeAuditMetadata` (the §17 structural guarantee — any value under a sensitive key [password/token/otp/apiKey/cnic/secret/…] → `[redacted]`, recursively; strings length-capped, objects depth/breadth-capped — so a secret/PII can NEVER reach an audit row), `summarizeAuditAction` (method+route → a stable namespaced action, dropping uuid/numeric/`:param` id segments), `AUDIT_SENSITIVE_KEYS` + `AuditLogView`/`AuditPage`/`AuditActorAltitude` types; PLUS the i18n layer — `Locale`/`LOCALES`/`isRtlLocale`/`dirForLocale`/`normalizeLocale`/`LOCALE_NAMES`, the EN/UR `MESSAGES` catalog + `translate` (en→key fallback chain), `MESSAGE_KEYS`; added `audit.view` to the PERMISSIONS catalog (CORE). **NestJS `AuditModule`:** `AuditService` (record = path-aware [tenant → `runWithTenant`, platform → `runAsPlatform`] + re-sanitises metadata + **NON-throwing** so auditing can never break the audited action + only ever APPENDS one row, never mutates domain data; listForTenant [RLS] + listAll [platform path]); a GLOBAL `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) — the cross-cutting "audit hook" that records ONE row for every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE across EVERY module with no per-module wiring, capturing actor/action/target/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params — **never the request body**, so no credential/OTP/CNIC is ever stored); two read surfaces — `AuditController` (`/audit`, `audit.view` OWN_TENANT, RLS read — a Khundi's own trail) + `PlatformAuditController` (`/platform/audit`, `audit.view` ALL_TENANTS — OMJ/Vendor cross-tenant oversight on the audited platform path). **New permission key `audit.view` (CORE)** — OWN_TENANT for a Khundi (added to President; Super Admin auto-holds), ALL_TENANTS for OMJ (added to OMJ Admin), PLATFORM for the Vendor (all-keys); NOT in `NON_TENANT_KEYS` (a tenant sees its OWN trail). **Web:** `/audit` (the Khundi's audit trail — action icons, actor/target/time, localized, RTL-ready) + a real **i18n layer** (`app/i18n.tsx` — a client `I18nProvider` that holds the locale, persists it, and flips `<html lang/dir>` at runtime so Urdu renders FULLY right-to-left with no reload; `LanguageToggle` EN/اردو; home localized) + **accessibility** (globals.css: visible `:focus-visible`, a skip-to-content link, large touch targets, `prefers-reduced-motion`, Nastaliq face for RTL; semantic landmarks/aria). **Backups:** `scripts/backup.sh` (pg_dump → gzipped timestamped dump + retention prune; non-destructive, no secrets, no fence-blocked strings; `bash -n` clean) + cron/restore/retention runbook. **Docs:** `docs/AUDIT.md`, `docs/BACKUPS.md`, `docs/I18N.md`, `docs/ACCESSIBILITY.md`. **Env:** NO new required env (backups read optional `KC_BACKUP_DIR`/`KC_BACKUP_RETENTION_DAYS`). **Seed:** a handful of immutable demo audit rows per tenant + platform-level rows; `reset.ts` clears `audit_log`.
