Card QR (`buildCardQrPayload`, shared) = `KC|{subdomain}|{omjCardNumber|NA}|{cardId}` — OMJ card number + ids only, NEVER a CNIC/secret (§2.4/§17), derived server-side on issue. `welfare_disbursements.journal_entry_id` is an optional NON-FK link — the welfare→accounting auto-post is DEFERRED (like the §18 lawazim→accounting auto-post) so AccountingService stays green. Deferred (noted in decisions): member self-apply/registration via the §22 PWA, PDF card printing + QR camera scanner UI, full per-request enforcement of the document `access_roles` row filter on reads (the field + `canViewDocument` helper + gate ship now). **Prior build-step 17 (now APPROVED):** **Build-step 17 essentials:** `audit_log` is the §7.11 immutable log — TENANT DATA on the §-template RLS BUT **append-only** (only SELECT+INSERT policies, NO UPDATE/DELETE → a row can never be edited/erased even by its owner tenant; proven by isolation + migration specs). `tenant_id` nullable (null = platform-level action) + SET NULL on tenant delete (trail survives detached). Rows are written by a GLOBAL `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) on every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE — **no per-module wiring** (existing module service specs untouched, all still green); it stores actor/action/target/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params — **NEVER the request body**, so no secret/CNIC/OTP is captured). `AuditService.record` is path-aware (tenant→`runWithTenant`, platform→`runAsPlatform`), re-sanitises metadata, and is NON-throwing (auditing can't break the audited action). New key `audit.view` (CORE): tenant `/audit` OWN_TENANT (President + Super Admin), cross-tenant `/platform/audit` ALL_TENANTS (OMJ Admin) / PLATFORM (Vendor). `sanitizeAuditMetadata` (shared, pure) redacts any value under a sensitive key (defense in depth). **i18n is now real, not just "RTL-ready":** `@kc/shared` `MESSAGES` EN/UR catalog + `translate` (en→key fallback) + `isRtlLocale`/`dirForLocale`; web `app/i18n.tsx` `I18nProvider` flips `<html lang/dir>` at runtime (Urdu = full RTL, no reload) + `LanguageToggle`. Accessibility baseline in `globals.css` (focus-visible, skip link, large targets, reduced-motion, Nastaliq RTL face). Backups = `scripts/backup.sh` (pg_dump + retention prune; non-destructive; `bash -n` clean) + `docs/BACKUPS.md` runbook. After editing shared, rebuild `@kc/shared` before jest/typecheck/build (done). **Deferred (noted):** wiring RICH per-action audit hooks into individual services (the global interceptor already covers all mutations; explicit `AuditService.record` calls with richer metadata are an incremental follow-on); impersonation banner/`tenant.impersonate` flow (auth-touching, build-step 18-adjacent); PDF/Excel report export; off-box backup sync wiring; per-string Urdu coverage of every deep page (the layer + a representative set ship now). **Build-step 16 reuses the build-step-13 reporting APIs:** the OMJ oversight UI (`/platform/oversight`) consumes `GET /reports/jamat` (`crossKhundi.view` ALL_TENANTS) and the Vendor analytics UI (`/platform/analytics`) consumes `GET /reports/platform` (`tenant.manage` PLATFORM) — both cross-tenant on the audited `runAsPlatform` path, NO per-tenant module gate (mirrors provisioning). The only API change is a **read-only** extension of `getPlatformDashboard` to also sum each tenant's (RLS-isolated) `subscriptions`+`payments` for §20 revenue, reusing the build-step-15 `toPaymentView`/`summarizeBilling`. New shared pure fns: `summarizePlatformRevenue` (never nets collected vs outstanding; reuses `summarizeBilling` per tenant) + `censusHeatBand` (5-band heatmap classifier). **Deferred (noted in decisions):** impersonation (`tenant.impersonate` — auth-touching, a focused later step), graveyard-records view (Phase-2 `death_records`, build-step 18), a dedicated OMJ Jamat-AI-insights panel, PDF/Excel export. **Billing model:** `subscription_plans` is GLOBAL reference data (no RLS, like `permissions`); `subscriptions` + `payments` are tenant DATA (RLS, one subscription per tenant, plan FK RESTRICT, payment→subscription FK SET NULL). Money is whole-rupee Int (PKR). New keys `billing.view` (OWN_TENANT) + `billing.manage` (PLATFORM Vendor duty, in `NON_TENANT_KEYS`, ≠ tenant.manage). **White-label adds NO column** — branding is `tenants.branding` JSON + `tenants.custom_domain`; `effectiveBranding` APPLIES it ONLY when the `whitelabel` module flag is ON (else KhundiConnect defaults, retained-but-not-applied, §15.3); `GET /tenants/current` honours this. `sanitizeBranding` whitelists the §15.2 safe subset (logo/brandName/hex colors/tagline) — re-sanitized on save. `/settings/branding` is module-gated (paid → reachable; off → 404 whole surface). Seed: whitelabel ON for jafrani-b (branding applies), OFF for toberiya-a/kath-a (demo of the paid gate). Module-toggle UI (`/platform/tenants`) is the build-step 5 one (unchanged) — build-step 15 added billing + branding around it. **Member portal `/me/*` is IDENTITY-gated, not permission-gated:** the service resolves the member from the AUTHENTICATED card (`user.omjCardNumber`) vs the resolved-host tenant on `runWithTenant`, so a card holder reaches only their OWN record (a non-member card → 404); `@RequireModule('portal')` still gates it (default-open). The admin `/portal/*` queue is dual-gated (`portal.requests`/`portal.suggestions`). **§22 SAFE-FIELD rule is structural:** `sanitizeProfileChanges` whitelists name/dob/education/occupation/income/contact and DROPS status/card/CNIC/member-type/gender — a member can never self-edit a constitutional field; the set is re-sanitized again at approval time. A profile change is applied to the member ONLY on an explicit admin approve (§3.5). The PWA service worker NEVER caches `/api/*` (member data + auth must stay fresh + session-scoped on a shared phone). Demo: sign in as `OMJ-JAF-0002` (OTP-only) on jafrani-b → `/me`. **Reports add NO table/migration:** they DERIVE dashboards from members/lawazim/accounting/census via the SAME shared pure functions those modules use (one source of truth — `MembersService.demographics` now also delegates to the shared `computeMemberDemographics`). The Khundi altitude reads on `runWithTenant` (RLS-isolated); the OMJ (`crossKhundi.view` ALL_TENANTS) + Vendor (`tenant.manage` PLATFORM) altitudes read on the audited `runAsPlatform` path and have NO per-tenant module gate (mirrors Vendor provisioning). The rich OMJ/Vendor dashboard UIs land with build-step 16; build-step 13 shipped the full Khundi dashboard UI + all three altitude APIs + CSV exports. After editing shared, rebuild `@kc/shared` before jest/typecheck/build (done). **AI generator SIMULATES insights unless `AI_LIVE=on`** and **messaging dispatcher SIMULATES sends unless `MESSAGING_LIVE=on`** (both optional env, default off) — so dev/staging/seed/gates never hit a provider, send PII, or bill anyone; live wiring flips the env on with real per-owner keys. **AI privacy (§11.6) is structural:** insights are built ONLY from anonymized aggregate counts (`aggregateMembersForInsight` drops names/CNIC) + `assertAnonymized` is a runtime backstop before any real provider call. **ai_insights RLS is a DELIBERATE widening** of the §-template — a tenant reads its own KHUNDI rows PLUS shared JAMAT rows (`tenant_id IS NULL`), gated on a tenant context (no-context still sees nothing); writes are own-KHUNDI-only (JAMAT rows are bypass-path only). After editing the schema, **rebuild `@kc/shared` (`npm run build -w @kc/shared`) before running jest** — jest maps `@kc/shared` to its SOURCE for tests, but typecheck/build resolve the built `dist/index.d.ts`, so rebuild shared before typecheck/build when you add shared exports. PGlite UUID literals must be **hex-only** (0-9a-f) — `s`/`n` etc. are invalid. Gate infra notes: isolation + migration gates use **PGlite** (in-process Postgres/WASM, no Docker/superuser); jest needs `NODE_OPTIONS=--experimental-vm-modules` (wired into the api `test` script). Service tests use pure-function fixtures + a fake transaction client, so no live services are needed (the accounting fake must set `entryId` on nested-created journal lines so the include join resolves). After editing the schema run `npm run prisma:generate` from `apps/api` before typecheck/build (set a dummy `DATABASE_URL` for `prisma validate`/`generate`). **`nest build` gotcha: `incremental:true` + `deleteOutDir` means a leftover `*.tsbuildinfo` makes tsc skip emit after dist is wiped (exit 0, empty dist) — `rm -f *.tsbuildinfo` before a clean build to verify; the turbo `npm run build` from root is the canonical build gate (it reported 3 successful).** NOTE: a stray `*/` inside a Prisma `///` doc comment will corrupt the generated client's `.d.ts` — keep doc comments clean. NOTE: `prisma/*.ts` (seed/reset) is outside the `src/**` typecheck scope and runs via `ts-node --transpile-only`; type-check it manually after edits.

Operator directive: deepen all flagged modules + add 3 subsystems BEFORE production promotion. Target: a working staging demo of the full depth to show the team. | confirmed (operator) |
| 2026-06-24 | Member classification fully derived | `member_type` enum + `is_honorary` flag REMOVED. Stored inputs only: gender, dob, is_okhai_by_birth, omj_card_number, status, marital_residence. Voting-eligible/honorary/child/non-member-okhai/pending-18 all derived on read. Khundi/Group-code removed from member (read from tenant). | confirmed |
| 2026-06-24 | Female married to non-Okhai husband | KhundiConnect registers her (OMJ Lawazim software does not). She stays an honorary member of her FATHER's Khundi (tenant) with `marital_residence=married_out`. Husband-side facts captured as attached facts (name, father, grandfather, CNIC, community/biradari, surname, community-membership-no) — never a Khundi/Group code. | confirmed |
| 2026-06-24 | Shared Form-Builder engine (step 20) | One engine powers Census + Prize (+ future). Option B customization: Khundi can't remove locked-core fields but authors own option sets (light: Below/Average/Above; or detailed: ranges/lists, +Other) and adds unlimited custom fields. Income band UNLOCKED/optional. Custom fields never enter cross-Khundi aggregation/Jamat-AI; OMJ still sees all per-Khundi. | confirmed |

| 2026-06-06 | `audit_log` is append-only at the DB (immutable) | Per §7.11 "immutable", `audit_log` carries ENABLE+FORCE RLS with ONLY a SELECT policy + an INSERT policy — no UPDATE/DELETE policy, so those commands match nothing and are denied even to the table-owner application role. A row, once written, can never be edited or erased. Proven by `audit.isolation.spec` (owner UPDATE/DELETE affects 0 rows) + `audit.migration.spec` (`pg_policies` shows only SELECT+INSERT). `reset.ts` clears it on the bypass path for dev re-seeding only. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | `audit_log.tenant_id` is nullable + SET NULL on tenant delete | A platform-level action (Vendor provisioning, OMJ cross-tenant read) has no single Khundi, so `tenant_id` is null (the §-template policy `tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()` excludes null rows from a tenant session — a Khundi never sees platform-level audit; only the bypass path does). On tenant delete the FK SET NULLs so the trail SURVIVES (detached, platform-path-only) rather than being erased — an immutable log shouldn't vanish with a tenant. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | Audit is captured by a GLOBAL interceptor, not per-module hooks | `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) records ONE row for every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE across EVERY module — the §22 cross-cutting "audit hook" with NO per-module wiring (existing module services + their specs are untouched, all 521 still green). It stores actor/action(method+route)/target(`:id` or created id)/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params) and **NEVER the request body**, so no credential/OTP/CNIC is captured (§17). Richer per-action explicit `AuditService.record` calls are an incremental follow-on. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | Interceptor altitude approximation | The interceptor sets `actor_altitude` = `tenant` when a tenant context is resolved, else `vendor` (platform host). OMJ users also operate at the platform host, so an OMJ action is recorded as `vendor` by the auto-hook; precise OMJ attribution comes from explicit `AuditService.record` calls (which take an explicit altitude) and the seeded demo rows. Acceptable for the cross-cutting default. | confirm (approximation) |
| 2026-06-06 | New key `audit.view` (CORE); tenant OWN + cross-tenant ALL_TENANTS | Added ONE permission key `audit.view` (CORE backbone, like `billing.view`). Tenant `/audit` requires OWN_TENANT (a Khundi sees its own trail — NOT in `NON_TENANT_KEYS`; added to President, Super Admin auto-holds); cross-tenant `/platform/audit` requires ALL_TENANTS (OMJ Admin holds it) and a Vendor PLATFORM grant satisfies it too. Mirrors the §13.3 oversight reporting routes. | confirm new key |
| 2026-06-06 | `sanitizeAuditMetadata` is the structural secrets guarantee | Any value under a sensitive key (password/pass/secret/token/otp/auth/credential/apiKey/api_key/key/cnic/cipher/encrypted — substring, case-insensitive) → `[redacted]`, recursively; strings/objects/arrays are length/depth/breadth-capped. Applied in the interceptor AND re-applied in `AuditService.record` (defense in depth). So §17/principle-#7 "no secret/PII in logs" holds by construction, not convention. Proven by `audit-helpers.spec` + `audit.service.spec`. | confirm reading |

| — | ORM | Prisma (per §4 recommendation) | no |
| 2026-06-05 | AI generation simulates unless `AI_LIVE=on` | The `InsightGenerator` only makes a real OpenAI/Claude HTTP call when the optional `AI_LIVE` env = `on`; otherwise it SIMULATES (returns a deterministic offline insight from the same aggregate via `simulateInsight`, no network). Mirrors `MESSAGING_LIVE`/the OMJ scheduler, so dev/staging/seed/gates never call a provider, send PII, or cost anyone. Flip on with a real, intended per-owner key. | confirm (default-simulate) |
| 2026-06-05 | AI privacy is structural (§11.6) | Insights are built ONLY from `aggregateMembersForInsight` (counts, never names/CNIC) → `buildInsightPrompt` references only the aggregate. `assertAnonymized` is a runtime backstop the generator calls before EVERY real provider request (throws on a CNIC/phone pattern). So the §11.6 "aggregate/anonymize before any LLM, never CNIC/identifying detail" duty holds by construction, not convention. Proven by helpers + service specs. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | `ai_insights` RLS widened for cross-altitude visibility | Unlike the standard §-template, `ai_insights` READ = own KHUNDI rows OR shared JAMAT rows (`tenant_id IS NULL`) — but the JAMAT clause requires a tenant context so a no-context session still sees nothing (deny-by-default). WRITE (FOR ALL) = own KHUNDI only; a tenant can never forge/modify a JAMAT row or a rival's (WITH CHECK). This implements §11.3 (Jamat insights shared downward, anonymized; never sideways). `ai_config` keeps the plain §-template (Khundi never sees OMJ's key). | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | AI Insights permission duty split | No new keys/module — the catalog already has `insights.{view,generate}` + `ai_key.manage` + module `insights`. Mapped per §11.5: `view`=read config + cached insights, `ai_key.manage`=integrate the provider (provider/model/enabled + the SECRET key), `generate`=spend/generate. Setting provider/model/enabled maps to `ai_key.manage` (managing the AI integration — there is no separate "insights.config" key). Added `insights.view`+`insights.generate` to **President**, `insights.view` to **General Secretary**; Super Admin already holds all three. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | This step ships the Khundi (tenant) AI flow; OMJ/Vendor generation UI deferred | Per §11 the data model + RLS + adapter support all three altitudes, but build-step 12 builds the tenant generate+view flow end to end. Vendor/OMJ JAMAT generation is DEMONSTRATED in the seed (an OMJ-owned config + a shared JAMAT insight on the platform path) and reachable via the bypass path; its oversight UI lands with build-step 16 (mirrors how notifications shipped only the tenant piece). | confirm (defer OMJ UI) |
| 2026-06-05 | AI config = encrypted key + non-secret provider/model | The per-owner provider API key is stored as ONE AES-256-GCM ciphertext via the SAME `CnicCipherService` cipher, decrypted only in-memory at generate time, never returned (`AiConfigView.hasApiKey` only) or logged. `provider`/`model`/`enabled` are non-secret and shown in the UI. Default models per provider live in the adapters (`gpt-4o-mini` / `claude-sonnet-4-6`), overridable per config. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Messaging simulates unless `MESSAGING_LIVE=on` | The dispatcher only makes real Twilio/Infobip HTTP calls when the optional `MESSAGING_LIVE` env = `on`; otherwise it SIMULATES delivery (records sends as delivered without touching the network). Mirrors the OMJ scheduler's self-disable, so dev/staging/the seed/the gates never bill a tenant or message a real person. Flip on with real, intended per-tenant credentials. | confirm (default-simulate) |
| 2026-06-05 | Notifications uses BullMQ-free synchronous send | §4 lists BullMQ for notification sending; built a direct dispatch (the adapter is called inline, fan-out per recipient) so the gates need no live Redis worker. ALL provider logic is in the `MessagingDispatcher`/adapters, so a BullMQ worker can wrap `send()` later with no logic change. Bulk sizes are small (a Khundi's roster, §10). | confirm (vs BullMQ now) |
| 2026-06-05 | Notification permission duty split | No new keys/module — the catalog already has `notifications.{view,send,config}` + `messaging_key.manage` + module `notifications`. Mapped: `view`=read config + comm log, `send`=compose+send, `config`=set provider/sender/enabled, `messaging_key.manage`=set the SECRET provider credentials (separate, write-only — mirrors `ai_key.manage`). Added `notifications.config` + `messaging_key.manage` to the **General Secretary** default role (the §9 "notifications" owner); Super Admin already holds all. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Provider credentials = encrypted JSON blob | The per-tenant Twilio/Infobip credentials are stored as ONE AES-256-GCM-encrypted JSON string (e.g. Twilio `{accountSid,authToken}` / Infobip `{apiKey,baseUrl}`) via the SAME `CnicCipherService` cipher, decrypted only in-memory at send time. Never returned (`MessagingConfigView.hasCredentials` only) or logged (§17). `from_label` (sender id/number) is non-secret and shown in the UI. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Comm log recipients stored as JSON | `notifications.recipients` is a JSON array of `{memberId?, name?, phone}`; counts (`recipient_count`/`sent_count`/`failed_count`) + `status` are stored alongside for fast log reads. A member is never messaged twice in one send (`normalizeRecipients` dedups by phone). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Seed records log rows, never sends | The seed writes per-tenant messaging config (encrypted demo credentials) + 4 historical comm-log rows directly (a record of past sends); it NEVER calls the dispatcher, so no message is ever sent during seeding. Demo credentials are non-functional and would be simulated anyway. | confirm (demo) |
| 2026-06-05 | One double-entry engine (no "simple" data model) | Per §18, EVERY transaction — simple cashbook or detailed journal — is stored as balanced `journal_lines`. `accounting_settings.mode` is a VIEW flag only; `setMode` upserts that row and never reads/rewrites journal data (proven non-destructive by `accounting.service.spec`). The engine refuses any unbalanced/both-sided/zero entry. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Cash side = a default "Cash & Bank" asset account | The double-entry cash side uses a seeded `isDefault` ASSET head ("Cash & Bank"); a line may also carry `bank_account_id` to attribute the movement to a physical bank. The cashbook = the asset-line ledger (debit=in, credit=out); opening balance = Σ `bank_accounts.opening_balance`. Keeps simple-mode auto-assignment unambiguous. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | Default chart auto-provisioned (default-open) | A tenant's default chart of accounts is auto-created on first accounting access (idempotent) AND seeded explicitly for the demo tenants. Mirrors the build-step 5 "module default = open" stance — a freshly-provisioned Khundi can use accounting immediately. Added an "OMJ Lawazim Remittance" expense head (beyond the §7.6 list) so the §2.5 bulk remittance posts to a clearly-separate head. | confirm (default-open + extra head) |
| 2026-06-05 | Accounting permission duty split | No new keys/module — the catalog already has `accounting.{view,entry,mode,banks,reports}` + module `accounting`. Mapped: `view`=read books, `entry`=record (simple/detailed) + add custom heads, `mode`=switch simple/detailed, `banks`=manage bank accounts, `reports`=ledger/financial summary. Account-head creation maps to `entry`. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Lawazim→accounting live auto-posting deferred | §18 describes lawazim posting income/remittance entries into accounting. To keep the build-step boundary clean and build-step 9 GREEN, LawazimService is left untouched (no live auto-post wired). The integration is DEMONSTRATED in the seed (this-year payments post as income, the OMJ remittance as a separate expense — never netted, §2.5) and the shared posting maths exist; live wiring is a small follow-on. | confirm (defer live wiring) |
| 2026-06-05 | `journal_lines` carries `tenant_id` | Like `member_status_history`, the child `journal_lines` gets its own `tenant_id` + RLS for isolation parity (no tenant-DATA table without RLS), beyond reaching it via the parent entry. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Jafrani-B detailed, others simple (seed) | §31.3 asks for one tenant in each accounting mode; seeded Jafrani-B in DETAILED and Toberiya-A/Kath-A in SIMPLE so both interfaces are demoable on real data. Demo bank opening balance Rs 50000. | confirm (demo) |
| 2026-06-05 | Lawazim liability = voting eligibility | The §2.5 fee is "per 18+ male member". `isLawazimLiable` DELEGATES to `isVotingEligible` (active ∧ male ∧ 18+ ∧ memberType=member) so the fee population and the constitutional voting population can never drift apart; named separately so a future divergence (e.g. should an honorary ever owe) is a one-line change. Derived on read, never stored. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Two independent ledgers, no money movement | The Khundi fee (income, `lawazim_payments`) and the OMJ fee (expense, `omj_remittances`) are SEPARATE. `summarizeLawazimYear` computes `collected` and `omj.remitted` from disjoint inputs and NEVER nets one against the other; the service records each independently. This is the §2.5 "NO AUTO-DEDUCTION / NO AUTO-TRANSFER" rule, asserted by `lawazim.service.spec`. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Khundi fee Rs 1500 / OMJ fee Rs 100 (seed) | Seeded the §2.5 example figures (Jafrani-B Khundi fee Rs 1500/yr; OMJ fee the fixed Rs 100/yr default). Real per-tenant fees are set via the UI; these are demo values only. | confirm (demo figures) |
| 2026-06-05 | Amounts stored as whole-rupee Int | PKR fees/payments/remittances are stored as integer rupees (no decimals/paisa) — matches the §2.5 examples, avoids float rounding, keeps the cashbook exact. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | Partial payments allowed; status derived | A member may have many payments per year; standing (paid/partial/unpaid) is DERIVED by summing them vs the Khundi fee — no stored "paid" flag. Over-payment still reads `paid`; a since-removed member's payment is retained (SET NULL) and counts as income but not against any member's debt. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | Fee-config set = `lawazim.record` | Setting the per-year fee config is mapped to the existing `lawazim.record` permission (an admin/accountant act), keeping it out of view-only roles without adding a new key. The OMJ remittance uses the separate `lawazim.remit` duty. No new permission keys/module — `lawazim.{view,record,remit}` + module `lawazim` were already in the catalog + default roles. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Census reuses the build-step 6 family tree | §10.2's person-centric family tree is already built (members + relationships, rendered on `/members`). Build-step 8 does NOT rebuild it; census adds snapshots + the §10.5 economic/welfare fields + approval/progress on top, and reads the existing tree. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Census permission duty split | No new permission keys/module needed — the catalog already has `census.{view,enter,approve,finalize}` + module `census`. Mapped: `view`=read, `enter`=submit (crowdsourced), `approve`=approve/reject, `finalize`=snapshot lifecycle (open + freeze). So opening a census needs `census.finalize` (President/Super Admin), separating it from day-to-day entry/approval. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Only APPROVED entries count | `summarizeCensusEntries` + the completion % count ONLY `approved` entries (§10.3 "on approval → counts in demographics"); pending/rejected never skew the roll-up. A submission is always created `pending` (never auto-approved), and finalising a snapshot freezes it WITHOUT auto-approving the remainder (§3.5). | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | One entry per member per snapshot | A member has at most one entry per snapshot (a partial unique index where `member_id IS NOT NULL`); a re-submission UPDATES that row and RESETS it to `pending` (re-approval required) rather than stacking duplicates or silently keeping a stale approval. New-person entries (`member_id` null) may be many. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Below-living-wage = none/below_15k | The §10.5 below-living-wage flag is DERIVED from `incomeBand` (`isBelowLivingWage`), with the at/under-line bands = `none` + `below_15k` (coarse PKR bands `none`/`below_15k`/`15k_30k`/`30k_60k`/`above_60k`). Chosen for low-literacy entry; exact figures are never stored. | confirm bands |
| 2026-06-05 | Census progress denominator | Completion % = distinct members with an APPROVED entry ÷ total roster members. The whole roster is the denominator (simple + defensible); new-person submissions are surfaced separately and don't change the denominator. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | OMJ sync is a Khundi (tenant) feature | §22 lists "OMJ Data Sync" under **Khundi Tenant Feature Areas**, so `omj_api_config` + `fetch_conflicts` are TENANT DATA (tenant_id + §-template RLS) and the queue is per-Khundi. Each Khundi configures its own key and reviews its own conflicts; OMJ-altitude cross-tenant oversight is a later step. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Cron = internal timer, not BullMQ | §4 lists BullMQ; built a dependency-free, self-rescheduling daily timer (02:00 UTC, `unref`'d, self-disables under tests/no-endpoint) so the gates need no live Redis worker. ALL per-tenant-resilient logic is in `runDailySyncAllTenants()` (what the tests exercise), so a BullMQ worker can replace the trigger later with no logic change. | confirm (vs BullMQ now) |
| 2026-06-05 | CNIC matching via in-memory decrypt | CNIC is stored AES-GCM (random IV) so it can't be equality-matched in SQL. The reconcile loads the tenant's members, **decrypts CNICs in memory** (Khundis are small, §10) to build the match index; plaintext never leaves the server / is never logged. Blind-index column deferred (not needed at this scale). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Conflict dedup, not stacking | A re-fetch UPDATES the existing PENDING `fetch_conflicts` row for the same person (keyed on `local_member_id` for a conflict, else on `match_value`=cnic‖card for a `new`) rather than inserting a duplicate (§7.4). `unchanged` records are never queued. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Partial feed never wipes data | `diffIncoming` counts an OPTIONAL field as "changed" only when the OMJ record actually provides a value; `merge` likewise only overwrites fields the feed provides. A sparse feed therefore can't blank out data the Khundi holds (a silent overwrite by omission). STATUS is never changed by a merge (no silent suspend). | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Resolve semantics | `accept` is valid only for a `new` record (creates a member, provenance `omj_fetch`); `merge` only for a matched `conflict` (updates the local member's identity/demographics); `reject` always valid (no member change). Wrong resolution for the type → clean 400. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | API key encryption | The per-tenant OMJ API key is encrypted at rest with the SAME AES-256-GCM field cipher as CNICs (`CnicCipherService`, key from `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, now exported from MembersModule). Never returned (`OmjConfigView.hasApiKey` only) or logged. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `omj_sync` is a toggleable module | Added module key `omj_sync` (auto-included in `PROVISIONABLE_MODULES`) + keys `omj_sync.{view,config,fetch,resolve}`. Granted to Super Admin (all), General Secretary (all four), Councilor (view/fetch/resolve). | confirm new keys |
| 2026-06-05 | Voting eligibility includes `memberType=member` | §2.3's literal formula is "active ∧ male ∧ 18+". Built `isVotingEligible` as active ∧ male ∧ 18+ ∧ **memberType=member**, because §2.3 also says a `child` (even a male who turned 18) must be human-confirmed before counting and a `non_member_okhai` is "not a member". So a pending child/non-member is excluded until promoted. Computed on read (age-dependent), never stored. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Male child ≥18 → `pendingVotingActivation` flag | Derived signal (male ∧ child ∧ active ∧ ≥18) surfaced for human confirmation; the platform NEVER auto-promotes child→member or auto-counts them (§2.3, AGENT.md §3.5). Admin promotes via a normal member edit. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Tenant cannot set `suspended` | Suspension is constitutionally OMJ-altitude (§2.3; `members.suspend` is in `NON_TENANT_KEYS`). The tenant `PATCH /members/:id/status` endpoint refuses `suspended`; the OMJ oversight suspend flow lands in its own build-step. Tenants manage active/inactive/expired. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | `member_status_history` carries `tenant_id` | §7.3 sketches it without one; added `tenant_id` + the RLS template for isolation parity (no tenant-DATA table without RLS). `changed_by` is a bare actor UUID (no FK), mirroring `user_roles.assigned_by`. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Family edges stored BOTH ways | Each relationship writes the edge AND its inverse (PARENT_OF↔CHILD_OF, SPOUSE_OF/SIBLING_OF symmetric) so the navigable tree (§10.2) resolves from any focal person with one "edges where from=focal" query; add/remove keep the pair in sync; unique `(tenant,from,to,type)`. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | CNIC encryption | A member's CNIC is encrypted at rest with **AES-256-GCM** (`CnicCipherService`), key = SHA-256 of the existing `ENCRYPTION_KEY` placeholder (now REQUIRED at boot). Plaintext CNIC is never returned (absent from `MemberView`) or logged (§17). Reversible (vs. password hashing) because OMJ-sync matching needs it later. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `households.head_member_id` is 1:1 | Modelled head as a one-to-one (unique) relation — a member heads at most one household — so Prisma is satisfied and the head FK is unambiguous. Member delete nulls the head (SET NULL), never cascades the household. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `module_flags` is tenant DATA (has RLS) | Unlike the step-4 authz backbone (no RLS), `module_flags` carries `tenant_id` + the §-template RLS — a tenant's commercial plan must not be readable/writable by another. First tenant-DATA table to reuse the step-2 RLS template. Tenant reads its own flags via `runWithTenant` (gate + SPA menu); Vendor writes cross-tenant via `runAsPlatform`. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Module default = open | `ModuleEnablementService`: `core` always on; an explicit flag row wins; a MISSING row is treated as ENABLED (default-open) — keeps the step-4 seam behaviour and means provisioning explicitly writes rows for the Vendor to toggle. Disabling is the explicit Vendor act that gates a module off. | confirm (vs default-closed) |
| 2026-06-05 | `core` never toggleable | The `core` module (auth/roles/settings) is never stored in `module_flags` and `setModule` refuses to disable it, so a tenant can never lock itself out of administration. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `tenant.manage` permission | Added a new CORE-module permission `tenant.manage` (PLATFORM scope) for Vendor provisioning + module toggles; excluded from every tenant role (incl. Super Admin) via `NON_TENANT_KEYS`. Granted to Vendor Owner (PLATFORM). | confirm new key |
| 2026-06-05 | Provisioning is atomic + links existing users | `provisionTenant` runs in one `runAsPlatform` tx (tenant→flags→roles→Super Admin→assignment); a person can be Super Admin of multiple Khundis, so an existing OMJ-card holder is LINKED (not duplicated). Default tenant role catalog extracted to `src/provisioning/default-roles.ts` (one source for seed + provisioning). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Fixed latent step-4 seed bug | `seed.ts` referenced lowercase `RoleAltitude.platform/omj/tenant` (undefined under the `@kc/shared` enum); only survived because the seed runs via `ts-node --transpile-only` and no live DB ran it. Corrected to uppercase members. `prisma/*.ts` is outside the `src/**` typecheck scope — consider widening it later. | no (flagging) |
| — | Subdomain base | `{tenant}.khundiconnect.com` — **CONFIRMED/LOCKED** | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Login credential | **[DECIDE AT BUILD] → built BOTH:** OTP-to-phone as the default/primary (low-literacy, §13.2) AND a password fallback for users who set one. OTP is the recommended path. | yes (confirm OTP-primary is acceptable) |
| 2026-06-05 | Users are global (no RLS) | `users`/`sessions` carry **no `tenant_id` and no RLS** — they are platform-global identity; a single human holds stacked roles across tenants/altitudes (§5.5). Tenant/scope binding lives in `user_roles` (step 4). All access via the audited `runAsPlatform` path. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Authz tables are global (no RLS) | `permissions`/`roles`/`role_permissions`/`user_roles` carry **no RLS** — the engine must read a user's STACKED roles across every tenant + platform/omj altitudes to authorize one request (an ALL_TENANTS/PLATFORM grant has null `tenant_context`; RLS-scoping would hide it and break cross-altitude authz). Read on the audited `runAsPlatform` path like `users`. **Tenant isolation is preserved by SCOPE resolution, not RLS on these tables**; every tenant-DATA table still uses the §-template RLS, and `tenants` RLS stays green (regression). `roles.tenant_id` is an ownership FK, not an isolation boundary. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Module-enablement seam (step 4 vs 5) | Build-step 4 ships the dual-gate **guards**; the persistent `module_flags` table + Vendor toggle UI are build-step 5 (per §27). `ModuleEnablementService.isEnabled()` is default-open until step 5 backs it with `module_flags` (no tenant has a reduced plan yet); the GATE's blocking behaviour is proven now by tests. `core` (auth/roles/settings) is always-on/never-toggleable. Step 5 swaps the service body with NO guard/route change. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Scope reach model | Route scopes form a reach order OWN_TENANT<TENANT_SET<ALL_TENANTS<PLATFORM; a granted scope satisfies a required one if it provides ≥ reach for the target tenant (`scopeSatisfies`). PLATFORM routes need PLATFORM; ALL_TENANTS need ALL_TENANTS/PLATFORM; single-tenant routes accept OWN_TENANT-anchored / TENANT_SET-containing / ALL_TENANTS / PLATFORM. Deny-by-default. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Role time-limit + IP restriction | Implemented from the schema: expired (`time_limited_until`) roles are skipped; a non-empty `ip_restrictions` array requires the requester IP to match (exact-match allow-list; **CIDR matching deferred** as a future enhancement). | confirm (CIDR scope) |
| 2026-06-05 | Session storage | Refresh **sessions persisted in Postgres** (`sessions` table) for durable rotation/revocation/reuse-detection; Redis used for ephemeral OTP + rate-limit. (§4 lists Redis for sessions; chose DB for refresh durability + testability.) | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Token transport | Access token (15m) returned in JSON body, held in memory by the SPA; refresh token (30d) only in an **httpOnly SameSite=Lax cookie** (Secure in prod). Two **distinct** JWT secrets required so a leaked access secret can't mint refresh tokens. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Password hashing | **Node `crypto` scrypt** (memory-hard, no native build dep) rather than bcrypt/argon2 — keeps gates runnable anywhere. Params encoded in the hash for future cost bumps. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Dev seed login users | 6 global identities seeded across altitudes (owner/OMJ/3 tenant admins/1 OTP-only member) with known OMJ card numbers; password users share a **dev-only fixture password** (env-overridable, dev/staging guard, NOT in this public file). Role assignment arrives in step 4. | no |
| — | Pricing (PKR) | [DECIDE AT BUILD] — placeholder tiers | yes |
| 2026-06-04 | Package manager | **npm workspaces** (not pnpm) so `deploy.sh` runs `npm ci` exactly per §28.6. `pnpm-workspace.yaml.disabled` documents this. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Foundation Prisma schema | **Model-free** (datasource+generator only). Tenant tables + RLS are deliberately deferred to build-step 2 so foundation defines no tenant data. `prisma generate` is a no-op until step 2. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Docker scope (step 1) | `docker-compose.yml` provisions dev **Postgres+Redis** (and CI service containers). App-process Dockerfiles deferred — VPS deploy path is **PM2**, not containers (§28.2); untested app images would add risk without value. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Node version (build env) | Target is **v22** (`.nvmrc`, engines `>=22`). This build/test ran on the sandbox's Node v24; `deploy.sh` warns (does not block) on version drift per §28.6. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | RLS enforcement model | **GUC-based RLS** with `ENABLE` + `FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY`, keyed on transaction-local `app.current_tenant_id`; an explicit `app.bypass_rls='on'` GUC is the single audited cross-tenant path (§5.1). Single `DATABASE_URL` role for operator simplicity — **requires the app DB role to be non-superuser / no `BYPASSRLS`** (documented in `docs/MULTITENANCY.md` + `VPS_SETUP.md`), since superusers ignore RLS even with FORCE. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | RLS test infrastructure | Isolation gate uses **PGlite** (Postgres compiled to WASM, in-process) so the test applies the *real* `migration.sql` and exercises genuine RLS with no Docker/superuser. Jest needs `--experimental-vm-modules` (PGlite loads WASM via dynamic import) — wired into the api `test` script. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Step-2 RLS demonstration table | RLS is proven on the **`tenants` registry itself** (a tenant session sees only its own row; cross-tenant read/write denied). The reusable per-table policy template (`tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()`) is documented for every future tenant-scoped table; those tables + policies arrive with their own build-steps (members in step 6, etc.). | no |
| 2026-06-04 | turbo.json typecheck order | `typecheck` now `dependsOn ["^build","build"]` so Next.js's generated `.next/types` exist/are fresh before `tsc` (prevents a build/typecheck race). Build-tooling only; no runtime/live-path change. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Reserved subdomain labels | `www`, `staging`, `app`, `api`, `admin` resolve as platform entries (not tenants), so they can never be provisioned as a Khundi subdomain. | confirm list |

## Environment / Deploy State
- Staging: not provisioned (operator runbook ready — `docs/VPS_SETUP.md`)
- Live environment: not provisioned (owner-Telegram-gated promotion only)
- Code repo (private): `staging` at build-step 2 (multi-tenancy landed); steps 3–12 APPROVED on their feature branches; build-step 13 on `feat/13-reports` (branched off `feat/12-ai-insights`, NO migration — pure read-only); build-step 14 on `feat/14-pwa` (branched off `feat/13-reports`). **Build-step 14 adds ONE migration** → now TWELVE migrations: `…_multitenancy_rls`, `…_auth_identity`, `…_permission_engine`, `…_module_flags`, `…_members`, `…_omj_sync`, `…_census`, `…_lawazim`, `…_accounting`, `…_notifications`, `…_ai_insights`, **`20260615000000_member_portal`** (`profile_update_requests` + `suggestions`, both RLS). Env: `OMJ_API_BASE_URL` (placeholder) is the platform OMJ endpoint; optional `OMJ_SYNC_CRON=off` disables the daily cron; **optional `MESSAGING_LIVE` (default off → SIMULATE) gates real SMS/WhatsApp; optional `AI_LIVE` (default off → SIMULATE) gates whether a real LLM is called.** Per-tenant OMJ + messaging provider keys + per-owner AI keys are entered via the UI + encrypted (never env). `ENCRYPTION_KEY` (from step 6) backs the OMJ-key + messaging-credential + AI-key + CNIC cipher. **Build-step 14 (member portal) adds NO new env** (reads existing data; no new secret) and ships the installable PWA (`manifest.webmanifest` + `sw.js`, member start_url `/me`).
- Public progress repo: not created
- CI/CD: `ci.yml` (lint/typecheck/test/build + Postgres/Redis services) + `deploy-staging.yml` authored; `deploy.sh` + `ecosystem.config.js` ready
- Cloudflare DNS: not configured

### Permanent build-correctness rules (deploy.sh / build config) — `feat/25-build-reliability`
Two deploy-blocking bugs were found on staging and fixed permanently (alongside the existing **prisma-generate-before-build** and **npm-ci-include-dev** rules). Both are now enforced by `deploy.sh` and asserted before PM2 restarts, and documented in ARCHITECTURE.md §28.5/§28.6 + docs/AUTH.md:

1. **API incremental-no-op trap.** `nest build` with `deleteOutDir:true` + `"incremental": true` (in `apps/api/tsconfig.json`) + a leftover `*.tsbuildinfo` = an exit-0 build that wipes `dist/` then emits ZERO files, crashing the API with `Cannot find module './config/env.validation'`. **Fix:** removed `"incremental": true`; `deploy.sh` §5a now purges `*.tsbuildinfo`, `apps/api/dist`, and the turbo cache (`.turbo`, `node_modules/.cache/turbo`) before building; `turbo.json` build `outputs` include `dist/**` (no more "no output files found" warning). `deploy.sh` §5c asserts `apps/api/dist/main.js` AND `apps/api/dist/config/env.validation.js` exist, exiting non-zero otherwise so a broken build never restarts PM2.

2. **`NEXT_PUBLIC_*` not baked at build.** `next build` runs with `apps/web` as cwd and reads `.env` from the app dir (not the monorepo-root `.env`); turbo's strict env mode also strips undeclared vars. So a plain `turbo run build` did NOT inline `NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATFORM_BASE_DOMAIN`, silently killing the cross-subdomain login redirect (build-step 24) after deploy. **Fix:** `deploy.sh` §5b writes an explicit ALLOWLIST (`NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATFORM_BASE_DOMAIN`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_OTP_LOGIN_ENABLED`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_MESSAGING_PROVIDER`) from the sourced `.env` into `apps/web/.env.local` before building; the same vars are declared in `turbo.json` build `env` for cache correctness. **Security:** the allowlist is the boundary — server secrets (`DATABASE_URL`, `JWT_*`, `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, `R2_*`) are NEVER copied. §5c greps `.next/static` to confirm the public value baked in (fail loudly if absent) AND scans for leaked secret values (abort if any found). Verified: clean API build emits `main.js`+`config/env.validation.js`; a plain web build bakes the domain into `.next/static`; no server secret appears in `.next/static`.

---

## Build-step 81 — Polling & Elections module — `feat/81-polling-elections-v31` (built 2026-06-28)

**WORK TYPE: FEATURE** (a full new module — the largest single build-step in v3.1). Spec `specs/81-polling-elections-v31.md`; CODEREF `specs/76-82-CODEREF.md`. Depends on 78 (audiences → eligibility), 61 (member/voting-eligibility), 76 (notify).

### What shipped
A complete **Polling & Elections** module at Khundi and OMJ altitude: nominations, a secret ballot, configurable winning rules, certification, per-poll configurable eligibility, and decision polls — on one set of machinery.

### Data model (NEW — migration `20260723000000_polls_elections`, ADDITIVE)
Five NEW **tenant-DATA** tables, each RLS **ENABLE + FORCE** with the standard isolation policy `USING/WITH CHECK ( app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id() )` and a **NULLABLE `tenant_id`** (a null row = an OMJ-level poll, reachable only on the audited platform path — build-step 49 pattern):
- `polls` — `id, tenant_id?, title, description?, kind('election'|'decision'), status('draft'|'nominating'|'open'|'closed'|'certified'), voter_eligibility Json, candidate_eligibility Json?, winning_rule Json, opens_at?, closes_at?, secret(default true), certified_result Json?, created_by?, certified_by?, certified_at?, timestamps`. FK `tenant_id → tenants` ON DELETE CASCADE; Tenant back-relation `polls Poll[]`.
- `poll_options` — decision options OR confirmed candidates (`member_id?` set for a candidate); FK `poll_id → polls` cascade.
- `poll_nominations` — `nominee_member_id, nominated_by?, status('proposed'|'confirmed'|'declined')`, `@@unique(poll_id, nominee_member_id)`; FK cascade.
- **SECRET-BALLOT pair** (the critical invariant):
  - `poll_vote_turnout` — WHO voted: `voter_member_id, voted_at`, `@@unique(poll_id, voter_member_id)` = one vote per eligible voter (no double vote). NO choice column.
  - `poll_ballots` — the CHOICE: `option_id, cast_at`. **NO voter column, NO FK to turnout** (FKs only to `polls` + `poll_options`); random UUID id; `cast_at` **coarsened to UTC midnight** in the service so neither row order nor timestamp can correlate a ballot to a turnout row. Voter→choice is therefore **structurally unlinkable**.

### Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`)
- `MODULES.POLLS = 'polls'` (auto-provisionable + default-open via the existing module-flag seam — no seed change) and permissions `polls.view` / `polls.manage` / `polls.vote` (module `POLLS`).
- Types: `PollKind`, `PollStatus`, `PollNominationStatus`, `WinningRule`/`WinningRuleType`, `PollEligibility` (`all_active|voting_eligible|audience|filters`), `PollView`/`PollOptionView`/`PollNominationView`/`PollTallyOption`/`PollTallyResult`.
- Pure `tallyPoll(options, ballots, rule)` — fptp (top count, tie → multiple winners, non-decisive), majority (strict > threshold, default 0.5), top_n (top N, boundary-tie non-decisive), quota (every option ≥ threshold share); ignores ballots for unknown options; deterministic (frozen-tally guarantee). Pure `pollEligibilityToFilters()` maps a rule to a build-step-56 `FilterState` (`audience` → null, resolved from the saved audience's own definition).

### API (`apps/api/src/polls/`)
- `PollsService` — runs the lifecycle with **every transition an explicit method** (§3.5: `openNominations`, `openVoting` (requires ≥1 option, sets `opens_at`), `close`, `certify` (computes the tally, freezes `certified_result`, records `certified_by/at`, refuses re-certify)). `castVote` enforces open-status + [opens_at, closes_at] window + live voter-eligibility + option-belongs-to-poll + no-double-vote, then writes turnout + ballot in ONE tx with the day-coarsened `cast_at` (P2002 race → clean 409). `resolveVoterMemberId` maps the signed-in user → their OWN member by `omjCardNumber` (never a request id). Eligibility resolves through the ONE shared `AudiencesService.resolveMemberIdsInTx` (`audience` rule loads the saved-audience definition in-context). `notifyBestEffort` sends open/close/result via build-step 76 to the eligible audience — wrapped in try/catch so a missing provider never blocks a transition (OMJ polls skip). Audited via `Logger('Audit')` (the events/audiences convention); the vote audit records only THAT a ballot was cast, never the choice.
- `PollsController` (Khundi, `@RequireModule(POLLS)` + dual-gate, OWN_TENANT) — list/get/nominations/turnout/results + create/update/delete (`polls.manage`) + lifecycle + nominate (`polls.vote`, self-nominate)/confirm/decline (`polls.manage`) + **vote** (`polls.vote`, voter resolved server-side).
- `PollsPlatformController` (OMJ, `polls.manage`@ALL_TENANTS, audited platform path, `tenant_id=null`) — management + lifecycle + certify + results (decision-record surface; member-driven nomination/voting is the Khundi path).
- `PollsModule` imports Auth/Permissions/Audiences/Notifications (no cycle); wired into `app.module.ts` after NotificationsModule.

### Web (`apps/web/app/polls/`)
- `/polls` — list (status badge, human kind/status labels) + create modal (title, kind, eligibility = voting-eligible / all-active / a saved audience, winning rule + conditional n/threshold, decision options).
- `/polls/[id]` — lifecycle controls (manager), nominations (self-nominate + confirm/decline), the **secret ballot** (radio options, "your vote is secret" notice, big touch targets), live **turnout** while open (never results), candidates/options, and **results** after close (winners flagged, non-decisive tie note) with a **Certified** badge.
- `shared.tsx` `statusBadgeVariant`; nav entry "Polls & Elections" (Vote icon, `polls.view`/`polls.vote`) in the Community section. 77 new `t()` keys in BOTH locales (`messages-extra.ts` EN+UR + delta `i18n-deltas/polls-elections.json`).

### Tests (+30 → **1612/1612**, 196 suites)
- `polls.tally.spec.ts` (12) — every winning rule, ties/no-majority non-decisive, decision yes/no, zero ballots, unknown-option ignored, purity.
- `polls.service.spec.ts` (10) — decision end-to-end (no-result-before-close, turnout, certify), double-vote 409, ineligible voter, window/status guards, immutable re-certify, **secret-ballot data shape** (turnout has voter not choice; ballot has choice not voter; day-coarsened cast_at), election nominate→confirm→vote→certify, ineligible candidate blocked, voter-by-card resolution, OMJ-altitude decision lifecycle. (In-memory fake DB with save/restore tenant context so the fire-and-forget notify can't corrupt scope.)
- `polls.isolation.spec.ts` (10) — REAL migration chain through step 81 on PGlite as a non-superuser: 5 tables RLS ENABLE+FORCE (saved_audiences unchanged); **ballot-secrecy schema introspection** (poll_ballots has no `voter_member_id` column + no FK to poll_vote_turnout; FKs only to polls+poll_options; turnout has no `option_id`); turnout unique = no double vote; Khundi sees only its own polls/ballots/turnout; cannot read/update/delete another Khundi's or the OMJ-level poll; WITH CHECK refuses cross-tenant + null-tenant inserts; deny-by-default; platform path is the only cross-Khundi/OMJ reader; tenant delete cascades polls+options+turnout+ballots, OMJ poll survives.

### Gates
typecheck (shared+api+web) ✅ · lint (web) ✅ · build (api+web, `/polls` + `/polls/[id]` emitted) ✅ · prisma validate ✅ · API tests 1612/1612 ✅ · i18n parity + web-coverage ✅. Zero physical-direction Tailwind; RTL via document `dir`; no raw enum on screen. (The "worker force-exited" jest notice is the known vm-modules teardown warning, not a failure.)

### Decisions / notes
- **Secrecy model documented in the migration + schema**: unlinkability is structural (no column/FK/order/precise-timestamp), the strongest property the spec asks for; randomized batching was considered but day-coarsening + random UUID + no-link is simpler, robust (never loses a vote), and testable.
- **Voter identity** is always the signed-in user's own member record — no `voterMemberId` is ever accepted from the client, so no one can vote as another.
- **Eligibility** is per-poll (audience/rule) through the single shared filter language; `voting_eligible` is ONE option, not the hardcoded rule (a Khundi may enfranchise differently).
- **OMJ poll casting** is intentionally not exposed at the platform altitude (a vote is a Khundi member's act resolved inside that Khundi's tenant context); OMJ supports management + lifecycle + certify + results.

---

## Build-step 86 — Permissions & roles correctness — `feat/86-permissions-fix-v32` (built 2026-06-28)

**WORK TYPE: FIX** (v3.2 Wave 1 / item 1 — PRIORITY; the testing BLOCKER). Spec `specs/86-permissions-fix-v32.md`; CODEREF `specs/86-91-CODEREF.md`. **PERMISSION-SENSITIVE — flagged.** First step of the v3.2 concern-resolution program (build-steps 86–93, `specs/README-v3.2.md`).

### The problem (operator concern, verified in code)
`SUPER_ADMIN_KEYS` (`apps/api/src/provisioning/default-roles.ts`) is correctly DYNAMIC — `ALL_PERMISSION_KEYS.filter(k => !NON_TENANT_KEYS.has(k))`, i.e. "every tenant-applicable permission" — but it is materialised into `role_permissions` **only at provisioning/seed time**. When later build-steps added permissions (`reports.view` build-step 84-era, `polls.view/manage/vote` build-step 81), **already-provisioned tenants' protected Khundi Super Admin roles never gained them** (no reconcile). Result: an existing Khundi Super Admin could not access Reporting/Polls — blocking the operator from testing those modules. New tenants were fine; existing ones stale.

### Scope decision — shipped §2.1, split §2.2 (spec-sanctioned)
The spec explicitly authorises splitting: "ship 2.1 (the reconcile — the actual blocker) in 86, and 2.2 (fork-on-edit) as 86b/87. 2.1 is the must-have." I shipped **§2.1 (the reconcile)** fully and split **§2.2 (fork-on-edit of non-protected seeded roles)** to a follow-up **86b**. Rationale: in this codebase each tenant already owns physical copies of the seeded roles (President/Accountant/… are TENANT rows with `tenantId`), and `isBuiltInRole` is NAME-based (`DEFAULT_TENANT_ROLE_NAMES.has(role.name)`). A faithful "fork, don't block" therefore needs an identity/schema decision (`derivedFromRoleId` + override row vs clone-on-first-edit with a non-protected flag) and risks regressing the working name-based role editor + its tests — too large to fold into the blocker fix safely.

### What shipped (§2.1 — the reconcile, two hooks)
1. **Idempotent one-shot data migration** `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260724000000_superadmin_perm_reconcile/migration.sql` (PURE SQL — the authz backbone `roles`/`role_permissions`/`permissions` is GLOBAL by design, **no RLS**, docs/PERMISSIONS.md — so no `runWithTenant`/GUC needed). A single `INSERT … SELECT` cross-joins every **protected TENANT-altitude** role (`altitude='tenant' AND is_protected=true` — the Khundi Super Admin) with every permission whose `key` is NOT in the platform/OMJ exclusion list (the 8 `NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS` inlined verbatim), guarded by `NOT EXISTS` on the existing grant. Therefore: **idempotent** (a second run inserts nothing), **isolated** (each role reconciled against its OWN grants — one tenant's Super Admin is never widened from another's), and the Super Admin **never gains an OMJ/Vendor power**. Uses `gen_random_uuid()` (already used by the build-step-74 graveyard backfill). **NO schema change** — `schema.prisma` untouched; this is a data backfill only. Fixes the operator's existing test Khundi NOW.
2. **Boot-time safety net** `PermissionService.reconcileSuperAdminGrants()` (`apps/api/src/permissions/permission.service.ts`), called from a new `onApplicationBootstrap()` (`implements OnApplicationBootstrap`). It loads the assignable permission rows for `SUPER_ADMIN_KEYS` (imported from `default-roles.ts` — DYNAMIC, so any FUTURE permission added to the catalog is included with **no new backfill**) and, for each protected TENANT role, `createMany({…, skipDuplicates:true})` the missing grants. Read/written on the audited platform path (`runAsPlatform`). **Never crashes boot** — a transient DB outage (PrismaService boots regardless) is caught, logged (`logger.warn`), and skipped; the next bootstrap or the migration reconciles. Audit-logs `permissions.reconcile roles=N grantsAdded=M actor=system` only when something changed. This is the "most robust available hook" the spec asks for (§2.1 b).

### Preserved (already-correct guards — verified, not regressed)
- Protected Super Admin/Owner role stays **non-editable** (`updateRole`/`deleteRole` still throw `Built-in roles cannot be edited/deleted` for `isBuiltInRole`).
- `sanitisePermissionKeys` still filters every tenant role edit through `ASSIGNABLE_KEYS` (`TENANT_ASSIGNABLE_PERMISSIONS`) — a Khundi can never grant platform/OMJ powers.
- Role queries stay `altitude: TENANT` + `tenantId`-scoped (a Khundi only sees/edits its own roles).
- The ≥1-Super-Admin-holder lock-out guard (`removeMemberFromRole`).
- `NON_TENANT_KEYS` exclusion (Super Admin never gets OMJ/Vendor powers) — enforced by both the migration's `NOT IN` list and the reconcile's `SUPER_ADMIN_KEYS` derivation.

### Files
- NEW `apps/api/prisma/migrations/20260724000000_superadmin_perm_reconcile/migration.sql` (data backfill).
- EDIT `apps/api/src/permissions/permission.service.ts` (+`OnApplicationBootstrap` import, +`SUPER_ADMIN_KEYS` import, +`logger`, +`onApplicationBootstrap()`, +`reconcileSuperAdminGrants()`).
- NEW `apps/api/src/permissions/superadmin-reconcile.migration.spec.ts` (real SQL on PGlite — the required migration regression).
- NEW `apps/api/src/permissions/superadmin-reconcile.service.spec.ts` (the boot-time reconcile unit test).

### Acceptance (spec §3) — coverage
1. ✅ A stale protected Super Admin gains `reports.view`, `polls.*`, and every other current tenant permission — proven by the migration spec (seeds the catalog-minus-later-keys, asserts the full assignable set after backfill) AND the service spec (stale snapshot → full set; the dynamic `SUPER_ADMIN_KEYS` hook is what picks up a newly-added key). **Operator can now test Reporting & Polls as Super Admin.**
2. ✅ Idempotent (second run inserts nothing — both specs) and tenant-isolated (each Super Admin reconciled against its own grants — migration spec asserts T1 & T2 independently; per-role `NOT EXISTS`).
3. ⏭ Fork-on-edit (§2.2) — **split to 86b** (spec-sanctioned).
4. ✅ Protected Super Admin/Owner remains non-editable/non-forkable — unchanged hard block (existing `role-editor.service.spec.ts` still green).
5. ✅ A Khundi role still cannot receive any platform/OMJ permission — `sanitisePermissionKeys` regression covered by existing role-editor spec; reconcile excludes them by construction.
6. ✅ Gates green (below); migration regression for the backfill shipped.

### Gates
- **typecheck** (`@kc/api`): clean.
- **lint** (eslint, api): clean.
- **build** (`nest build`): clean.
- **api test suite**: **201 suites / 1649 tests pass** (+2 suites, +11 tests vs 199/1638). Includes the new migration-regression spec (backfill + idempotency + non-tenant exclusion + per-tenant isolation + roles/role_permissions stay no-RLS while `tenants` keeps RLS) and the new service spec (stale→full, idempotent, only-protected-TENANT touched, never grants platform keys, boot never throws).
- **isolation**: the migration spec's RLS-regression assertion + existing isolation suites green. No tenant table's RLS policy touched (data-only migration).
- web/shared/i18n gates: **N/A** — API-only change, no web/shared edits, **no new `t()` keys**.

### Follow-up owed
- **86b — fork-on-edit (§2.2):** when a Khundi edits a NON-protected seeded role (President/Accountant/…), create a Khundi-specific editable copy (decide `derivedFromRoleId`+override vs clone-on-first-edit with a non-protected marker; keep names unambiguous), still passing `sanitisePermissionKeys` and `altitude: TENANT`; the protected Super Admin/Owner stays locked.

---

## Build-step 87 — Dynamic-filter rollout to every list (v3.2 Wave 1 / item 2)

**Built:** 2026-06-28 · **WORK TYPE: FIX** (completion/roll-out) · **branch:** `feat/87-filter-rollout-v32` · **NO schema / RLS / auth / permission change** (web client + per-list filter configs; isolation ➖ — client/server filter over already-tenant-scoped, fully-loaded data).

### Problem (concern [19])
The build-step-56 dynamic-filter ENGINE (`<FilterBar>`, `applyFilters`, `shouldFilterServerSide`, `filtersToQuery`, the `filterConfig`/`getFilterValue` props on `<DataList>`) shipped and worked — but had been adopted on ONLY the members roster (1 of ~19 lists). Every other list had just the free-text search box.

### Approach — configuration, not new engine
Reused build-step 56 entirely. The ONLY new code in `@kc/shared` is one tiny PURE helper:
- `labelDomainOptions(domain)` — enumerates a `LABEL_CATALOG` domain in catalog order → `FilterOption[]` (`{value, label:en}`). The `<FilterBar>` renders each option's label through `formatLabel(value,{domain,locale})` at render time, so the helper keeps every select filter in lock-step with the same `labelDomain` the column registry already declares — no raw enum ever reaches the screen, and a list can't drift from the catalog.

Key realisation: each list's filterable fields ARE exactly the `labelDomain` columns already declared in `LIST_COLUMN_REGISTRY`, so the configs mirror the registry. Field labels reuse the EXISTING `col.*` i18n keys (status/type/fund/source/category/gender/kind/channel/income/education/employment/marital/ceremony/rsvp/method/matched_by/submitted_by/action/actor/date/when/graveyard_type/welfare_flag/posted/printed/attended/this_year/dues_running) ⇒ ZERO new web keys for the DataList pages.

All target lists already fetch the WHOLE list (no server pagination except members), so every rollout config sets `clientRowCap: 100_000` ⇒ always client-side, instant, fuzzy — the honest match to a fully-loaded list. The members list keeps its proven server-side path (`onServerFilter` + refetch) unchanged.

### Lists covered
**DataList lists — `filterConfig` + `getFilterValue` (16):**
- `census` (status/income/education/employment/marital selects + welfare boolean), `welfare` (caseType[governed taxonomy]/fundSource/status), `lawazim` (yearStatus + defaulter boolean), `prize_applications` (category[taxonomy]/status/submittedBy), `omj_sync` (type/status/gender/matchedBy), `notifications` (status/kind/channel), `deaths`/graveyard (graveyardSource/posted boolean/date-of-death range), `accounting_journal` (voucherType/source/date range), `accounting_ledger` (account type), `donations` (fund[dynamic]/method/date range), `documents` (category/uploaded-date range), `cards` (type/printed boolean), `events` (type/status/starts-date range), `event_registrations` (rsvp/attended boolean — config lives inside the `EventPanel` sub-component), `billing` (status/paid-date range), `audit` (action-namespace[dynamic, audit_domain]/actor/date range — and `platform_audit` gets it free via the shared `AuditViewer`).

**Non-`DataList` lists — standalone `<FilterBar>` + `applyFilters` (2):**
- `polls` (status/kind selects over the card list; options derived from the polls present, labelled via the existing per-status/per-kind dynamic `t()` keys), `taxonomy` (origin[taxonomy_option_origin] + status[taxonomy_status] over the per-domain value list).

**members** — already done at build-step 56; kept verbatim (its config + server-side path are the reference, untouched).

### Notable refactors
- **AuditViewer** migrated from its bespoke toolbar (manual `<Select>`s + `<DateField>`s + a hand-rolled `filtered` useMemo + 4 pieces of state) to the standard collapsible accordion + active chips via `filterConfig`/`getFilterValue`. Dropped the now-unused `DateField`/`Select`/`useState` imports.
- **documents** dropped its redundant category-toolbar `<Select>` in favour of the accordion's category filter; removed the dead `query`/`catFilter` state and the now-unused `filterDocuments` import (the page already loads all docs; `<DataList>`'s own search + the accordion cover it).
- Hook-placement: for census/welfare/prize/omj-sync/notifications/billing the config `useMemo`/`useCallback` had to sit BEFORE the page's early `return`s (rules-of-hooks); placed accordingly.

### i18n
Zero new keys for the 16 DataList pages (reused `col.*`). TWO new keys for taxonomy — `filters.origin`/`filters.status` — authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` (`MESSAGES_EXTRA_EN`/`_UR`) AND `i18n-deltas/filters.json`, then shared rebuilt. (polls' "no match" empty-state reuses `common.nothingToShow`.)

### Out of scope (documented decisions)
- `events_attendance` — owned by build-step 91 (the blank-table fix registers its listKey); left untouched.
- `audiences` — the page IS the audience BUILDER, already centred on `<FilterBar>` over the member domain; its saved-segment list (named segments) has no enum dimension to filter, so a redundant accordion was deliberately not added.
- platform billing catalogs (`billing_plans`/`billing_tenants`) — Vendor console, outside the spec's tenant-list scope.

### Files
`packages/shared/src/index.ts` (new `labelDomainOptions`), `packages/shared/src/messages-extra.ts` + `packages/shared/i18n-deltas/filters.json` (2 new filters keys ×2 locales), `apps/api/src/ui/filter-engine.spec.ts` (3 new `labelDomainOptions` cases), and the web pages: `census`, `welfare`, `lawazim`, `prize`, `omj-sync`, `notifications`, `bereavement`, `accounting/page` (journal+ledger), `accounting/funds-panel` (donations), `documents`, `events`, `billing`, `polls`, `taxonomy`, `ui/audit-viewer`.

### Do-NOT-break — honoured
build-step-56 engine + `filterConfig`/`getFilterValue`/`applyFilters`/`shouldFilterServerSide` unchanged; members list config kept; tenant scoping intact (filters are client-side over already-tenant-scoped data — they never widen); per-user column prefs (build-step 55) coexist (filters are a separate concern in `<DataList>`).

### Gates
typecheck ✅ · lint ✅ (rules-of-hooks clean after the hook moves) · web build ✅ (44 routes) · i18n parity (`i18n.spec.ts`) + web-coverage (`audit/i18n-web-coverage.spec.ts`) ✅ · filter-engine spec (incl. new `labelDomainOptions` cases) ✅.
